cclxij deposicyon kyng henry sixte ad kyg edward fourth toke poscessyon reaulme bataille palmesonday crowned cap cclxiij phow lade englode fyrst named albion ad encheson named ther noble lade surre noble myghti kig grete renome men called dioclisian well worthely hym gouerned ruled thurgh noble chiualrie conquered landes hym almost kynges world entedant hit befell thus thys dyoclesian spoused gentill damysell woder fair emes doughter ad men called hyr labana loued hy reso wolde gate vpon xxxiij doughtres whiche eldest men called albine thees damiselles wha come vnto age bicomen fayre woder wherfor dyoclisian anon let make somaunce commauded lres alle kinges helden hy shold come certay day hyr lres coteyned make ryall feste whyche day thider come brought wyt hem amyrallis prince duke ad noble chyualrye fest rially arayed ther lyued en ioye myrthe ynough woder wit befell thus thys dyoclisian thought marie doughtres amog kinges tho solepnite punctel spaken ad ded albyne eldest doughter hir sustres richely maried vnto xxxiij kinges lordes grete honour power solepnite whan solempnyte done every king toke wyf ad lad owne contre ther made quenes befell thus afterward dame albyne bycome stoute sterne tolde lytel pry lorde hym scorne ad despit wolde done wyll wolde haue hyr owne wil diuerse mater hyr sustres euerichone bere euel ayest hyr lordes wo der wyt asmoch thought hyr husbondes nought hye age comen hyr fadre kinges hyr lordes wolde haue castised fayr speche behestes also yeftes warned hem fayr maner vpon loue fredship sholde ame de lyther condycyons nought dydden hyr owne alle thyng hem lyked power wherfor xxxiij kynges vpo tyme often tymes beten hyr wife wed wolde haue ameded tacches hir wikked thewes suche condicions fair spech warnyng dydden alle wers betynges eftsones mochel wers wherfore kyng yt wedded albyne wrote tacches condicions hys wyfe albyne sent letter dioclisian hyr fadre wha kinges herde albynes lord sent letter dyoclisia anone sent lettres ensealed hyr seales condycyons tacches hyr wyfes also whan noble kyg dyoclisian saw herd many complayntes hys doughtres sore ashamed became wo der angrye wroth toward hys doughtres ad thought night day might ame de mysded anone sent lres vnto ye xxxiij kyges shold come hy bringe hem hir wife euerichone certay day wolde ther castyse wikkednesse yf might maner wyse kiges camen alle day tyme tho sette bytwene hy kyng dioclisian vnderfeng hem moche honour made solempne feest alle vnder lordship thridde day solempnite noble kyng dioclisian sent hys xxxiij doughtres shold come ad speke wyth chabre whan come hir fadre spake vnto hem hyr wikkednesse ad hir crueltie dispytously hem reproued vndernam punctel hem said yf wold chastysed shulde loue lese euermore ladyes herde thys became moch abasshed gretly ashamyd fadre sayd wold make alle amedes departed owt hyr fadres chambre dame albyne eldest suster lad hem alle hyr chabre made voyde alle theryne lyue amoge hyr sustres tho sayd albine fayr sustres well knowe kyg fadre v hath reproued shamed despysed encheso make v obediet vnto oure housbodes certes shal j neuer while yt j lyue syth come hyer kynges blode tha husbode wha th sayd hir sustre said ye tho sayd albyne j wote wel fayre sustres yt husbodes haue playned vnto fadre vpo v wherfor hath v thus foule reproued despysed wherfore sustres counseyll thys night whan husbondes ben bedde wyth owne assent cutte hir throtes may bene pee hem ad better mowe doo thyge vnder fadres power elles anone ladyes consented graunted counseyll whan nyght come lordes ladyes went bedde ad anone hir lordes slepe cutte hir husbodes throtes slowen hem whenne dioclisian kyg fadre herd thyg become hugely wroth ayest doughtres anon wold hem haue brent alle baron ad lordes surre counceylled suche sternesse hys ownes doughtres sholde voide lad hem euermore neuer shold come ayen dyde dioclisia fadre anoue commaunded hem gone ship delyuered hem vytailles half yere whan done sustren wet ship sayled forth see bytoke alle hyr fredes appolyn hir god loge saylled see tyll last came ad arryued yle wildernesse whan dame albyne come londe hir sustres albyne went forth owt ship sayd hyr othyr sustres asmoche sayd oldest suster thys companye fyrst land haue taken ad moch name albyne wyll lo de called albyon owne name ad anon hir sustre grau ted hyr wyt good wyl tho went alle sustres owt shippe toke land albyo hyr suster called ther wente vp ad downe fonde nether man ne woman ne child wilde bestes diuerse kydes hir vytailles dispended hem faylled fedde hem wyt herbes frutes seson yere leued best myght ad token flessh dyuerses bestes bicame wonder fat ad desired mannys companye mannys kynde hem failled hete woxen wo der coragious kynde desyred mannis copanie ony othir solace mirthe whan deuel perceyued went dyuerse cotreyes nomme body eyr likynge nature shad men ad come lande albyon lay wymen shad nature vpon hem ceyued brought forth geants whych men kalled gogmagog la gherigan nepned dyuerse name ad maner came forth ad borne horryble geants albyo dwelled caues hulles hyr lo de albion hem lyked vnto tyme brute arryued ad came totnesse yle albyon ther brute conquered sconfyted geants aboue sayd phere endeth prolog albyon tho ile herkene brute goten slowe fyrst hys moder afterward hys fader conquered albyon nepned bretaygne hys owne name kalled englod name engist saxonie capitulo primo ther noble cyte grete troye noble king ad man grete power kalled eneas whan cyte troye lost ad destroyed thurgh heem grece eneas wyt hys meyne fledde thes come lumbardie tho lorde gouernour lode king called latyne othir kyng kalled turocelyne strongely werred vpon king latyne often tymes dyd hym moch harme whe kig herde eneas come vnderfeng hy wyth mochel honour hym helde moch herde hy wist well noble kinght ad worthy body ad dedes eneas helpe king latyne werre shortly telle well worthely dyd slowe turocelyne discomfyted hy peple whan thys done kyng latyne yaf londe turocelynis eneas mariage lauyne doughter moost fayre creature wist lyued gedre ioye myrthe hir lyfes tyme wedded wyfe vpo hir begate sone called silueyne thys sylueyne wha coude reson man vnwytyng fadre ayenst acqueynted damisell cosy leuine kyg latynes doughter quene eneas wyfe brought damisell childe ad whan ascamus fadre wist anone let enquere wysest maistres gretest clerkes child ye damisell shold bring forth answerd seyd shold bryng forth sone sholde quelle bothe fadre ad moder ad dyd moder deyed beryg hy ad wha child borne fadre let calle hy brute maistres sayd shold moche harme sorwe many diuerse place ad shold come grete honour worship kyng ascam deyde wha god wolde silueyne sone receyued ye land made hy wonderlich wel beloued amoge peple brute yt silueynus sone xv yere olde went vpo daye wyt fadre pley solace brute shold shete vnto hert arwe myshapped glaced brute quelled fadre brute dryuen owt land helde hy grece capitulo secundo myschance befalle peple lade made sorwe ynough sore gred ad encheson therof dryuen brute oute lande wolde suffre amoges saugh must abide went fro then grece ad ther fonde vijm men lygnage kynryd troye come grete blode storie telleth men wymen ad chyldre whiche holden throldome bondage kyg padras grece deth achylles bitraied slayne troye brute wonder fayr man stronge ad hughe hys age glad chere se blant also worthy body ad wel beloued amonge peple king padras herde speke hys goodnesse codicyons anone made hy dwelle wyth brute bicome wonder pryue moch beloued wt king longe tyme brute dwelled wyth kyng ye last troye brute spaken gydre kynred lygnage acqueyntauce ad ther pleyned hem vnto brute hyr sorwe hyr boundage many shame kyng pandras hem done brute saide vpon time ye lord owr lygnage ad strog man myghty ye capiteyn lorde wyll bycome yowr men comau dements done alle maner thy ge ad bringe ye v oute wrecchednesse bondage fight kyng thurgh grace grete god shal hy ouercome shal make kyng lande yow done homage yow shull holde euermore brut tho grete pite hyr bondage brought preuely went hy kiges court tho troye went ad put wodes motaignes hem helde sent vnto kyg pandras sholde yeue leue sauelych wete owt lade wold leger dwelle hys bodage kyng padras wax tho sore annoied swore wolde slee euerichone ad ordeyned gret power went towardes hem fyght brute men maly hem defended fiersly foughten quelled ye kyges none escaped toke kyg hy helde pryso ordeyned cou seyl bitwene might done somme sayd shold put deth somme sayd shold exiled oute lande somme sayd shold brent tho spake wyse knight called pry sayd brute ad troye yf kyng pandras wolde yelde haue hys lyfe couseyll yeue vnto brute duke souerayngne doughter gennoge wyfe mariage hyr hoderd shippes wel arayed tresour gold ad syluer corne wyne moch nedeth haue thig go owte land punctel ordeyne v lande elles wer fore ne none owr kynred comen v shall neuer haue pee lad amonges grece haue slayne many hyr knightes fredes euer werre ad cotake sholde ben amonges v brute tho alle folke cosented well co seyll thys thyng tolden kyng pandras therfor haue hys lyfe grauted moche axed anone yaf vnto brute gennoge hys doughter wyfe c shippes wyt moche nedeth alle vytailles ordeyned brute tho toke hys wyfe men forsoke lad grece wente hem vnto hadde wynde weder came thridde day ile called lorgers brute anon sente men lande aspie maner cotre fonde olde cyte vasted ad forlet therinne nether ne woman ne thyng dwellyg ad middel cyte fonde olde teple fayre lady called dyane ye goddesse camen ayen vnto brute tolde seyn fonde counceilled hy gone done sacrefice vnto dame dyane wont yeue answer thyng euer man praied hyr ad namely vnto honoured wt sacrefice brute wet jmage sayd dyane noble goddesse lady thing hast might thy power wyndes water wodes feldes alle thynges ye world alle maner bestes ther ben yow make prayer ye counceylle telle ad place shall maye haue ad fynde couenable dwellyng ad peple ad whan shal haue fonden thys couceill shall make honour yow well fayre temple noble wheryne ye shal euermore ben honowred whan done hys prayer goddesse dyane answerde hy maner brute sayd go euen forth thy wey ouer ye see ito frau ce toward west ther ye shall fyde ile kalled albyo yle bycompasset wyt see punctel man may come ther ben shippes lade wont geats nowo wyldernesse punctel forsayde land destynyed ad ordeyned peple phow vaillaut knight coryn became brute men kyng goffars discomfyted capitulo iij whan brute herde thys aswere diane goddesse anone let ancres wynde vp sayled hygh see ad whan hys men saylled xx dayes moo fonden fast beside cost see thousad men lygnage ad kynred troye hyr soueraigne ad hyr maistre kalled coryn whan brute wiste whennes tho vnderfeng hem wyth moch joye shyppes ad lad forth wyth hym thys coryn tho become brute men dyd feaulte homage longe saylled forth see tyll camen gasconye anone arryued haue lyrgers ad ther dwelled viij dayes reste hyr saylles amede ther nede thyse tydyges sone camen kyng goffar punctel lord lande mochel folke strange lande arryued hys land hauen lirgers wherfore sore angred anoyed camen arryued lande wythoute leue anone ordeyned hy grete power dryuen owte ad destroye brute wyth peple kyng goffar discomfyted alle hys folke hym self fledde fraunce seke helpe ad socour tyme regned fraunce xij kynges xj kynges assembled grete power helpe goffar fyght ayenst brute goffar dwelled hem fraunce halfe yere brute mene tyme hys companye destroyed alle lad gasconie let take alle tresour goffar hath let bringe shippes brute fonde land fayre place moche couenable made fayre ad stronge castel whan alle thing dou kyng goffar came fro fraunce xj kynges wyth hym broughte xxm men fyght ayest brut companye brute vijm ccc men neuertheles two hostes mete gedre brute folk thurgh helpe self turyn cosyn coryn wel ad manly hym deffended foughte lytel time quelled frenshme two thousad moo tho lyue fledde way bataill tury brute cosyn slayn ad brut let burye worthely wha space leyser castell made tho let calle castell tour ye name turyne buryed ad yet thys day ther noble cyte called tour whan kyng goffar wyste turyn dede came ayen hys men yaf stro ge bataill vnto brute brute men wery fyghtyng myght lenger endure magre hise brute went castell wyth alle men ad made yates fast saue hym selfe take counseyll amonges hem best brute coryn toke counceill ordeyned coryn preueli sholde go owte hyde hym wode ther bi tyl morne mornyng whan kyg brute sholde fyght wyt hys enemyes coryn shold come folke owne syde slee doo harme might mornyng dawenyng brute went owte castell faught vaylliauntly hys enemyes ad fiersly defended hem wythyn lytel tyme brute folke slew viijc kyng goffars men tho came coryn fro busshement smote grounde ad hys companye wolde stonde abyde kyng goffart folke discomfited begonne fast flee brute coryn hyr companye fersely hem pursued quelyd mo theyr fleddyng dyden bataille maner vaillaut kyng brute victorye hys ennemyes neuertheles made moch sorowe cosyn thury slayn othir also hys men lost bataille ther slayn hys men vij c xv whyche let nobely burye ye castell tour ther buryed turyn hys cosyn phow king brute arryued tottenesse ile albyon bataille bytwene coryn gogmagog capitulo quarto alle thys thing done brute wolde lenger ther dwelle fyghte ne moo lese hys peple kynghts goffarus peple myght euery day encresse moo moo brute peple lassen ad therfore toke alle hys men ad wet vnto see ad wynd ad weder wylle fyfthe daye afterward arryued hauen tottenesse camen jle albyon ther fo de thei nethir man nethir woma storye telleth ye geats dwelled hylles ad caues brute sawe lode fayre ad lyking good also ad hys folke goddesse dyane hym behyght tho kig brute wonder glad ad ryght wel content ad lete assemble vpo day alle hys folcke make solempne sacrefyce grete fest honowr reuerence dyane ye goddesse thurgh who counseyll comen good fayre lad whan hyr solempnyte made vpon day sate mete ther camen vpon hem sodenly xxx geants quelled brute men xxx brute hys men anone sturte vp foughten wyth geants quelled euerycho one geant maistre alle called gogmagog stronger hyer geats ad brute kept saued hys lyf encheson shold wrestell wyt coryn coryn greter hyer brute men fro gerdelstede vpward gogmagog cory vndertoke wrastlyn ynfere gedre wrastled longe tyme last gogmagog geant held coryn faste brack two rybbes hys syde wherfore vaylliaut knight coryn sore angry toke tho gogmagog geant bytwene hys armes kast downe vpon roche gogmagog brak peces deyed euyll deth therfore ye place called yet vnto day saulte gogmagog ad tho yaf brute alle contre coryn coryn kalled hys name cornewaille hys men kalled cornewailles ad shull men cotre ben called euermore contre dwelled coryn men made townes ad howses inhabyted land hyr wylle brute made london kalled thys lande bretaigne scotland albyne walys cambir capitulo quinto brute men wente forth sawen aboute diuerse place wher might fynde good place couenable thei might make cite folke ye last camen fayr ryuer kalled thamys brute bega make fair cyte let calle newe troye mynde remebrauce ye grete troye place hir lygnage come brute let fall downe wodes let crye sowe lades ad done mowe mede sustenauce peple punctel departed lad hem euerychon certay place dwelle vpo ad brute let calle thys lande bretaigne owne name folk let calle breton brute goten wyfe geunogen thre soens worthy deedes fyrst kalled lotry secod albanak thred caber brute bare corone ye cite newe troye xx yere time cite made ther made lawes bretos holde thys noble kyng brute wonderly well beloued among alle men peple brute sone also loued wonderly well gedre whe king brute sought alle ye londe legthe brede fonde lande joyned bretaign north ad land yaf brute albanack sone let kalle albanye hys name kalled scotlad brute fond othre contree toward west yaf camber hys sone let calle camber name ad nowe kalled wale wha brute regned xx yere sayd deyed cyte newe troye hys sone hym entryd wyt mochel honour lotryn brute sone crownyd king wyt mochel solempnite alle lande bretaigne wha crownyd albanack camber two bretheren went ayen hyr owne contre lyued mykel honour lotryn brother regned kyg gouerned land wel wysely good man wonder well beloued alle hys land befell albanack lotryns brother dwelled hys owne lande wyt mochel honour worshyp gouerned hys lad wysely thenne cam kyng humbar hunlad wyt grete power arriued albayne wolde haue coquered land began werre vpo albanack hy quelled bataille wha albanak slayne folck ye land fled vnto lotryn told kig bretaigne brother slayne prayed hy helpe auenge brother deth lotrine anon let assemble alle bretos ket douer derewent north folk southfolck keftefen lyndessey assembled sped fast ward ennemies yeue bataille lotryne sent caber brother shold come al hy alle power might make hy helpe dyd good come gedres toke wey preuelich sech hu bar wher might hym fynde betell hubar besides water grete ryuer wyt folk hy dispotre tho came lotryne caber brother hyr folk sodely er ony wist whan hubar saw hy come sore adrad moche men wist ad also vnarmed ad anone hubar drede lept water dreched hy selfe died men alle slayne none escaped ad therfore water called hu bar euermore shall called thus encheson kyng humbar therinne dreched lotryne wente hys shippes toke goold syluer moche fand vnto hym selfe ad othir pilfre yaf vnto othir folke hoost founden one shippes fayre damysell kyng humbars doughter kalled estilde whan kyng lotryne sawe hyr toke hyr hy hyr fayrnesse ouertaken wyt loue wolde haue wedded hyr tydyges came coryn anone thought auenge vpon lotrin moch lotryne made couenat spouse corines doughter kalled gue tolen coryn haste wente vnto newe troye ad thus sayd kyng lotryne nowe certes sayd ye rewarde full euell alle paynes suffred haue many tymes kyng brute fadre therfore wyll nowe auenge vpon yow ad drewe owt swerd hyghe wolde haue slayne kyng lotryne damisell wente bytwene hem made hem accorded maner kyng lotryne sholde spouse guentolen whiche corynes doughter ad lotryne dyde neuertheles spoused guentolen corines doughtyr preuelych came estrilde brought hyr chylde gate hyr fayre doughter called abra hit befell anone corine deyed anone ded kyng lotryne forsake guentolen hys owne wyfe made estrilde quene hys royaulme guetolen wente thes cornewaille seysed le londe hyr handes punctel moch hir faders heir ad vnderfong feaultres homage men land ad assembled grete hoost grete power ben vpon lotryne auenged hyr lord came hym yaf strog bataylle ther lotryn slayne men discomfited xv yere regne guentolen let take estrild abra hyr doughter ad lete bynde bothe ha de fete ad cast hem water drenched wher fore water euermore called abram name ye damisel estrildis doughter englisshmen calleth water seuerne walshmen calle abram day gwentelon let crowne hyr quene londe ad gouerned land full well wysely vnto tyme madan hyr sone lotryne beget vpon hir xx winter age myght king quene regnyd xv yere ad tho let hir sone crowne regned gouerned land well ad honorabely went cornuwaille ad ther dwelled hyr lyfes tyme pof kyng madan regned pee hys lyfes tyme ad menpris maulyn sone menpris slewe maulyn brother ad wulfes drow hym peces capitulo sexto whan vaylliaunt kyg madan regned xxx yere deyed lyeth newe cyte troye punctel two sone whyche owne called menprys men kalled maulyn thyse two brother hir fadres deth stryuen fast lande meprys encheson eldest sone wolde gladli haue lade punctel maulyn wolde graunte ne suffre hym token day loue accorde day mepris let quelle brother thurgh treson hym self afterward helde londe ad anone let crowne hym kyg regned ad bicame lither man destroied alle men hys londe last became wikked lecherous forsoke hys owne wyf vsed synne sodome wherfore almighty god wroth vpon hy toke vengeaunce day wet wode hountyng loste folke went allone vp ad downe crieng hys men ad ther came wulfes drowe peces regned xxiiij yere wha hys called edenburgh king xx sone ad xxiij doughtres dyuerse wymen goten ad sone called ye shal brute grenesheld margat seysel morgh wyth flenghan bladud iaky kybar rocelm spadogh gother kaier assaruth regned good man nygromancer capitulo xi lud ludibras regned bladud sone grete nygromancer thurgh hys craft nygromancye made meruaillo hothe bathe gest tellyth regned xxi yere lyeth newe troye pof kyng leyr answere iogest doughter gracyously maryed kyng fraunce capitulo xij kyng bladud regned leir sone thys leyr made towne lycestre let calle towne name gouerned towne wel nobely thys kyng leyr iij doughteres fyrst called gonorill second rygan thridde doughter called cordeill ad iongest doughter fairest ad best condicyos kyng hyr fadre became olde man wold hys doughtres maryed er deyde fyrst thought assaye whiche hem loued hym ad best whiche loued hy best shold best ben maryed axed fyrste moche hym loued answerd said better tha hyr owne lyfe nowe certes sayd fadre grete loue tho axed secod doughter moche hym loued sayd ad passyg alle creature ye worlde bi trouth sayd ye fadre may axe tho axed ye thridde doughter moche loued certes fadre sayd susters haue tolde yow glosing wordes forsothe shall telle trouth j loue moch j ought loue fadre ad bryng yow certayn loue yow shal yow telle ye bene worth ye loued kyng hyr fadre wende scorned become wonder wroth ad swore heuen erthe sholde neuer haue good doughters loued hy moch sholde ben wel auauced maried ye fyrst doughter maried managles kig scotlad second maried hanemos erle cornualle ordeyned spake bitwene sholde departe reaulme bytwene hem two deth kyg leyr hyr fadre cordeyl yongest doughter shold thyng haue land cordeyll wonder fayre good condicyos maners kyng frauce agape herde hyr speke ad sente kyg leir hyr fadre haue hir vnto wyfe praied hy therof kyng leir hir fadre sent hy word departed lo de vnto ij doughtres ad said lande wherwyth hir marie whan agape herde answer sente anon leir said axed nothyg hyr onely hir clothyng hyr anone kyg leir sent hyr ouer see kyng fraunce receyued hyr moche worship wyt moch solempnite spoused hir made hyr quene fraunce phow kyng leir driue owte hys land thurgh hys folye cordeill hys yogest doughter helpe hym hys nede capitulo xiij th fel afterward two eldelst doughtres wolde abyde tyll leir hyr fadre dede werred vpon hym while lyued moche sorwe shame hyd dyd wherfore benomen hy holy royaulme bitwene hem ordeined one shold haue kyng leir soiorne lyfe tyme xl knyghtes squyers might worshuply go ride whidder wolde cotre lyked pley solace managles kyng scotlad kig leir hym maner aboue sayd half yere wer passed corneil eldelst doughter ad quene scotland anuoyet hy peple anone ad hir lorde spake gedre wherfore knyghtes half hys squyers hy gone mo left xxx wha leir began make moche sorwe encheson estate empeired hy scorne despyte euer befor wherfore wist ye last thought wold go cornewaille rygan othir doughter whan comen erle wyf leires doughter welcomed hym wyth moche ioye dwelled wyt xxx knyghtes squiers dwelled ther scarsely xij monthes doughter hy wery ad companye hir lorde hy scorne despite fro xxx knyghtes broughte vnto x afterward v ther left moo tho made sorowe ynough ad said sore wepyng allas euer cam londe sayd yet ben better haue dwelled wt fyrst doughter anon wet thenes fyrst doughter anone hym saw come swore alle goddes ad bi moch might yt shold haue mo wt hi one knyght wolde ther abide tho bega leir ayen wepe made moch sorowe sayd tho ala haue longelyued sorwe meschyef falle poure som time riche haue frende ne kyn yt woll good wha riche men honoured worshipped euery man hath scorne despyte wote wel cordeil yongeste doughter said trouth whan sayd moch j moche shold ben beloued ad alle j good tho beloued ad honoured richesse two doughters glosed tho nowe sette lytell pry soth tolde cordeill wolde byleue ne vnderstande therfor j let hyr go fro thing sette lyttell pry j wote neuer syth yt two doughters thus haue disceyued j somoch loued nowe must nedes sech hir othir lad lightly let gone fro wytoute rewarde yeftes sayd loued moch ought loue hir fadre alle maner reson tho sholde haue axed hyr ad fayre beheftes thurgh fals speche ij eldest doughters disceyued thys maner leir log time began make mone last shope hy see passed ouer frau ce asked ad aspied wher quene might fonde told hy wher ad wha cam cyte ther preuely set squyer vnto ye quene telle hir hir fader comen hyr gret nedes wha squyer came quen tolde hyr euery dele hyr susters beghynyng vnto ye ende cordeill quene anon toke gold syluer plente toke ye squyer couseille shold gon bere vnto hir fadre shold go certay cite araye wasshe tha come ayen hir bringe hy honest copanye knightes x atte lest wt meyne shold sende hyr lord king saye yt comen speke wt doughtir seen dyd whan king ye quene herde camen wt mochel honour receyued kyng frauce tho let sende thurgh royaume mau ded alle men sholde hy entendaund kyg leir quenes fadre alle maner thyng self wha kyg leyr dwelled ther moneth tolde king ye quene doughtyr hys ij eldest doughtres serued agape anone let ordeyne grete hoost send bretaygne wt leir quenes fader conquere land ayen kygdo cordeyll also came wyt hyr fadre bretaigne haue ye royaume hyr fadres deth went ship passed see came bretaigne foughte felon scofyted quelled tho land ayen lyued thre yere helde royaume pee afterward deyed cordeill hys doughter hy let eburye mikel honour lycestre phowe morgan conedage neveus cordeyl werred vpon hir put hir pryso cap xiiij whan king leir dede cordeil yogest doughter helde land v yere mene time deyed hir lord agampe kyng fraunce ad deth left vydue tho came morga conedage cordeyl sustre sone hyr enymite moche aunte sholde haue lande bytwene ordeyned grete power vpon hir werred gretly ad neuer rest tyl hir taken put hir vn deth tho morga conedage seysed alle land departed bytwene hem helden xij yere wha ye xij yere gon ther began bitwene hym grete debate yt werred strogli togedre eueri hy dyd othir moche disese morgan wold haue lande fro beyonde hubar conedage helde came ayest hy wyt stroge power yt morga durst abyde fled away wale conedage pursued hi toke hi queld tho came conedage ayen seysed lade hade helde regned xxxiij yere tho deyed lyeth newe troye phow reygnold conedages sone regned aftir fadre time rayned blood thre dayes tokenyng grete deth capitulo xv conedage regned reygnold hys sone wise knight herdy curtois wel nobeli gouerned lad woder well made hym beloued alle maner folcke tyme rayned blode lasted thre dayes god wold sone ther came grete deth peple deyde without nobre wherfore man might skape tyll almighty god therof toke mercy pite tho began cese reignold regned xxij yere dyed lyeth york phow gorbodyan regned pee reygnoldes sone capitulo xvi reygnold regned gorbodia sone xv yere ad dyed lyeth york gorbodyan ij sone one slowe haue herytage ad ydoine hir moder quelled wherfor lad destroyed cap xvij gorbodya dede hys ij sone becamen stoute prowde euer warred gedre ye lad one called ferre othir porres ferres wold haue lad othir wold suffre hy ferres felos hert thought thurgh treson slee brother preuely wet frauce ther abode wt xix clote sone called donebat deth fadre became herdy man fayr curtois passed ye ky ge britaigne frauce hede worthynesse anon knight wist wel wha fader lyued rightfull heyr alle lad shold haue reson kiges yt stregth benome hy lad afterward donebant ordeyned power fyrst conquered ye lande loegiers wolde haue quered scotland walys scater cam men yaf hy bataill ad rudac cam aye walshmen helpe befell tha shold lese lyfe donebant made towne malmesbury towne ye vyse ad wha regned wel wortheli xl yere deyed lyeth newe troye phow brenne bely departed bitwene thay ye lad deth donebat hir fadre werre capitulo xxi doneband dede sone departed land bitwene hir fader ordeyned bely hys eldest sone lade thys half humbar brother brene lad fro humbar vnto scotland moch belyn best part brene therfore wroth wolde lad belyn brother wold graute hi wherfor cotak werre arose bytwene ij brene yonger brother might ne strengthe ayes bely ad therfor brene thurgh coseyl folck went fro thes norwey ye kyng olsinges praied hy helpe socour conquer ye lad vpon belyn hys brother vpo couenant wolde haue doughter wyfe kig olsinges hym graunted belyn anone brother norwey seised hys hade ye lande northuberland ad toke gutlagh hy tolde hyr cousell brene shold haue hir hir lede wt hy euermore shold lese hir wtoute might forsake delyuered fro brene ad wha gutlagh herd thys tidyg lay aspye bre ne wt many shippes might haue ye ij fletes mette gedre fougte log time brene shippes turned ayen discofyted kyg gutlagh toke samie put hir shippe brene shamefulli fled then discofyted gutlagh wolde haue gon ito owne co tre cam vpo hy grete tepest v dayes lastyd tepest driue bretaigne wyt iv shippes ad mo tho kept costes ye see token gutlagh famye folke presented belyn belyn put pryson phow belyn drofe oute hys lande kyng gutlagh demarke samye ca xxij hit longe ye brene came ayen grete nauye sete hys brother bely shold yelde ayen hys land wyf folke castelles elles wold destroye lade bely drade thig menace wold thing desyre wherfor bre ne came wyth folk ad fought belyn brenne discofyted folke slayne hy self fledde xij men fraunce belyn brennes brother went yorke toke couseyl might king gutlagh kyg gutlagh profred become hys man holde hys lade hy yeldyg yere thousand pounde siluer euer ad sikernesse couenaunts behold gutlagh shold bryg good hostage shold done homage folke yet shold swere vpon boke yt couenats shold neuer ben broke ne falsed belyn tho counseyl lordes folke grauted hy axyng gutlagh became man ad belyn vnderfeng hy homage othe writyng couenats vpo couenats king gutlagh nome samye newe toke folke feaultes homage went ayen lad ad came forth orkeney fode xxx shippes full men woman besides kost see ye king axed thei erle maistyr hem courtoysly aswerd vnto ye kyg sayd exiled oute tolde ye emperour tyding well wysely emour sent lande hi owne cosyn vncles sone noble knight stronge called maxymian spoused octauianus doughtyr crowned kyg lande maximian emours cosyn coquered almorican yaf conameriedok cap xlix king maxymia bicame ryall thought co quere land amorycan grete rychesse herde telle yt ther lande ne lefte man worthinesse knight squier ne none othir man ne toke wyt grete domage land left home behynd hi kepe lande toke hem hym fro land xxx thousad knyghtes doubthy mennys bodyes wet ouer lande amorican ther slewe king whiche called imball conquered alle lade wha done kalled cona said moch kyg octauyan haue made king bretaigne thurgh ye lette destrobled ye kyg yeue land amorican make therof kyg moche ye ben breton men also become fro bretaigne lad haue name ad nomore kalled amorica shal called lyttel bretaigne lad fro whes ye ben comen shall called mochel bretaigne ad shal knowe one bretaign fro conan moriedok thaked hi frendeli made kyg littel bretaigne wha al maximian went thes rome tho made emperour constantyne conan meriedok dwelled littel bretaigne mochel honour let ordeyne ijm plougme lade erye land harwe ad sawe fessed richely moche kyg conan ne none hys knyghtes peple wolde take wife nacyon frauce set tho grete bretaigne ye erle cornewaille men called dyonothe shold chese thurgh owt alle lande xjm maydens saye viij mene peple thre thousad gretest lordes sholde hem spouse whe dionothe vnderfounge comaudemet let seche thurgh ye grete bretaygne many nombre came man durst withstonde commaudements moche alle lad taken hymward kepe done thing hem good lyked whan alle maydes assembled let hem come hym londo let ordeyne shippes hastely asmoch nedeth ye vyage toke owne doughtere called vrsula fairest creature man wist ad wold haue sent hyr kyg conan shold haue spoused hir made hir quene land anone made preuely god vowe chastite hyr fadre wiste ne man elles lyuing vpon erthe vrsula xim maides copanye wet toward lyttell bretaigne martred coleyne cap l vrsula chese hyr companie xi maides ladye ad maistresse alle wente ship one tyme ye water yt called tamyse mau ded hyr kyn alle hyr frendes almyghty god ad sailled toward lyttell bretaigne come ye hygh see stro ge tepeste arose goddis wille vrsula wyt hyr shippes hyr panye dryue toward hundlad thurgh tempest arryued haue cyte coleyne kyg ye lad called gowan tho ye cite wha wist tyding many fayr maides ther arryued toke elga brother houshold hym went shyppes see fayre companye whan saw hem fayre companye wold haue ouer fayne betake fro hem hyr maydehode vrsula good mayd couseilled prayed warned thought hem hir felawes shold defende hir myght rather suffre deth suffre hir body defowled alle maydens became stedfast god thei defended grace none hem power done shame wherfore kig gowan sore anoyed wroth let slee hem euerychone ad alle maydenes martred loue god lyen coleyne phow kyg gowan came destroye lad grete power kalled gracyan deffended land capitulo lj wha kig gowa sarezy called brother elga sayd hy shold go co quere ye lad fayr maydes borne ordeyned tho grete power pechitet denmark orkoney norwey thei came lande bret townes slewe folck cast downe chyrches house religio robbed lad leght brede put deth alle wolde forsake right beleue cristedome moch ther soueraigne might helpe kyg maxymian take wyt hy alle ye worthy men goon coquere littel bretaign time ye telle seynt albone martred thurgh ye wode tyrant dyoclisia place abbye made seint albone whyles yt paynyme couerted hi god thurgh predicacyon clerk wyse man called antybell herburghed night howse thys incarnacyon jesu crist ccxxvi yere shal vnderstade sayt albone suffred martyrdome seynt edmond martred ad therfore seyt albone called fyrst martyr englond thys gowannes brother folk sarasynes wet thurgh oute land destroyed thig fonden thing ne spared whan tydyg cam rome kyng gowan bigonne destroye thys land emperour rome set strong man ad grete power called gracia wyt xxiiij men wel fyghtyng cast owt sarasenes owt land alle arryued porte mouthe maximian might come hym selfe moch chosen emperour deth constatin sait elynes sone whan gracya arryued host let aspie preuely wher kig gowa might fonde ad came vpo hem sodely lay hir beddes discomfited slew hem hyr beddes euery cho non hem escaped sauf gowan fled moche sorowe hys contre sone aftir maximian slayne rome thurgh treson whan gracyan wist tydyng let crowne hy self kyng lande phowe gracyan made self kyng whan maximia slay afterward ye breton queld wikkednesse c lij gracya wha began regne became wikked sterne moch dyd ye bretos thei slowe hy amoges tho ye kyg gowan vnderstod gracya slayne downe deth assebled grete power came ayen lad er harme tho dyd moch tho destroyed alle thys lade criste peple moche bretaign man herdie nempne god dyd anon put stroge deth bisshop londo tho called gosseley escaped wete thes rome seche socour helpe destroye sarrazenes yt destroyed land romays sayde thei ofte anoyed hir sending folke bretaigne helpe ye bretos wolde done ye bisshop gosseleyne went thes withoute socour helpe tho went kyg lytell bretaigne kalled aldroye ad thridde king gowa meriedoke sayd bisshop prayed thys kyng aldroye helpe socour kig grete pyte hys herte whan herde bisshop fledde cristen men slayne grete bretaigne thurgh paynyms sarazenes graunted hym constantyne brother helpe hy wyt power folke hym dyd araye hors armure shippes alle thig hem nedeth vyage whan thyng redy called bisshop hy said punctel take helpe socour co statyn brother vpon thys couenant god yeue grace paynymes sarazenes shende discofyte ye make hy kyg bisshop graunted hy good wille constantyne bisshop toke leue king aldroye betok hem god ad delyuerd thaym xij men wete hyr shippes sailled toward grete bretaigne arryued totenesse wha breton herde tydynges came socour stro gely holpen ordeyned hughe nombre peple cam moch honour gowa anon wist tydynges assembled sarazenes came ayenst hem yafe hem bataille constantyne slow owne handes alle sarazenes discomfyted slayne non escaped conuerted vnto god costantyne kynges brother lytel bretaign crowned kyg mochel bretaigne worthynesse capitulo liij annone bataylle went lodo crouned ther constatyne made hy king lande ad bisshop gosselyne sette croune hede anoyted falleth king ben tho began cristedome king costatine whan crowned anone spoused hys wyfe thurgh ye counseyll breton begate thre sone hir fyrste called constance othir aurelambros thridde vter constace eldest brother wha came age made hi mo ke wyncestre constatyne hyr fadre slayne thurgh treson befell tyme pehite came hy vpon day message said wolde speke preuely kyng counseyl king let voyde chabre ye men yt wythyne ther abode mo king pehyte mad cotenau ce though wolde haue spoke king ere ther queld hy longe knyfe went secretly oute chabre othir chabre last wist become wha ye kiges meyne wist hir lord ded made moche sorwe yt wist doo hys two sone anrilabros ad vter yo ge yt none might kyg ye thridde brother moke wi cestre sayd vortyger erle westsexe thought preuely herte queyntyse kyng punctel went winchestre ther constance monke said costa ce fader dede yowr two bretheren ben wyt gosseleyne bisshop lodo norysshe ben yonge none hem may king wherfor j cou seyll ye forsake habyt come shal breton ye shall made kyng pof constance kyng costantyn sone mok wynchestre made king hys faders deth counseyll vortyger yt erle westsexe moche aurylambros vter hys two brother yonge age vortyger let slee hy kyng hym selfe ca liiij thys vortyger couceylled thys constace moche tyll forsoke habyte went hy anone afterward crowned made kyg assent bretos kyng constauce whan crowned made kig wist ne knewe lytel ye world ne cowde thyg aparteigned kyng made vortyger chief maistre counseillier ad yaf alle power ordeyne asmoche royaulme aparteigned selfe thing entermedled onely bare name kyng whan vortyger sawe ye land ward gouernaille owne wyl thought pryue treson ad slee constaunce king might selfe ben crowned made king regne let sende c knyghtes pehites worthiest alle land helde thaym dwelle wyt hy kepars bodi wold wente thurgh lad ordeyne thynges aparteigned kyg vortyger honoured moche hodred knightes moche yafe thaym gold syluer ad ryche iewelles robe hors othir thyges ple te wherfore helde moch lord dyde kyg vortyger tolde yf might kyg ye thurgh treson wolde make richest lande ye last thurgh grete yeftes yeue largely cryed thurgh ye contre vortiger better worthy kyng costau ce wherfore vortyger made semblaut ben wroth departed then fro court said must gon elles whidder thi ge done ad traitour sayd encheson yt shold slee say constance whan vortiger gone befel sone ye ho dred knightes pehites broken dores kinges chabre ad ther slowe smoten heed bare vortiger ther dwelled vortiger saw heed wepte ful te derly wyth hys eye notheles full glad deth anone let take hondred knightes pehites bynde hir hades behynde lede londo ad dapned deth fals traitours anone alle breton ye lade comune assent crouned vortiger made hy king lande phow wardeyns two child kepe costatynes sone ladde hem lytel bretaygne treson falsenesse vortyger capitulo lv kyng vortyger wha crouned thei two childre keping aurylabros vter thurgh ordinace gosseleyne bisshop lodo hys deth durst dwelle lade ye child lad kyg litell bretaigne asmoche tho wist ye treson vortiger tho made king thurgh co stance hir brother slay wherfore hondred knightes pehytes put deth bare ye blame vortyger wist therof ne nothir ther consented kepars two child dred lest vortiger wold put deth thurgh hys treson falsenesse hyr brother beforne therfore lad ouer littel bretaigne kig thaym receyued mochel honour lete hem norysshe ther dwelled tyll becamen fayre knightes stronge fers thought auenged vpon deth costace hyr brother wha sawe hir time ad dyd ye shall telle afterward hit longe tydinges ne came ouer see kynred hondred knyghtes pehites dampned put deth vortiger lade therfore wo derly wroth swore wolde ben aueged hir kynnes deth camen thys land wyt grete power ad robbed many place queld dyd alle sorwe myght wha vortyger wist made moche sorwe sore anoyed place tydynges came aurilabros vter brother ordeyned ad assebled grete host come mochel bretaign saye lade ben auenged vpo constance hir brother deth one halfe ad othir brought moch sorwe ne wist whidder gon engist xj thousand men came lade vortyger yafe place kalled thong castell capitulo lvi sone sorwe tydynge came vortiger grete nauye stra giers arryued contre ket wist whes thei ne wherfore thei come lad kyg sente anone messagier thidder sholde come speke wyt hy wyt folke axed contre wolde gon ther two brethere maistres price strong copanye one kalled engist ad othyr horsse engist went king tolde encheson wherfore arryued lad said syr bene contre called saxonie lande ermanie wher yn moche sorwe peple moche lade may susteyne maistres prince haue lande gouerne rule maken comen hem men woman bolde ben amonge hem fyght best may trauaille dyuerse landes shall hem yeue hors harnaye armure alle thyng hem nedeth shall saye hem go othir cotre wher mowe lyue hir auncestres dyd beforne therfore syre king yf ye haue ought companye come lande wyth good well wyll serue lande helpe kepe defende enemyes yf ye aue nede wha vortiger herde tydinge sayd wolde glad hem withold vpon couenant might delyuere hys land enemyes wolde yeue hem resonable lode wher sho dwelle euermore engist tha ked goodly maner companye xjm shold dwelle king vortiger ad moche dyd thurgh boldenesse delyured land clene hys ennemyes tho prayed engyst kyng moche lad myght make hym cyte hym meyne kyng answerde done without couseyll hys bretos ne engyst prayed hym estsones moche lande place myght compose wyth thonge skynne wervpon might make hi maner dwelle kyng graunted hym freely tho nomme engyst bully skynne cut smale might thwoge roude ther compased moche lande made vpon fayr castell whe castell made let kalle ye thwoncastell moche place marked thonge pof romewen engistes doughtyr kig vortyger spoused hir hir beaute capitulo lvij wha castell mad full well arayed engyst sent letter co tre came hondred shippes fylled wyth stronge man bolde fyghtyng batailles ad shold bryng hem romewe hys doughter ye fayrest creature man might see whan peple comen sente toke hem castell moche ioye ad selfe vpon day wente vnto king prayed hym ther worthely wolde come se newe maner made place compassed thonge skynne kyng anone grauted freely hym wente thydder ad wel payed castell fayr werke ad gedre ther eten dronken wyt mochel ioye whan night came king vortyger shold gon chambre take ther nyghtes reste romewe engistes doughter came wt coupe gold hyr handes ad kneled king said hi waissaille ye kig wist mene ne shold aswere moche hym selfe ne none hys breton yet coude none englysh speke ne vnderstond spoken tho langages breton yet done neuertheles latiner tolde ye kig fulle vnderstanding ther waissaille ad shold aswere dryke haille first tyme wassaille drinkhaille came vp land tyme vnto time wel vsed lade king vortyger sawe fairnesse romewen armes layd aboute hir necke swetely kyssed hir anone right anamered vpon hir desyred haue hir wyfe ad asked engist hir fadre engyst graunted vpo thys couenat king shold yeue alle contre kent might dwelle theryn ad peple kyng graunted preuely wyt good anone spoused damysell moche cofusion selfe therfore alle breton became wroth encheso spoused woman mysheleue wherfor went fro thing toke kepe ne helpe thig phow vortymer vortigers sone made kyg engist dryue owte vortimer slayne cap lviij engist wet ket seised lad hys men ad bicame lyttell whill grete poer moch peple yt men wist lyttel tyme whiche kinges men engist men wherfor bretaigne drede said amog ne toke othir counseill betwene land shold betraied thurgh engyst peple vortiger ye king bigote first wife iij sone first called vortimer ye ij catagre thridde passet breton alle bi one assent chosen vortimer hir lord soueraine hir coucellier euery bataille crowned hy made hy king wolde suffre vortiger lenger regne encheson alia ce bitwene engist hy breton ordeyned grete host driue oute engist ad copanie lande yafe thre batailles first kent ther lorde secod tetforde thridde shire kalled nycoll bataille hem met catagre horsse engistes brother eche hem slewe moche contre yeue log horne thurgh vortyger tho spoused hys cosin ther made fair castell men called horne castell owne name vortimer anoyed brother deth catagre dede suche maner wherfore anone let felle ye castel grou de ne lest night ne day tyll dryue owt engist peple lande ad whan engist driuen away romewen doughtyr made sorwe ynowe queyntely spake next king vortymer pryuyest hym moche yaf yestes enpoisened deyed lo iiij yere hys regne ad ther lyeth breton chose othir tyme vortiger theyre kyng engyst came ayen thys lande foughten gedre capitulo lix vortemers deth breton bi hir mune assent estsones made vortiger hir king vpon couenant yt shold neuer suffre engist ne none estsones comen land wha done romewen ye quene preuely sete letter engist epoisened vortymer vortyger hir lord ayen bare crowne regned shold come land well arayed moche peple auenge vpon breton wynne lad ayene wha engist herde tidinge made grete ioye apparailled hym hastely xv thousand men yt doubgthy euery batayll came thys land wha vortiger herd telle engyst ayen come grete power land assembled breton wente ayenst engist haue yeuen bataill ad folke engist drad hy sore breton discofyted beforne driuen owte wt strengthe wherfore engist prayed loue day ad said comen lande fight haue lade ayen might accorde breton hem haue grace kyg vortiger thurgh couceyll hys bretos grau ted loue day ad thus ordeyned thurgh breton loue day shold ben holde fast besyde salysbury vpo hyll engist shold come thidder wyt iiijc knightes withoute moo king many ye wysest lande day kyng came cou seyll ordeyned engist warned knightes preuely hem comauded euery hem shold put longe knyf hose whan said fayre syres nowe tyme speke loue pee euery man anon shold drewe knyfe slee breto quelled thousand lxi knyghtes moche sorowe many hem escaped ad ye king vortiger selfe tho taken lad thongcastell put pryson engystes men wolde kyng ben brent quyke ad vortiger haue lyfe grauted hem asmoche wolde axe yaue vp alle landes townes castelles cytees burghes ne knewe neuer land vortiger helde hy ther breton ared cou ceyl best done yaf couceyll make stronge castell might self therynne kepe ad defende nede werkmen anone begannen werke castell vpo ye hylle breigh certes thus befel ye werke mason made day fell downe night wyst myght ben therof king sore anoyed chauce wist done wherfore sent wylest clerkes also alle lerned men thurgh oute wale might fonde sholde telle wherfore foundament failled vnder werke sholde hym telle thyng best done punctel whan thiese clerkes ad wyse maistres longe tyme studied sayden king shulde done seke chylde borne woman neuer man done childe sholde slee tempre hys blode mortier werke sholde werke euer endure withoute ende howe kyng lete seche merly thurgh alle wale speke wyt hym capitulo lxi whan king herde comauded hys messagiers anone wete thurgh oute alle wale seke ye childe yf might hym fynde shold bringe hym forth vnto recorded witnesse thys thynge delyuered lres thei ne destroubled man ne lette tho messagiers wente thes spedde fast came towne yt kalled karmardyne ad thei passed forth hir waye fonden two chyldre xiiij yere age chydyg gydre wt hasty wordes one hem said othir done bat sayd ye done wronge chydde stryfe ye haue ne wit ne reson haue certes merly said ye child wit ne yowr reson make force men telle comuneli ye haue thing god almighty syth ye neuer fadre euery man knoweth well moder messagyers king vortyger wha herde stryfe bytwene ye two chyldren axed hem stode besydes hem whes merlyn borne also norisshed folke tolde grete gentyll woman bare karmardyne called adhan neuer man might wite might chyldes fadre whan kynges messagiers herde tydig ten anone wardeyne towne tolde hy kynges wyll lre shewed hy wherfor come thydder merlyn moder anon set fore ye wardeyne towne commaunded hem sholde gon kyng ordeyned messagiers merlyn moder wente then camen fore kyg vnderfonge wyt mochel honour kyg axed lady yf ye childe hyr sone begate lady answerde full tederli wepyg ad said neuer companye man wordely syre kyng quod yoge mayden fadres chabre grete lygnage companye ofte tymes wot playe solace beleft allone chambre wold gon owte brennyng ne vpon time ther came fayre bacheler entred chambre ther allone came wiste neuer ne yet wote j dores fast barred wyt dyd game loue ne might ne power deffende fro ofte cam forsaid maner begate thys chylde neuer might wyt pof answere merly wher king axed hys werke might stande begonne ner proue cap lxij wha merly herde moder sayd spak kyg thys maner syre begote axe ye fallyth nought ne non othir wyte telle encheso wherfor brought wherfore ye haue sent certes said king wyse counceilliers haue vnderstode ye mortier werke j haue begone behoued tempred blode fou dament shall faill euermore syr sayd merlyn wyll ye slee
