sought fonde came kyng kig tolde hys monument yt wold haue made tho answerde merlyn kyng saide ben grete stone jrland loge vpon hyll kylia men kalled geants karoll yf place ben shold endure euer remebraunce knightes ben entered throuth sayd king hard stone lad jrland soth said merly landes bene suche geants set hem grete good hem selfe eueri time wouded maner hurte wesshe stone hote water ad wesshe hem self ther anone hole breton wente seche grete stone irland capitulo lxvi whan bretos herde thys thing wet ad swore among wolde gone seche stone nomme hem vter ky ge brother ben hir cheueteyne xvm men merlyn couceylled hem gon irlad ad dyde whan kyg irlad called gwillomer herd tell straugiers arryued lade assebled grete power fought ayenst folk discofyted bretos wente forth tyll came ye monte kylian clemed vnto ye mote wha saugh stone ye maner thei stode thei grete mervaille sayd bytwene sholde remene strength ne engyne hughe ad loge merly thurgh craft queytise remened brought hir shippes came ayen land merly sette stone yt kyg wold haue set ye maner stode irlad wha kyg saugh yt made tha ked merly rychely hy rewarded owne wille place kalled stoheuge euermore passet vortigers sone ye kyg guillomer cam lad traitour called coppa epoisened king aurilabros ca lxvij men shall vnderstode passat vortyger sone liued ye tyme came thys lade wyth grete power ad arryued north contre wolde ben aueged fadres deth vortyger strongely trusted vpon co panye brought hy owt lande germayne conquered alle north contre vnto york whe king aurylabros herd assembled grete hoost brytons went fyght hy peple discofyted passent eskaped then wyth folke fled thes irland ad came kyg guillomer prayed helpe socour kyng graunted hy wyt good wyll ad saide wold helpe vpo couenat selfe must gone alle power bretaigne wolde auenge vpo bretos rather lande came token stone streth called geants karoll kyg guillomer let ordeyne hys shyppes wente see xv thowsand men arryued wale begone robbe moch sorwe done hit befell kyg aurilambros lay seke wychestre might helpe self sent name vter brother grete power helpe wale ad thydderward wente moch might king irlad passent herd telle aurylabros seke came sarazen called coppa said sire dwelle ye pee wyt hoost behote yow thurgh queyntyse shal slee kyg aurylabros seke ye said passet shal yow rycheli auauce traitour coppa put vpon habyt relygyon let shaue brode crowne came kyges court ad sayde wolde hele kyg maladie tho said ye traitour ye king syr ben good confort shal yeue suche medicine ye shall swete anone right luste slepe haue good rest ad traytour yaf hy suche poyson slept anone ryght ad deyed slepyg traitour said wold gone owte felde tyl wer awaked escaped away suspectyon encheson habbyt clothed also brode croune wha kinges men wisten dede moche sorwefully soughte fast traitour might fynde hy coppa turned ayene ye hoost fro whes comen yt wha aurilabros dede ye mornyg sterne seyne wt clere light bought beme seyn hede orryble dragon cap lxviij wha kig aurilabros thus dede winchestre morne dede aboute ye time prime ther seyne grete sterre clere ye beme ye sterre brighter tha sonne ye bought ye bee appered dragos hede oute mouth came ij grete lightes bryght fyre brenyg yt one beme saw toward frauce straught ouer ye see thidderward owt beem came vij bemes full clere longe light fyre thys sterre seyn many man none wist betokened vter yt kyges brother walys wt host bretos sawe sterre ye grete light yaf wodred ther gretly might betoke let calle merly praied hy telle might betoke pof ye betokenyg ye sterre cap lxix merlyn saw ye sterre behelde hy loge time fithenes quoke ad wept tenderly ad sayd allas allas noble kyg worthy dede j vnderstade aurilabros brother epoisoned j see wel sterre self betokeneth ye heed ye drago seyne ye bought ye bee self yt shal kyg regne bi ye bee stond towardes ye est vnderstode ye shal gete sone yt shal conquere frauce lades longyg ye croune frauce shal worthier kyg honour euer aucestres bee stryght toward irland betokened ye shall gete doughtir shal quene jrland vij bemes betokened punctel ye shal haue vij sone euery shall kyg regne wyt mochel honour abyde ye le ger goo yeue bataill enemyes fight wyt boldely ye shal ouercome haue victorie vter thaked hertely merly toke hys men went toward hys enemyes foughten gedre dedely discofyted ennemies destroyed hym self quelled passet vortigers sone breton queld gwillomer yt king irlad men vter anon aftir bataill toke way toward wychestre done enburye aurylabros king yt hys brother tho body brought stohege wyt mochel honour made remebrauce ye bretos slayn thurgh treson engist day shold haue beu accorded ad place beryed aurylabros secode yere regne wyt worship myght beloge kyg who sowle god haue mercy pof vter pendragon wher kalled ye shall ouertake wyt ye grete loue jgerne ye erles cornewaill wyfe c lxx deth auryla bros vter brother crowned regned well worthely remebrauce dragon lyked let make ij dragon thurgh cou seill breton one bore beforne hy whene wet bataille abyde wynchestre bysshoppes chyrche encheson called euer vter pe dagron otta engystes sone commended lyttell vter made newe kyng ayest hy began meve werre ordeyned grete copanye hys fredes kyne offa brother yt take lad fro huber vnto york thei york helde strongely ayenst wold suffre hem come towne nothir yelde cyte hem besieged towne anone right yafe ther stro ge assaulte cyte kepte well strogly wha vter herde therof came thydder grete power helpe reseue toune put awey siege yafe stroge bataill ad otta copanye deffended well might last discofyted ye part queld otta offa take put pryson lodo vter hy self dwelled yorke ad went lo ester suyng wolde crowned holde solempne fest let sompne hys erles baros thei shold come fest ad thei wyfes shold bringe hem also fest thei came kynges commaudement commauded fest rychely holden worthely sette mete estate erle gorloys cornewaille jgerne wyfe seten alther next king kig sawe fairnesse ladi rauisshed hir beaulte ad ofte made hir nyce semblaut lokyng lawghyng last erle perceyued pryue lokyng lawghyng loue bytwene hem aroos vp fro table wroth toke wyfe called knightes went thes wrath withoute takyg leue king king anone sent shold come aye go thes despyte hy ye erle wold come aye maner wyse wherfore king full wroth wrath deffied dedely enemye erle went then cornewaylle wyf castel ty tagell kyng let ordeyne grete hoost ad came cornewaille destroye erle myght put hym suche castell stronge wel arayed tyntagell wold yelde hy king kyg anone besieged castel dwelled xv dayes neuer might spede euer thought vpon jgerne vpon hir laid moche bone nyst dou last called hy knight called vlfyn pryue hy told hy couseyll axed hym best done syre sayd dothe send merlyn kan telle yow best cou seyl man lyuing merlyn anone sent came ye king king told hym hys wyll syr said merly shal done moch thurgh craft j yt shall make yow come nyght castell tyntagel ye shal haue lady phow vter bigate igerne yt erles wyf cornewaill kyng arthour capi lxxi merlyn thurgh crafte cowde changed ky ge figure lykenesse erle vlfen garlois chambirlayne vnto figure iurdan erles chabyrlayne eche hem trasfigured othir lykenesse wha merlyn done sayd kyg syr mowe ye goo sodenly castel tyntagel axe entrie haue wyll king toke preuely hoost gouerne lede knight moch loued ad toke way toward ye castel vlfyn chaberlayne merlyn whan came thydder portier wed ben owne lord whan tyme cam go bedde king went bedde igerne erles wyf dyd wyt hir wille bygate vpon hir sone called arthur vpo morne noble myghty king toke leue lady ad went ayen hys hoost ye night kig lay bi jgerne bedde wyt erles wyf kinges knightes men yauen stronge assault castel erle men manly deffe ded last befell assaulte erle self slayne castel taken kyng anone turned aye tyntagel spoused igerne wyth mochel honour made hyr quene sone tyme came shold deliuered bere chylde sone whiche kalled arthour gate hir doughtir whiche kalled amya wha came age wa nobely maryed noble baron kalled aloth lord leon whan vter longe tyme regned ther came vpon grete sekenesse sorwe ye mene time thei kepe otta engistes sone offa hys brother tho pryson let hem gone owt grete yeftes yaf wente hem wha two brethere escaped ad came ayen hir owne contre ordeyned hem grete hoost grete power begonne werre vpon king kyng vter chose alot kepe land bretaigne whyles seke moche might helpe hy self sekenesse capitulo lxxij asmoche kyg vter seke myght helpe hy self ordeined alot sone eley yt tho chosen wardeyne ad chiueteyne folke anon hys breton assebled grete host yafe bataille otta ad hys folke otta last discofyted hit befell th afterward bretos indignacyon aloth wolde hym ben attendaunt wherfor kig anoyed wonder sore let hi putte horse litter ye host amonges folke lad hy veroloyne tho fayre cyte ther seyt albone martred cite destroyed paynim thydder sente otta offa ad hyr peple dwelled towne let make fast yates ther helde hem kig came besieged made stro ge assaulte yt thery manly hem defended kyng let ordeyne gonne hys engynes breke walles ad stronge thig myght hem mysdoo otta hys peple grete despite kig lyggyng lyttier hem besieged toke counseyll amonges hem ryse vp morwe ad come owte yeue bataille vnto king dyden bataill bothe otta offa slayne al e ye escaped fled scotland made colegryne hir chyuetayne saxon alyue escaped fro bataill broughten ayen grete strength amonges hem saide kyng vter dede thei shold wel conquere land amoges hem thoughte enpoisen ye king ordeyned men done dede yaf yeftes grete plente thing ordeyned hem thidderward ther kyng dwellyg clothed poure habites better spedde hyr lyther purpose neuertheles alle falsenesse queytyse might neuer come nygh kyg last aspied king drake none licour onely water clere welle ther nyghe besydes ad thees fals traytour vpon daye preuely wente welle put therin poyson water enpoysened anone king dronke ye water bega swelle sone deyed many droke water deyde also anone falsenesse aspied folke towne let stoppe ye welle euermore whe king dede hys folke bere stonhege wyth grete solempnite bysshops baros yt enburyed hy beside aurylambros brother turned ayen euerycho let sende aftyr arthour hys sone made king ye lad moche reuerece aftir faders deth ye xvij yere regne phow arthour sone vter crowned hys faders deth drofe colegryne saxon cheldryck almaygne owt thys lad c lxxiij whan arthur made king ye lad punctel yonge age xv yere faire bolde doubty body meke folke good courtoys ad large spedyng made hy well beloued among alle men ther nede whan bega regne swore saxos neuer sholden haue pee ne rest tyll dryuen thay owte lad assebled grete hoost fought colegrine tyme otta dede saxon mayntened colegryne discofyted fledde vnto yorke toke toune ther helde hi kyg besieged towne might spede towne stronge withynne kepte ye towne wel orpedly mene tyme colegrine let towne bladulf fled hi selfe cheldryke king almaigne haue socour king assembled grete power came arryued scotland wyt vc shippes arthour wist thys tydyng power ne stregth ynough fight ayes childrike let ben siege wente londo sente anone lres ye kyg littel bretaignn called hoell neveu sustres sone shold come hi wyt power might assebled grete hoost arryued southmpto wha artur yt wiste glad wet ayest hy receiued hy moch honour ye ij hostes assebled toke hir way nycol yt cheldryck besieged yet take came vpo childrik vpo peple er thei jt wist ther egrely assailled king cheldryk ad meyny defended maly hyr power kyg arthur queld many saxos neuer er sayne suche slaughter ad cheldryk men left lyue fledden awaye arthour pursued drofe wode might ferthir passe cheldryk ad men sawe wel thei brought moche dysese yolde hem arthur maner shold take hir hors hir armures suffre thay go fote hir shippes sholde gon owne lade neuer come agayn land vpon assurauce thyg yaue hy good hostage arthur bi couseyll hys men graunted thyg receiued hostage vpo ye wet hir shippes whan ye see hir mynde chaunged deuell wolde retourned hyr nauye came ayen land arryued tottenesse wet hir shippes toke ye lad clene robbed slewe moch peple token armure might fynde wet forth tyll came bathe men towne shitte fast hir yates wolde suffre come wyth towne deffended wel orpedly ayens howe arthour yafe bataill saxon whan came aye besieged towne bathe ad hem ouercame cap lxxiiij whan arthour herde thys tydinge let hage anon hostage lefte hoel bretaigne neveu kepe marche toward scotland half peple hy selfe te helpe reskew ye towne bathe whan came thydder punctel yaf stroge bataill cheldrik killyd peple man might stond ne endure vnder stroke swerd ad ther bothe slayne colegryne ad bladulf brother cheldrik fledde thes wolde haue gone hys shippes arthur wist toke xm knightes cador erle cornewaill lete stoppe comyg self te toward marche scotlad messagiers told hi ye scottes besieged hoell bretaigne ther lay seke therfore hasted thydder ward cador pursued cheldryk toke hi er might come shippes queld cheldryke hys peple whan cador done thys voyage hasted hym ayen faste might towardes artur fonde scotlad ther reseued hoell bretaigne scottes al ferre mouref punctel ther held hem artur hem pursued fled then limoigne co tre lx jles grete plete briddes grete plente egles wont crye fyght gedres ad make grete noyse wha folk come robbe land werren moche thei myght dyden ye scottes grete rauennours token myght fynde lad lymoigne without sparyg ther thei charged ayen folke scotlad wente king artur axed merlyn auentures vj laste kynges regne englond howe land shold ende capitulo lxxv sire sayd merlyn yere incarnacyo jesu criste mccxv shall come lambe owte winchestre shal haue whyte thonge trewe lippes shall haue write herte holynesse la shal make many goddes house shall haue pee part hys lyfe shall make one fairest place world hys tyme shall fully made ende ye ede lyfe wolf straug land shall moche harme sorwe thurgh werre ye ende ye labe shal maister thurgh helpe rede fox shal come nortwest hy shall ouercome wulf wolf shal deye water ad aftir tyme labe shal lyue ne shal deye sede tha shal straunge land ye land shal withoute gouerneur litell whyle tyme shal come dragon melled mercy eke wyth wodenesse shall haue berd goot shall yeue englond sadewe shall kepe land colde hete ad owne foot shal sette wyke ye londo shal enbrace inhabitacyons ad shall open mouth toward walys tremblyng hydour mouthe hys eres shal strech toward many inhabitacions ad contreys breth shall full swete straunge lande time shal ryuers renne wt blode rayne ad shal make place lad walles shulle moche harme vnto seed tyme thene shal ther come peple owt northwest regne shal lad thurgh owt wikked hare ye drago shal crowne kyng whyche afterward shal flee ouer see wythout comyng ayen drede drago tyme sonne shal rede bloode men tha shal see thurgh al world whiche shal betoken grete pestilence deth folk thurgh dent swerde peple shal fadreles tyl time drago shal deye thurgh hare shal mewe ayenst werre vnto end lyfe yt shal fully ben ended hys time dragon shall hold tyme best body alle world shall deye besydes march straunge lande ad land shal dwelle fadreles without good gouernour men shal wepe deth ile scheppey vnto haue marcyll wherfor allas shall commune songe fadreles folke shull ouerlyuen hys land destroyed thys dragon shall come goot owt kar shall haue horne berde syluer ther shall come nostrell domp shal betoken hunger sorwe ad grete deth peple punctel moche lade begynnyng regne shall wasted goot shal go fraunce shall opene flour hys lyfe deth pin time ther shal aryse egle cornewaille shal haue tethres golde pride shal wythout pere la de shal despyse lordes blode ad shal flee shamefully bere gauersech shull made brigges men vpon costes see ad stone shull fall fro castelles many townes shull made playne tyme shal seme bere shal brenne ad bataill shal vpon ye armes ye see feld ordeyned sheld ad bataill shal deye many white hedes wherfor batayll shall called white bataill forsayd bere shall done goot moche harme ad shal come southwest blood shall goot lese moche hys lande tyll tyme shendshyp shal hym ouercome shal clothe lyon skynne shal vailliauntly wynne hast lost therto peple shall come owt northwest shal make goot sore drad tha shal auenge hym hys ennemyes thurgh counseyll twoo owles whyche fyrst shull ben paryll bene vn done olde owle shall wete certayne tyme therafter shall come ayene land thise two owles shall grete harm many ad shal cou seylle goot shall arere werre ayest forsayd bere last goot owles shall come burton vp tret shull wente ouer ad drede bere shall flee swan fro companye burton toward north ad ther thei shull ben hard shour swan shall slayne sorwe bere taken beheded alther next nest shal sto de vpon broke brygge sonne shall cast hir bemes ad many shall hy seke vertu fro hi shal come jn shal deye sorwe ad care peple lad many lades shull ben hy bolder afterward two owles shulle doo moch harme forsaid flour delyse shull hyr lede distresse yt shall passe ouer frau ce make pee bytwene goot flour delyse ther shall dwelle tyll tyme hyr seed shal come seche hir ad shull hem clothe grace shull seche two owles ad shull put hem despytous deth shall goot ben brought dysese grete anguysshe ad sorwe shall lyue alle hys lyfes tyme thys goot shall come oute vyndesore bore shall haue hede white lyon herte ad pytous lokyng vysage shal reste seke men brest shall stanchyng therst ben therst worde shal gospel beryng shal meke lambe pin first yere regne shal haue grete payne iustifye hem ben vntrewe tyme shall lad multiplyed wt alien bere thurgh fiersnesse herte shall haue shall make wolfe become lambes shal called thurgh owt world boor holynesse fersenesse nobylesse ad mekenesse shall done mesurably shall haue vnto burgh jerusale shall whette hys teth vnto yates parys vpon fowre lades spaigne shal tremble drede gascoyne shal swete fraunce shal put wynge hys grete taille shall reste englond softely almaigne shal quake drede hy boor shal yeue two matelles ij tounes englond shal made ryuer renne blood ad brayne shall made many medewes red ad shall gete moche auncestres dyden ad er shal dede shal bere thre crownes shall put land grete subiectyon shall releued hys tyme thys boor dede doughtynesse shal entered coloigne land shal tha fullfylled alle good boor shall come labe shal haue foot leed hede bra hert loppe swynes skyn ad harde hys tyme lad shall pee fyrst yere regne shal make cyte ye world shall speke therof lambe shal lese tyme grete part hys lade thurgh hydous wolf shal recoure yeue lord ship egle landes ad egle shal well gouerne tyl tyme pryde shall hym ouergone allas sorowe shal deye brother fuered shal lade fall forsaid labe whiche shal gouerne land pee hys lyfes tyme punctel shal deye lade ful fylled maner good labe shal come molde warpe kursed goddes mouthe caytyfe coward hare shall haue elderly skyne gote vengeaunce shall fall vpon hym synne fyrst yere regne shal haue alle good grete plente lande toward also land shal haue grete preysing tyll tyme shall suffre peple lyue moche pride withoute chastisyg wher god wyll wroth shall aryse vp dragon north whiche shall fulfers ad shall mewe werre ayenst forsaid molde warpe shall yeue hy bataill vpon stone dragon shall gadre ayene hys companye wolfe shal com owt west begynne werre ayest forsaid molde warpe hys syde shall dragon bynde hyr taylles gedre shal come lyon owte irland whiche also shall falle companye hem shal tre ble land tha shall called englond aspen leef pand tyme shulle castelles felled downe vpon thamyse shal seme neuer shal flothe bodyes shull falle dede theryn fowre chyef flodes englond shull renne bloode grete drede shull anguysshe shal arrysen ther molde warpe shal flee ad drago lyon wolfe shull dryue away lande shall withoute hem molde warpe shal haue maner ne power sauf onely shippe wher shall mowe flee wente ad shall gon lande whan see withdrawe shal yeue thridde part lande haue fourth part pee rest shal lyue sorwe lyfes tyme hys tyme hote bathe shulle becomen colde ad shall molde warpe deye auetoursly allas sorowe shal drayt flode see seed shal become fadreles straunge lad euermore shal land departed thre partyes saye wolfe drago lyon shall euermore shal lad kalled land conqueste shulle righful heires englond ende arthour ouercame gwillomere king irland scotes became men capitulo lxxv wha guillomer king irland tydy ge kyng arthur entred glastenbury ordeyned grete power ire men came see ire peple came scotland ouer see arryued faste ther kyg arthour hoost anone wiste therof wente towardes hem ad yafe bataill ouercame anone right gwillomer fledde wyt men ayen irlad wha disconfyture done arthour turned hym ayene ther yt place ther lefte scottes wolde haue slayne bisshoppes abbotes othir folke contre ladyes wyth opehede came kyg arthour creyd mercy saide gentyll king mighty haue mercy pyte v selfe ben right lawe hold maynte cristedom full grete dishonour sholde kylle hem byleue almyghty god ye goddes loue haue mercy ad pyte v suffre v lyue haue moche sorwe payne saxos haue many tyme thurgh lade passed ynowe often tymes haue done v sorwe dysese castelles haue taken bestes slayne eten moche harme haue v ye wolde v quelle non honour kyg quelle hem cryen mercy ye haue v ynowgh ouercome ad loue god suffre v lyue haue mercy crysten peple byleuen crist ye whan king arthour herde sorwe pyte hem ad yaf hem hyr lyfe fyll done foot became liegeme ad toke homage aftyr kyng arthour turned ayen wyth hys hoost came yorke abode duryng vyage tho yaf loegers aloth spoused hys suster othir yeftes grete ple te tho gawen cosin yonge age alle hys men hym serued hys werke yaf ryche yeftes thaked hem moche hyr good seruyce phow kyng arthour spoused gunore gunores cosy erle cornewaille co querede gwillomer irland capitulo lxxvij wha arthur brought land pee rest ad goode state rest euery cotre tho toke wedded wyf whiche called gunnor made hir quene ad fayre lady gentyll cador erle cornewaill longe tyme norysshed cha bre owne cosyn neuer childe gedre ad neuertheles kyng arthur loued hir wonder well derely anone wyter passed let assemble grete hoost alle hys baron sayd wolde te irlad coquere ye lad taryed longe ne passed ouer irlade gwillomer king let assemble grete host yaf bataill kyg arthur gwillomer discofyted yolde hy kyg arthur bicame man hy dyd feaulte homage hy helde land fro tyme forward passed kig arthur furthermore coquered gutland island toke homage folke lode ther dwelled xij yere pee regned ioye myrthe werred maner man ne vpo hym bicame courtoys large honorable emperours court rome ne none thurgh ye world accompted king arthour wist ne non well preised therfore best knightes alle maner lode came hi dwelle ad receiued good wyll reuere ce ad knightes good knewe werst ad therfore kyg arthur made rou de table wha thei sholde sytten mete shull alyche hir euen lyk serued table none might make awaunt one wer hyer tha othir ad king arthur table breton fressh men norman flemyges bourgouners mauser lotherms alle landes halfe monthe gorye also hys lande bretaigne grete lade cornewayille walys irland scotland shorteli telle alle landes wolden worship chyualrye seche punctel camen king arthoures court phow king arthour came fraunce conquerd land froll romayne hym queld capi lxxvij hit befell kyg arthur thurgh counseyll hys baros lordes wold gon conquere frauce tho cleped galle thurgh romais helde lade hir power hyr lordship romays take lad noble knyght ad worthy body kalled frolle wha wist arthur came ordeined host grete power fought wyt king folke discomfyted thennes fled vnto parys entred towne ad closed fast yates wha arthour wyst froll gone paris pursued cam thydder hy besieged cyte stroge well arayed thei withyn defended hem wel ad manly king arthour dwelled moneth ther moch peple cyte vytailles faylled grete huger bicame amo ge hem deyden wonder thykke cyte hunger camen frolle praied hy ben accorded kyg arthur haue pee wolde yelde hym ad towne also froll saw lenger ne might holde towne ayenst hir wylle trust gretly vpon hys owne strength sent kyng arthour shold come fight wyth hym body body shold departe frauce bitwene hem two kyng arthour anone grauted ad wolde non peple shold vndertoke hym vpon morwe bothe camen well armed aboute cyte paris grene felde ther shold fyght anone smytten gedres fyersly well foughte bothe sydes man cowde deme better hem befell frolle yaf arthur suche stroke kneled grownde wolde nolde frolle withdrowe swerde wounded king arthour forhede blood fell downe eye face arthur anone sterte vp hertely whan felte hym hurt man semed almost wode toke tabourne goode swerd drewe vpon hygh yafe frolle suche stroke therwith clafe heed downe sholdres yt helme might warrant fyll anon dede place cyte made grete sorowe frolle neuertheles anon yolde kyg arthur ye towne also became men dyde hy homage feaulte vnderfege toke good hostage king arthur went forth wyth hoost coquered angie angiers gascoigne pehyto nauerne bourgoigne barry lotherne tury puthiers othir lad frauce conquered holych ad whan conquered take homage feaultes turned ayen paris ther dwelled log tyme ordeyned pee log tyme ouer cotrey thurgh alle frauce wha pee made ouer thurgh hys noble knighthood also hys owne worthynesse man grete lord durst meve werre ayest hy nothir aryse make land frauce quyte pee dwelled ix yere ad dyde many grete wondres reproued many proude man ad lyther tyraunt chastysed hyr deseruyng kyng arthur auauced men trauailled seruyce capitulo lxxix afterward befel th estre ther helde fest paris rychely began auauce knightes hir seruyce holpen conquest yafe styward called kay angye angiers beddeler brother yaf normandye tho called nestrie holdyne chabirlayn yaf flaudree mace dorell cosyn yaf boloigne ad richard nevew yaf po tyf othir yaf large landes fee aftyr yt estate wha arthour th hys knightes feffed auerill next sewyg came ayen britaigne owne lad aftir whytsontyde next sewyg bi cou seil baros wold crouned king glomergo helde solepne fest let sompne kynges erles baron sholde come thidder euerichone punctel scater kyg scotlad cadwre king southwales gwillomer king northwales maded king irland malgam king gutland achilles king iseland aloth kyng denmarck gone king norwey hell hys cosyn kyg dorkeney cador king lyttell bretaigne norwyth erle cornewaill maura erle gloucestre gwerdon erle wynchestre boellerle hertford vrtegy erle oxuford cursall erle bathe ionas erle chestre enerall erle dorchestre kymare erle salisbury waloth erle caterbury iugerne erle chichestre arall erle leicestre ad erle warwyke many othir rych lordes breton also ther cam mo yt say dippon donan gene many othir nepned feste many fair fest kyg arthur hold beforne neuer none suche ne solempne lastid xv dayes mochel honour myrthe pof letter sent fro cyte rome pryde kig arthour ca lxxx iij day kig arthur sate mete amoges kiges amog setten fest forne came xij eldren men age richely arayed courtously salued kig said camen fro rome sent messagiers fro emperour toke hy lettre th moche vnderstode gretly v mervaylleth arthure thow art one hardy yen thi hede make open werre cotake ayens v rome owen worlde deme thow hast neuer yet beforne tyme proued ne assayed stregth ye romains therfore thou shalt lyttell tyme iuli cesar conquerd lad bretaign toke ther truage oure folk haue longe thurgh thy pride thou witholdest wherfore commaunde thou yelde ayen yet hast thou foly done thou hast slayne frolle baron fraunce wro ge therfore alle commune rome warnen commau de vpon lyue lyme thou hast rome amedes make thy mysdedes thou hast done ad yt thou come nought shull passe hylle ioye strengthe shull seke wher euer thou may fonden thou shalt haue fote lad thy owne ne shall destroye afterward wyth thy body shull wille wha lre rad men herd noyed alle solempnite bretos wolde haue slain messagiers kyg wolde suffre hem ad sayd ye messagiers sholde haue none harme mowe reson none deserue commaunded hem worshipfully serued mete toke couseyll kinges erles baron answere might best yeue ayen messagiers cou ceylled onys shold asseble grete hoost ad power lades lordship manly auenge hy vpo emperour despyte sent suche letter thei swore bi god bi name shold hym purswe brenne moche might sayde nold neuer faill kyg arthour rather dede let wryte lettre sende ye emour bi messagiers maner bolde answere king arthour send emperoure rome ye romais ca lxxxi vnderstondeth amonges yow rome kyng arthour bretaigne freely hold shal hold ad rome hasteli yeue truage axen truage constatyne eleynes sone emperour rome ad honour ther longed maxymian kyng conquered frauce almaigne passed mounth yoye conquered lu bardye ad thyse two myne auncestres helden j shal haue thurgh goddes wylle ye reuerence arthur dyd emperours messagiers rome capit lxxxij whan lre made ensealed kyg arthur messagiers yafe grete yeftes ad messagiers toke hyr leue went thes came court rome ayeu tolde emperour worthely vnderfonge whyche ryalle copanye serue hi rialli seruid tha ye eour kyng lyuing worlde whan emperour seyne lettre herde thery saw arthur wolde ruled aftyr hym let asseble ordeyne hugh host destroye kyng arthur myght kyg arthur touchyg power partye ordeyned power knightes rownde table pof kynges lordes came helpe kyng arthur ayest emour ca lxxxiij king scotlad irlad gutlad de marke almaign euery men duc normadye gascoyne flaudres pehyto boloygne iiij gery chartres x hoell bretaign xij hym self hys owne lad xij alebrestriers archiers othir folk foot cowde nobre whe alle redy wente thene kyng arthour toke hys lad gunnore wyf kepe one hys neuews wy knyght hardy kalled mordred trewe ye shal afterward kyg arthur toke reaulme mordred sauf onely ye croune ad kyg arthur nome hys hoost wet southampto shippes brought folk assembled dyde see good wynd wether wille ad also sone myght arriued harfleet went hir shippes spradden contre kyg arthour fought wyt geaute spaigne called dynabus queld eleyne kyng hoelles cosyn lyttel bretaigne cap lxxxiiij kyg arthur dwelled contre littel men ne tolde hym comen grete geaut spaigne rauisshed ye fair eleyne cosin hoell bretaigne brought hir vpon hyll kalled moute seyt bernard ther man cotre bolde ne hardy durst wt fight ner come nere place geaunt dwelled called dinab moche sorwe dyd contre wha king arthour herde tyding kalled key bedewere commauded hem go preuely ad espie wher geant might fonden camen riuage ther men sholde gon ye mounte enclosed aboute water yet euer shall saw brenyg fire vpon hylle ther also othir hille nye thervpo othir fire brening key bedewere camen next hille fonde widewe opehede sittyg besides tobe sore wepyg grete sorwe made ofte said eleyne eleyne key bedewere ed hir wherfor made moche sorwe lay ye tobe said sorwe misaueture faire lordes seke ye geant may yowe finde ye worth anone dede bene stille good wyfe sayd therof dysmay ye telle v soth thou makest moch sorwe wepyg syres said damisell yt norisshed wt brest called eleyne yt nece hoell kyg bretaigne lyeth ye bodi yt betake norissh ther came deuel geat rauisshed hir also lad v way wolde haue forlain maide yt yoge tedre age might suffre grete hugh ye geat punctel come woned certis wil quelle therfore fast wet ye ne wherfor said go ye henes certis sire said eleyne dede geant made abide haute must nedes suffre god wote good leuer dede hy dele moche payne haue wha forlyeth whan key bedewere herde al woma tolde turned ayen came kyg arthour tolde hym seyne herde arthour anone toke loth wete preuely bi night none hoost wist came moru erly geant faught wyt hy strogely laste slowe hy arthur bad bedewere smyte hys heed bryg ye hoost shewe hem wonder grete hugh wha camen ayen ye hoost tolde wherfor ben owte shewed hem heed ad euery man glad ad joyefull worthy dede ye kyng arthur done hir lord ad hoell full sorwefull hys nece loste aft wha space let make fayre chapelle lady ouer eleyns tombe phow kyng arthour yafe bataille emperour bataill emperour slayne capit lxxxv arthour ad peple tydyg emperour assembled grete power wel sarazis paynyms crysten men wher nombre lxxx hors men fote men arthour peple ordeyned fast forth hyr way toward ye emperour passed normadye frauce vnto bourgoigne wold euen haue gon hoost men tolde hy emperours host wold come lucie emperour ad hoost begynyg august remeved fro rome cam forth ye right way ward ye hoost kig arthur espyes comen sayde yf arthur wolde shold fynde ther fast emperour thei said emperour grete power wt hy kynges lade paynyms ynfere ad also criste peple nere grete folye kig arthur mete wyt hy espies tolde emour v men vi ayens owne hyse king arthour bolde hardy thyng hym dismayed ad sayd gowe boldely goddes name ayes romays wt hy lede sarasins paynyms maner trust haue god oneli vpon hyr stregth gowe sech hem sharpely ye name almyghty god slewe paynyms cryste men ben destroye criste men god shal v helpe haue right ad therfore haue trust god ye enemyes cristendome god mowe dede destroied ad men mowe recorde worthynesse knygthode wha kyg arthour th said cryed hygh voys god fader almighty wurshipped thy name withouten end ame grau te v grace well destroye enemy ben ayest crystendome name fadre sone holy gost amen god yeue hy neuer grace ne worship world ne mercy haue day shal feynte wel smyte egrely roden softely ordeyned wyges wel wisely emperour herd telle kig arthur ad folke redy arayed fight wyt hy thydder came ordeyned hys wyges best maner might ad trust vpo strengthe tha god almyghty sey afterward wha ye two hoostes mette gedre emperour lost moch folk also dyd kig arthur many slayn well one side othir grete pyte se wit jn bataill slayne thurgh king arthur v kyges paynys othir woder moche peple kig arthures men foughte wel romais ad paynyms stregthe withstonde tha xx shepes ayes v wolfe befell batayll wonder hard longe duryg owne syde ye emperour amonge slaine wist soth hy slowe kyng arthour let enburie knyghtes lost bataill ad set emperours body rome slayne bataille capitulo lxxxvi whan romays wist yt emperour dede thei forsoke felde paynys also kyg arthur chaced till night ad many queld wonder telie tho turned kyg arthour aye tho night ad thaked god victorye ye morne let loke see felde knightes loste say burel erle maut bedewere kay ligiers erle boloign vrtegj erle baar aloth erle wychestre cursale erle chestre holde erle flaudres thees ye grete lordes king arthour lost bataille amonge grete knyghtes ad let entier abbeyes bi contre somme let borne hyr owne co tre ad emptrours body let take put vpon beer ad sent rome set saye romains bretaigne frau ce whiche helde othir truage wold non pay axed hy othir truage right suche truage wold paye king let bere key kene owne castel entered ligier borne boloigne ther lord ad holden borne flaundres ther entered alle let entiere mochel honour abbeyes howses religyo ye contre ther dede arthour selfe soiourned yere bourgoigne wyt hoost ad thought yere folewyng passe ye mounthe ioye haue gone rome take cyte haue put romayns subiectyon wykked tyraunt mordred hy lete ye shall phow mordred traytour kyng arthour toke hys land kepe hys castelles ad helde ayenst hym capitulo lxxxvij whan king arthour taken mordred reaulme kepe gon ayens emperour rome ad passed see mordred anone toke homage feautes hem lade wolde haue lade owne vse toke castelles aboute ad let araye falsenesse dyd grete wroge ayens lawe cristedom toke hys owne emes wyfe traitour shold ordeyned hym grete hoost ayest arthur comig holde lade ayenst hy wt stregth euermore slee kyg arthur yf might send see land lette assemble painyms crysten peple send saxones danoys helpe hym also mordred set cheldryck done men come hy owte saxoyne worthy duke promysed hym brought hy moch peple wold graute bretaigne euermore ye lad fro beyode humber vn scotlad lande engist vortigers yift whe spoused hys doughtyr cheldryk came grete stregth power peple mordred asse bled also halfe xlm stronge knightes nede phow arthour enchased mordred traitour ad slayne also kyng arthour wounded deth capitulo lxxxviij whan thys tydynge came kyg arthur ther burgoyne full sore anoyed ad toke alle frauce hoell kepe wyt halnedel men prayed hy wolde kepe tyl came ayen selfe wolde went bretaigne auenge vpon mordred traitour forth went hys way ad came wytsand made hys men gone shippes hy self wolde haue arryued sadewith brought hy host frau ce also owne lade er might come lande hys peple come oute shippes mordred comen wyt alle power yafe stroge bataille kyg arthur lost many man er might come londe gawe nevew slayne anguysshel helde scotland many wherof kyng arthour full sory comen land mordred might ayest hem endure anon discofyted fledde thes nyght hys men vpon morne cam londo cyte wold suffre hy come fro then fled wynchestre ther helde hym peple hy came kyng arthour let take body gawen cosyn ad body anguissell let borne scotlat hyr owne contre entered anon kyg arthur toke wey destroie mordred fled fro thes ito cornewaill quene gumore yt kyg arthours wyf tho soiourned yorke punctel herd yt mordred fled thes might endure ayens kyg arthur sore adrad grete doubte wist best done wist wel hir lord kyg arthur wold neuer hir haue mercy grete shame toke hir way preuely iiij men withoute mo came katlione dwelled hir lyfe neuer seyne amonge folke hyr lyfe duryg arthur wist mordred fledde cornewaill let sent men scotlad northuberlad vn hubar let asseble folk withoute nobre camen fro thes cornewaill seche purswe mordred mordred assebled hy alle folk cornewaille peple without nobre wyst arthur comyg ad leuer deye take chause tha ferther flee abode yaf hard bataille king arthour peple moch peple slayne half ad othir wiste better partie befell last morded slayne folke ad good cheualrie king arthour gadred norysshed dyuerse la de also noble knyghtes roude table moche preysed thurgh owt alle world slayne arthour selfe wounded deth let hy borne lytier surgye heled woundes yet bretos suppose lyued othir lad shall come yet conquere bretaign certes proposicye merlyn sayd deth shall doubtous sayd soth men ther yet haue doubte shulle euer men saith men wyt whether lyueth dede arthur borne auyone xxij yere regne incarnacyon owr lord ihesu crist vc xlvi yere king arthour delyuered royaulme constantyn ye sone cador nephew capitulo lxxxix whan kyng arthour wyst myght lenger regne let come beforne hy constatyne cadors sone erle cornewaill cosy hy betoke reaulme said bad therof kyg tyll came ayen asmoch non heir body begoten grete harm noble king doubty child bodi begote alle thyg god wyl haue must who name blesshed withoute ende ame kyg constatyne werred mordredes two sone capitulo xc thys constatyne noble knight worthy body ye ij sone mordred begoten grete enuye costatine tho crowned king begonne mene werre ayens hy punctel asse bled grete hoost fore mordred bene dryuen away dyde moche sorwe thurgh land one brother ordeyned lo take cyte winchestre costatyne came london slew hy wet wychestre slow hy also enemy dede wha costatine regned iiij yere deyed lyeth lodo kyges adelbright ad edelf ca xcj affter kyg costatines deth ther ij kyges bretaigne one called adelbright danoys helde cotre northfolk south fol othir hight edel breto punctel helde nychol lydesey ye land vnto hubar thise ij kyges fast werred gydre accorded loued gedre borne owne body kig edel sustre kalled orewe ne yafe hir thurgh grete fredshyp king adelbright wyfe begate hir doughter kalled argentyll ye thridde yere came vpo hym stronge sekenesse nedes must deye sent kyng edelf brother lawe shold come speke hym cam wyt good tho prayed king ad coniured also name god dede shold take arge tyl doughtyr lade kept hyr well norisshe hyr hys chambre wha age shold maryed strogiest worthiest man might fynde shold yelde vp hyr sad ayene edel grau ted othe confermed hys prayer whan adelbryght dede entered edell toke damysell argentil norisshed hir chambre became fayrest creature myght lyue man fynde kyng edel maried damysell knaue kychene capitulo xcij kig edell vncle damysel argentill bethought howe might falsely haue ye land nece euermore falsely ayest othe thought deceyue damisell marye hyr knaue hys kyche kalled curan bicame ye worthiest strengist man bodi man wyst lande tho lyued hym thought hyr shenfully haue maryed haue hir lad afterward clene deceyuyd cura hauelockes sone king kyrkelane denmarke curan conquered wyfes lad slewe kig edelf wife vncle hyr land othir place telled openly regned thre yere saxon danoys hy kylled grete harme bretaigne breton bare stonhenge hy enburyed wt mochel honour pof kyng conam ca xciij thys curan regned conam cosyn wonder prowde knight regned coude haue maner loue euer medelyg peple ad toke vncle wt werre quelled ij child saxones werred ayenst ofte time ouercame last pee lyfes tyme regned xiiij yere deyed lyeth london pof kyng cortyfad gurmo de came thurgh paynys bretaigne cap xciiij conam regned ye lad saxos ye afterward shal tyme paynym yt called gurmod ye kyges sone dauffrykes paynys folke reaulme fadre kyg sauf bequath yave brother said neuer sholde kig might gete ad conquere reaulme strauge cotre bold right stroge bodi hy profecyed merlyn said shold wolfe see let asse ble paynyms withoute nobre ad let appareill shippes ad went many londes toke homage ad feautes many went see conbuered many dyuerse lades came jrlad coquered lad oftentymes werryd vpo bretos breton vpo hem ofte wone ofte losten ad yaue hostage bretos thei sente gurmonde ther irlad shold come bretaign helpe ayest ye bretos helpe hem delyuer land wolde gladly holde hir lord paynyme also paynyms ye bretos criste wel ought helpe one lawe wha gurmod herd prayer hasted hy moche might arryued scotland came northuberlad saxon dwel yg ad cofermed couenauts bitwene hem made bi othes hostage bere hy trewe fayth holde hy lorde paye truage yere tho began saxon affrycas destroye robbe brene townes destroye thing asmoch myght spared nethir man woman ne childe lered ne lewde alle quelled cast downe townes castelles ad chirches put ye lad grete destructyon alle thei might fleen punctel fledde then well palione bisshop called paulyn made prymat ad erchebisshop englad yaf hi power make ordeyne bisshoppes land ad anone augustyn pallione dignite erchibisshoppe made ij bisshoppes hys felaws came hy fro turned god seyt augustyn went land breton kepe fro englisshme seyne jn wale fonde moke abbeyes vij bisshoppes breton desyred allway crysten peple seint augustyn couerted said bisshoppes legat rome pmat england shold alle reson obedyent wyt englysshemen saide nolde erchibysshop carlyon ad said nold neuer maner thyng ben obedyet englisshme ye englisshmen sayd ben aduersaires enemyes haue dryue v owt owne contre ben cristen men euer haue ben englisshmen haue euer ben paynys nowe late ben conuerted seint augustyn might none answere haue otherwyse sayde ately nold neuer hem obeye hy ne pope rome seit augustyn turned ayen ye kyng adelbright king ket told hy thys folk wold man obedyet erchebisshop karlyon whan kig herde sore annoyed said wold destroye sent olfride kyg northuberland hys frend shold come hym wyt alle power might shold mete hy leicestre punctel ad thes wold gon wale destroye erchebisshop carlyon refused seynt augustin kyng adelbright kyg olfride queld brecmale kyng breton helde contre leicestre capi xcix hit befel ther king breton helde contre leicestre contre aboute named brecmale breton herde telle two englysshe kynges wold mete ther leicestre wente walys let ordeyne power fight thees two kyges lyttell avaylled folk slayne self fled lost landes euermore two kynges adelbright olfryd dwelled whyle leicestre departed landes amoges token homage feautes folk contre ther wente ward wale wale herd telle ye discomfyture brecmale hath leicestre wonder ore adrad two kynges ad anone chose amonges hem good men holy heremytes mo kes prestres ad othir folk grete plente wenten baarfoot wollwerd haue mercy two kynges ky ge sterne wikked old neuer speke wyth hem queld hem euericho allas sorowe ne spared nomore wolf doth shepes punctel smote hedes euerychon alle martred hem camen vndersto de v hodred xl afterward two kynges went fro thes bangore quelle alle might fynde ye breton whan bretos herde assembled ordeyned hir power fight wyt hem tho baro wale called bledrik cornewaill som tyme lord denoushyre ye kyg adelbright driuen wale yeue bataille bataill kyg aldelbright slayne eldryf wounded sore forsoke felde part peple slayn eldrif fled northuberland owne land afterward ye peple leycestre shire made stregthe cadewan brecynalis sone kyng leicestre regned nobely grete honour phow cadewan kyng leicestre elfryd king nortu berland frendes debate afterward bitwene edwyn cadwaly bothe hyr sone capit c bataill breton assembled hem went camen vnto leicestre made cadwa brecinalis sone kig leicestre contre ad toke homage feautes folk contre assembled grete hoost said wolde gone northu berland destroye kyng elfrid slee yf might wha comen thydder frendes went bitwene hem made accorded manere elfryd shold hold alle londe fro hubar vnto scotland cadewa shold haue alle land syde huber vnto south punctel became good frendes hys lyfes duryng ad loued gedre two brethre elfride sone kalled edwyn ad held lad northuberlad fadres deth fader holde hys lyfes time cadewa sone called cadwalyn helde fadres lad helde whyles lyfe ad loued gedre bretheren loue last bitwene onely two yere began debate bitwen lyther enuyous cosin cadwalyne yt called bryeny thei assembled grete host partyes ye last befell cadwalyn discomfited edwy pursued drofe fro place place last fley irlad destroyed land kast downe castelles bret maners departed cadwalyns land amoge hys frendes long tyme came cadwalyn ayen irland wt strog power plaine bataill quelled edwyne fredshippes nameli thaym witheld lades thurgh edwynes yefte phow king oswald queld thurgh kyg cadwalyn peanda oswy seit oswaldes brother regned queld peanda capitulo cj whan edwyne slaine offris sone vndertoke werre ayenst cadwalyn eme offrys deyde duryng werre deth offrys tho regned gentill cristen man moche loued god almighty land northuberlad herytage called oswold kyg lad moche frend edwyne helde grete part land cadwaly cadwaly werred vpon hy drofe hy toward scotland whe cadwaly sawe wold ferther hym purswe toke somme folke peada brother lawe ad praied purswe oswald tyll take slayne cadwaly turned home ayene whan oswald herd tydyng cadwalyn turned hom ayen wold le ger flee abode peada yafe bataille peada discomfyted fled ad came ayen cadwaly said wold neuer holde ony foot lond hy wold aue ge oswold cadwalyn let assemble grete hoost fight oswold peada came vnto northuberlad yaue bataill vnto oswold bataille oswold slayne hede smyte etered abbey bardeney whyche place god hath wrought many fayr myracle ther elles anone oswy brother seised hys lad oswaldes folck northuberland loued wonder wel helde hyr lord men hys kyn worthy ynough wold haue departed lod werred gedre ad moche nat strog ynough came peada prayed helpe socour ad promysed lod largely vpon couenant wolde gyde help counceill pea da herd hyre prayer spake king cadwalyn shold ordeyne grete hoost ad fast ordeyn northuberland fighte oswy ad oswy meke man moche loued pee charyte prayed peanda loue pee proferd gold syluer grete plei te peada proud nolde graunte hym pee maner thig thig wold wyt hy fighte ye laste ther set day bataill oswyne trust vpon god peanda trustyd vpon pryd vpon hoost gedre smoten egrely peanda anone discomfited slayne ye jncarnacyon lord ihesu crist vjc lv yere oswyn regned tho xxviij yere ad king called oswyn peanda cosyn werred vpo kyng oswy foughten gedre oswy victorie oswy discomfyted slaine lyeth tenemouth kyng cadewaldre yt cadewaleynes sone regned aftir fadre laste kyng breton capitulo cij deth cadwaley regned hys sone cadwaladre well nobely moder suster kyng peanda whan regned xij yere fell grete sekenesse thene grete discord bytwene ye lordes land euery weried vpon othir yet tyme ther fell grete derth scarcite corne vytailles thys nd man might goo thre day iiij fro towne towne yt shold nat fynde bye gold ne syluer brede wyne ne none othir vytaille wher man myght lyue onely peple lyued bi rote herbes othir lyuyng none moche failled aboute fisshes wilde bestes alle thyg yet thys mysauenture ther fell grete mortalite pestilence amonge peple corrupcyon eir lyuyg peple ne suffysed burye ye dede body deyde sodeli grete smale lord ad seruaunt etyng goyng spekyng neuer herd sodeyne deth among peple wende gou burie dede body wyt dede body buried yt might flee fledde forsoke hir lo de house wel grete huger scarcite corn vitailles ye horrible mortalite pestilece lad wente othir lades saue hir liues left ye lad desert wast yt ther man trauaille tille ye lod ne ere ne sowe ye land bareyne cornes othir fruites defaulte tiliers thys mysauenture dured xj yere moo man myght ere ne sowe phow cadwaldre went owt land littel bretaigne cadwaladre saw grete hunger mortalite pestilence lond poure faylling cornes othir vitailles folke perisshed saw also moost partie hys lad wasted voide peple appareilled hem folke left lyue passed ouer lyttel bretaigne wyt littel nauye vnto kig alayne moche loued cosyn fadre moche loued time sailled see made grete lame tacyo dyde sayde dedisti no dne tan quam oues escarum getib dispersisti no began cadwaldre copleyne folke pytously said allas said v wrecches caytyfs punctel owr grete synes wolde amende v whyle space repetaunce come vpo v mysauenture chaceth v oute owne reaulm propre soyle fro owt whiche somtime romains scottes saxon ne dane might exilen v avaylleth nowe v tyme oft fithes haue gote many othir la de sith wylle god abyde dwelle owr owne lande god werray jugge alle thyg knoweth done made sech wolde cese owr sy ne ad enemy ne myght v ne lignage exylen fro reaulme wolde amend v folyes ad sene propr defaultes therfore shewed v wrath wull chastise v mysdedes sith v doth without bataill strength enemyes bi grete copanyes wrecchedly leue owre owne reaulme propre land turne agayn ye romains turne agayn ye scottes turne agayn ye sa o turne agayn ye fraunsoys sheweth bretaygne desert whiche power myght neuer make desert ne yet yowre power hath put v exill onely power ye king almyghty haue ofte offended bi folyes whyche wolde leue vnto ye tyme tyll chastised v bi dyuy power amoge wordes lametacion kyng cadwaladre made folk thei arryued littell bretaigne came ye king alayne said king receyued wyt ioye made hi serued wondre nobely dwelled longe time eglissh peple lefte lyue escaped grete huger mortalite lyued best wyse might moche peple spronge came hem sent saxoyn borne hir fre de men woman childre restore ye cytees peple othir tounes voide peple trauailie telle erthe whan saxon herden tyding thei camen land wondre thikke grete companye logged ad herberwed hem self ye cotre wolden fonde man hem lette ne withstonde woxen multiplied gretly vsed customes contrees wher thei come lawes langages hir owne land changed name cytees townes castelles burghes yaf hem name called hem thei apparailen hy take hys way viage lande prayed god almyghty deuoutly wolde make hy demonstracyon yf yt hys prayer land plesauce none agayn wyl god almyghty wolde thyg wha thus deuoutly made prayer voys fro heue said bad hy leue iourney way englond ad shold go pope rome wylle almighty god breton shulde nomore regne bretaigne ne neuer recoure land vnto ye tyme prophecye merlyn sayd fullylled sholde demarke yt called rafyg iiij erles grete power day ye danoys shame thei driuen vnto englisfelde ad xv day danoys englisshme foughte othir tyme rafyg englisshmen discofyted then danoys called roynt wet well land pee thys kyng edgar lord kyng aboue kynges scotland walys tyme arthour gone neuer sithe kyng hys power noble kig edgar seyt edwardes fadre wha edgares wyfe dede yt seint edwardes moder
