onely hir saw edelwold faire yonge knight worthy ryche wel kyg thought doughter shold wel maryed wel beset vpon hy grauted hy doughter yf good lord kyg wold sente ther edelwold came ayen king told hy fair ynowe vpon see wo der lothly tho answered kig said toke littel charge syre said edelwold tho hir fadres heir nat rych landes ye wold consente graute must hir haue tha shold j rych ynowe goddes name sayd king cosent ther edelwold thanked tho moch king went ayen dene shire spoused ye damisell contre dwelled th befel vpon tyme tolde counseyll thing vnto wyfe howe maner begylled lord ye kig wolde haue hir wyfe ad anone wist loued hy neuer afterward beforne lady conceyued sone whan tyme child shold borne edelwold came king prayed haue sone fouston kig hy grau ted let calle hym edgar aftir owne name whan thought yt sure ynowe ye king shuld take wyfe asmoch lord ioly man amerous phow kyng edgar wedded fayre estrylde deth edelwold yt edelwold deyed capitulo centesimo xiij th befell alle men kyng edgarys court tho speken saiden thys knyght edelwold rychely auawnced thurgh mariage wyf yet thei said avauced ho derfeld spoused fayrest woma euer seyne kyng herde speke somoch hir beaute thought edelwold hy deceyued begylled thought preuely hert wold gone deneshire hu te hert hynde ad othir wilde bestes sholde se lady er departed thenes lady dwellyg maner besides forest king wold hunte ye maner herburwed al ye night wha tyme came king shold sope axed gossyp godsone edelwold made hyr come kyg notheles myght haue bene sholde haue comen hys sighte wyll lady welcomed king swetely kissed toke hir hande tho next hy sette soped gedre tho custome vsage thys land whan man dronke vnto othir punctel drynker shold sey wassaill othir shold answere drynkehaille thus dyd kyg lady many tymes also kyst ech othir sope wha tyme gone bedde kyg wete vnto bed hertely thykyg vpo lady fairnesse tho ouercomen hir loue thought shold deye wyll hyr vpon morne kyng aroos wet forest disporte hertes hyndes alle wilde bestes hertes grete plente ladi sent ofte wente solacen speken ladj while dwelled cotre ye kyg remeved thenes thought myght best delyuer edelwold wyfe hy fyrst deceyued king anone viij dayes let ordeine parlament salesbury hys baronage counceill haue ordeyne contree northuberland might best ben kept danoys camen ther destroye land edelwold came also vnto ky ge parlamet king sent hi yorke keper cotre thus befel men knewe hym slowe hy wey anone kyng herde dede let sende lady estryld shold come cyte londo ben wedded kyg grete solempnite worship held solempne fest weryd crowne golde ad quene weryd also othir seint dunston morwe came vnto king chambre fonde kyng bedde ad quene also ynfere seit dunston axed king answerde quene estrilde erchebisshop seint dunsto said grete wrong ayenst goddes wylle take woman wyfe who child take foustoun quene word neuer loued seynt dunston notheles good man warned thaim foly lete warnyg availled littell ye loue bitwene hem moch king begate vpon woman sone kalled eldred tho chylde vi yere olde kyng hys fadre deyed ye time regned xvij yere lyeth glastenbury seynt edward martyr estrild hys stepmoder lete hym quelle make eldred hyr owne sone kyng capitulo centesimo xiiij edgard regned edward sone begote first wyfe wel nobely gouerned lande full alle maner goodnesse lad full holy lyfe aboue alle thig loued good holy chyrche quene estrild hys stepmoder let hym slee encheso make hir owne sone eldred king thus slayne afterward ye shull hit befell th daye kyng edward went wode playe south contre besides towne kalled warham forest grete plente hertes hydes ben hym pleye thought vpon brother eldred whiche moder quene place nigh forest thought gon thydder visite ad see brother toke hy lyttel meyne went hy tho toward stepmoders house time soiourned ye castel corfe ad rode thikkenesse wode aspie hys game jt befell went amys ad lost meyne came last came owte wode thene loked aboute sawe ther fast besides maner stepmoder dwelled ad thyddderward went allon anon told ye quene edward kyng comen allone wythoute companye therfor made yoye ynowe thought hys mynde might slain preuely myght anone preuelich called hir one knightes told moche hir couseill bitwen hem camen ye kig ad courtously receyued king told comen hir visite also speke wyt eldred brother quene many tymes thanked hy prayed wold abyde wyt hir night kyng saide myght ayene wolde wente vnto folke might hem fynde whan quene sawe wold nat abyde praied hy wold one drinke graunted hir anon drinke came quene dranke vnto kyg kig toke ye cuppe set mouth mene tyme while yt dranke knight wt quene knife smote eue king vnto herte fyll downe dede hys palfray vnto erthe quene dede yaf knight gold syluer grete plente othir richesse ynowe knight anon thys wente hy ouer see escaped oute land whan kyng edward thus martred hit ye yere jncarnacyo lord iesu crist ix clxxx yere regned xij yere halfe lyeth glastenbury king eldred ye kig swyne denmarke helde englond eldred seint edwardes brother nat beloued reaulme therfore fledde normadie capitulo centesio xv king edward regned eldred brother seynt dunston crouned hym king seynt dunsto dyed sone afterward foryeue quene hir trespace estrild echeso cause king edward deth ad seyt dunston hir assoyled ad penaunce hir enioyned yued chaste lyf clene kyg eldred wedded englissh woman ad hir begate edmond irenside ad othir sone called edwyne deyed quene hir modre tyme came englad swyn king de marke chalenge conquer hys auncestres tyme conquered yg good erle cutbert lyndes peple northu berland ad moost grete lordes england helde wyth swyne kyng denmark moch loued kyg eldred encheson hys good brother edward slayne falsely encheson hy therfore man sette littel wherfore kyng swyne wille toke alle land eldred king fledde tho normandie spake duke rychard duke yaf suster emma wyfe vpo whyche begate two sone one called alured othir edward wha swyn conquered lad regned nobely lyued xv yere deyed lyeth yorke phow king eldred came ayene normadye knoght danoys regned werre bitwene edmond ire side capitu cxvi deth swyne yt danoys knoght sone dwelled englod wolde haue kyg tho came ayen eldred oute normandye moche peple wt stro ge meyne knoght durst abyde fley then demarke kyg eldred ayen reaulme helde grete lordship began destroye thai helpen swyn danoys ayenst afterward came ayen knoght fro demarke grete power king eldred durst wyth fight fledde fro then london punctel ther helde tho came knoght besieged long tyll king eldred deyed ye cyte london lyeth seyt paulus regned ix iere kyng knoght cap cxvij deth thys eldred knoght danoys began tho regne edmond jrenside kig eldredis sone first wife ordeyned grete hoost began werre vpon king knoght dyd many tymes ofte werre stronge ad hard woder wyte quene eme dwelled tho westmynstre grete drede hir two sone ye werre alured edward lest thei shold defoilled misdone thurgh werre wher fore sente ouer see normadye ye duke rychard hir vncle ther dwelled saufte pee longe time thys edmond jrenside knoght werred strogely gedre last thei accorded maner thei shold depart reaulme bitwen dyde became good frendes wel loued became sworne brethere ad wel loued gedre bretheren geten body one modery borne king edmod jrenside traitoursly slayn thurgh traitour called edrick stratton capit cxviij tho regned kyg edmod irenside knoght danoys th befel afterward yere accorded ad moche loued gedre wherfor false thef traitour euye vnto loue bytwene frendship who name eldryk straton grete lord edmond jresides helde lade notheles thought betraie lord ad make knoght king land intent richely ben avauced hy wel beloued wherfore prayed hys lord edmond jrenside vpo day eten dwelle kyg courtously grauted came hys prayer mete king serued ryally dyuerse mete drinkes ad wha night came shold go bedde king toke owne meyne wente chabre loked aboute saw woder fayr jmage wel made semblant archier wyth bowe bent hond bowe fyne arwe kyg edmod went tho nerre beholde better might ben anon arwe smote thurgh bodi ther king slowe engyn made quelle owne lord traitoursly wha king edmond thus dede slain regned x yere peple made grete sorwe bodi bere vnto glastebury hy etered fals traitour edrik anone went ye quene king edmondes wyfe ye wist hir lordes deth anone nome hir hir two sone fayre yonge hir lord vpon hir gote owne called edward edwyne lad hem bothe hy lodo toke hem kyng knoght shold wyt wille tolde que tely quelled king edmond encheson loue hy kyg knoght englond hys power holy might haue po thow fals traitour hast thou trew brother slayn encheson man loued world hede shal thy trauaille rewarde well thow hast deserued anon let hy take byd ho de foot maner traitour let cast hi thamyse maner false traitour ended lyfe kyng nomme ye two child toke abbot westmynster warde kepe till wist best hem done kyng knoght sent kyng edmondes sone bothe denmarke flee saued capitulo cxix hit bebell sone afterward kyg knoght al lande hande spoused quene emme thurgh consent baronage fayre woman yt eldredis wyfe duke suster normandie leued gedre moche loue reson wolde king axed vpon day cou seyll quene best done wyt sone edmod iresides syr said right heires lad lyuen wyl doo moche sorwe werre ad therfore let sent hem straunge land ferre somme man may hem defoille destroie kig anone let calle danoys called walgar commau ded shold lede ij child denmarke ordeyn hem neuer herde moo tydinges hem syr said walgar gladly comau dement shall done toke two child led hem den marke ad moch saw two chyldren wonder faire also meke grete pyte routh wold slee led kyng hu gerj noryce walgar wel knowen kig ad wel beloued anone kyng axed whens chyldren walgare told ad said right heires englod ther men wold hem destroye therfore syr becomen mercy helpe seche soth mowe lyuen men shull becomen yow shull holde hir land kyng hungery hem vnderfenge mochel honour lete worthely kepte thus befell afterward edwyne yonge brother deyed edward elder drother liued fair man stronge large body getyl curtoys dicios men hy loued thys edward cronycles called amonges englisshmen edward oute lawe made knight kinges doughter hungery moche hy loued goodnesse ad fairnesse made called hym hyr derling kyng hir fadre perceyued wel loue bitwene two none heir doughter ad kyng vouched hys doughter man wel dyd hi loued hir yaf hir vnto hy ith good edward hir spoused moch honour king hongerye sent baronage made solempne fest ryche weddyng ad made men vnderstonde shold king wha dede therfor maden grete ioye tidinge full glad thys edward begate vpon lady sone yt called edgar belyng ad afterward doughtere called margarete aft er ward quene scotland king scotlad called mancholyn doughter called maude quene englond thurgh kyg henry first sone conquerour hir wedded ad begate hir doughtir yt called maude aft empresse almaigne maude came kyg englod vnto day kalled ry empress sone yet edward doughter bi wife kalled cristian nonne kyng knoght proude man conquered norwey became afterward meke milde capitulo cxx haue ye herde edmondes sone ire side kig knoght de bene dede commaunded walgare punctel knoght hys hand englond denmarke went norwey lad conquere kyng lande called elaf came peple wende lande well haue kept defended ad faught tyll last slayne bataille tho knoght nome land hys hande whan coquered norwey take feautes ad homage ther came ayen englod helde selfe grete lord hy thought world hys pere man became proude hauten grete wonder befel vpo day herd messe wesmynstre wolde haue gone palays wawes ye thamyse swyftely ayest came moost touched hys fette tho said kyg wt proude hert commaude water turne ayen elles shal make turne wawes commaundemet wold spare flowed ouer hye ad kig proude hert wold flee water abode stille water bete water smale yerde helde honde commaunded water sholde wete ferther al commaundement water wolde cese euer wax hyghe king vete stode ye water whan saw abyde ther log water wolde thing commaudement tho sone withdrowe hy tho stode vpon stone helde hondes high said wordes heryng peple god maketh see th aryse hygh king kinges mightes caytyf man dedely may neuer deye alle thing doth co maudement obediet ye god praye warrant knowelech caityf feble poer therfore wyll go rome wythoute lettyng wykkednesse punysshe amende god j clayme land hold non othir anon made redy heir selfe rome withoute lettyng ad bi waye dyd many almesse dedes came rome also wha ben synnes penaunce came ayen englod becam good man holy lefte alle maner pride stoutenesse liued holy lyfe lyfe made two abbey seyt benet owne englod norwey asmoch loued specyaly seint benet seintes moche loued also seint edmond kyng ofte yaf grete yeftes hows wherfor made rych whe regned xx yere deyed lyeth wynchestre pof kyng harold leuer gone fote tha ryde hors capitulo cxxi knoght haue spoke ij sone bi wife emme ye one kalled hardeknoght othir harold lyght fote kalled hy communely harolde harefoot harlod thyng condicions maner kyng knoght fadre sette littel pry cheualrye ne curtoisye nothir worship bi owne wyll became wykked exyled moder emme wente oute lad flaudres dwelled erle wherfore tyme neuer good loue bitwen brother hys brother hy hated dedely whan regned ij yere lyttel deyed lyeth westmynstre kyng hardeknoght haroldes brother capitulo cxxij harlot harefoot regned brother hardeknoght noble knight stronge ad worthy punctel moche loued cheualrie ad maner goodnesse whan hardeknoght regned littel let vncouer brother harold smite hede brother westmynster let cast ye hede gonge ye body thamise ad came fisshers toke body hyr nettes bi nyght bere hy seyt clementes chirch ther hy beried thys maner aueged hardeknoght brother none othir maner might auenged thys kyng hardeknoght large yeuer mete drike table sette euery day thre time full ryall mete drynkes hys owne meyne camen vnto court rychely serued ryall mete kyg hardeknoght sent eme moder made hir come ayen englod driue oute eglod while harlod harefoot regned thurgh couseyll erle godewyne tho gretest lord englod next king myght doo wold thurgh englond thurgh commaudemet moche spoused doughter good king knoght danoys whiche doughter bi first wyfe whe quene driuen englond came ye erle flau dres kalled baldwyne cosyn sonde hyr alle thyng hyr nedeth vnto ye tyme went ayen england ye king hardeknoght sent hir hir sone made hir come ayen wyt mochel honour kyng hardeknoght wha regned v yere deyed lyeth westmy stre bilonye ye danoys dyden englysshmen wherfor fro tyme danoys made king englod capitulo cxxiiij deth kyg hardeknoght moche thyg begoten body erles baron assembled made counceill neuer noma danoys though neuer grete man amoges shold neuer king englond ye despite yt ye danoys englisshme euer beforne hand ye englisshmen danoys hapete mete vpo brygge ye englisshme shold n hardy mene ne stere foot stand still till ye danois passed forth ouer gentyll englisshme bowyd doune hir hedes reuerence vnto danoys shold haue bene bet ad defouled ad suche maner despytes vilainye dyden danoys englisshme wherfore driuen oute land tyme kyg hardeknoght dede lord might maynten pin maner voyded danoys englod neuer came ayen erles baron hir commune assent ad counseill senten vnto normadye seche two brethere alured ad edward dwellyg duke rychard eme entet crowne alured elder brother hym make kig eglod thig make ende erles baron made hir oth erle godeweyne westsex falsely traitoursly thought slee two brethere anon shold come englond intet make sone harold kyng whiche sone begote vpon wyfe kig knoghtes doughter danoys ad godewyne preuely wet self southampto mette ye two brethere wha shold come lod th befell messagiers wet normadie fonde oneli alured yt ye elder brother edward brother gon hungerye speke wt hys cosyn edward oute lawe edmondes sone irenside messagiers told said alured erles baros englod sent hy boldely shold come englond vnderfenge reaulme punctel kig hardeknoght dede punctel alle danoys dryuen owt land godewyne fals traytour toke alured vpo g desdoune whan came fro normadie ben king englond dyd hym martred ile ely capit cxxiiij whan alured herde thys tydinge thanked god went shyp wyt hast might passed ye see arryued sowthapton ther godeweyne ye traitour tho traitour saw come welcomed hym ad vnderfeng hy wyth mochel ioye said wold lede hym london baron englod abode make king went hir wey toward lo whan camen vpo gyldesdoune tho said ye traitour godeweyne alured take kepe aboute yow lyfte side ye right side ye shul kyg hondred soth said alured j behote j king shal ordeyn make lawes wher god folk shall hold wel payed nowe traitour comau ded hys men wyt hy whan comen vpo gildesdone thei shold slee alureds companie came hy norma dye take alured lede hy ile ely ther put oute eyen hede afterward bring vnto deth dyde quelled copanie xij nombre gentil men comen wyt alured fro normandye toke alured lad hy ile ely put eyen owte hede kutte vp hys wombe toke vp ye chief boels put stake grounde ad ende boels ther fastned nedles jren prikked good child made go aboute stake till hys bowelles drawe owte deyed ther alured thurgh treson erle godewyne whan lordes englod herd wist alured shold haue ben king put vn ye deth thurgh fals traitour godwine woder wroth swore amo ge thay bi god bi hys holy name yt shold deye werse deth dyd edryk stratton betraied lord edmod jrenside wold haue put hy ye deth thef traytour fley thenes demarke ther helde iiij yere lost land englod pof seint edward cofessour aluredes brother king englod ca cxxv ad done baros englod senten othir tyme normadie edward shold comen england wyt mochel honour edward chyldehode loued almyghty god drad honeste clennesse lad lyfe hated ye synnes ye deth wha crouned anoynted wt ryall power foryate good maners codicions fyrst vsed ad foryate good custom maner honour ne non rychesse ne maner hyghnesse euer yafe hy goodnesse wel loued god al mekenesse loued god holy chirch passyng maner thyng poure men also hem loued helde thei ben owne brethere hem ofte yaf grete almesse good wylle pof first specialte god shewed seint edwardes loue lyfe capit cxxvi befel day wet chyrche westmynstre herde messe seynt iohan euagelist moche loued specialy seint iohan euangelist god lady dyd othir seynt cam hym pylgrym prayed loue god seynt iohan euangelist good yeue kyg preuely toke ry ge fynger perceyued yafe vnto pilgry vnderfenge went thenes thys kyg edward made good lawes englond yet ben moost holden merciable full pyte noma might erle godewyne came ayen englond ayene land afterward seint edward wedded doughter capitulo cxxvij whan erle godewyne dwellyng de marke mochel herde goodnesse kyng edward full mercy ad pyte ad thought wold go ayen englod seche haue grace hym might haue lad ayen pee arayed moch myght put toward see ad came englod lodo kyng tyme alle lordes englond helde parlament godewyne sent hem frendes ad moost grettest lordes land prayed sech kynges grace ad wold pee land graunte hys enemy ladden hy king seche grace anone king hy saw appelled treson deth alured brother wordes vnto hy said traitour godwyne yt appelle thow hast betraied slayn brother alured certes sir said godwyne saue grace pee lordship j neuer hy betraied ne slew therfore put reward court fair lordes sayd king ye bien liege erles baron land ben assembled full well ye haue herd appelle aswere also godwyne therfore j wyll ye award right erles baros tho drowe hem gedre done award bi hem selfe ad thei speke dyuersely amonges hem somme said neuer alience bi homage sermet seruyce ne lordshyp bytwene godwyne alured whyche thing might drawe last devised demed shold put kynges mercj gedres tho spake erle leuerich couetre good man god ye world told reso maner sayd erle godewyne best frended man englod king well might bene gain said withoute couceill godewyne alured neuer put deth wherfor award touching part hy self sone euery v xij erles ben frendes wente king charged moche gold syluer mowe bere bytwene handes praye kig foryeue euell erle godewyne ad receyue homage lad yelde ayen alle accorded vnto award came maner aboue said euery hem gold ad syluer moche might bere bitwene hyr handes king sayde ye forme maner hyr accord hir award king wolde nat hem gayn saye moche ordeined grau ted confermed erle godewyne accorded wyt king ayene land afterward bere hy wel wisely king loued wonder moch wyth hy full pryue within littel tyme kyg loued hy somoche spoused edwyne hys doughter made hir quene notheles king wife lyued euer chastite clenesse body withouthe flesshli dede doyg wyt wyfe ad qne also hir halfe lad holy lyfe ij yere ad deyed afterward kyg lyued lyfe withoute wyfe king yafe erledome oxenford harold edwynes sone made erle well beloued bothe fader pryue wyt kyg fadre sone might done thyg wold right ayest right wold thingh done maner man good trewe conscience therfore lord ihesu cryst grete specyall loue shewed kyng edward saw swyne kyng denmarke drenched see sacrament stode herd masse capitulo cxxviij befell vpo wythsoday kig edward herde masse grete chirche westmyster right leuacion ihesu cristes body ad gadred chirche ad came nere auter sacryge see king ho de lyft vpo hyghe grete laughter toke vp punctel wherfore alle aboute hy stode gretely wodred masse axed kynges laughter fayre lordes sayd kyg wyne yonger kyng denmarke came see hys power haue comen englod vpon v haue werred sawe hym ad alle folk drenched high see saw eleuacyo iesu cristes body bytwene prestes ho de ad therof moch ioye myghte nat laughter witholde erle leuerich besydes hym stod leuacyon openly sawe fourme brede turne lykenesse childe yoge toke vp ryght honde fyrst blessed king ad afterward erle erle anon turned hym toward ye kyg make see holy sighte tho said kyg syr erle quod see well ye see thanked god j haue honoured god sauuour vysibly ihesu cryst fourme who name blisshed worldes phow rynge seint edward yeue poure pilgry loue god seint ioha euangelist came ayen vnto kyg edward cap cxxix noble man seint edward regned viij yere ad thus befell vpo tyme beforne er deyed two englod gon holi land ad hadden done hir pilgremage goyg ayen hyr owne contre went wey mette pilgrime courtoisly hem sa ued axed hem land contre borne thei sayden englond tho axed kyg englond ad answered ad said good kig edward fair fredes tho said pylgrim ye come ayene contre praye yow ye wyll goo vnto ye kig edward ofte tymes grete myn name ofte tymes thanke grete curtosye hath nameli rynge yaf whe herd messe westmyster seynt johannes loue euagelist delyueryd tho ryg vnto two pilgrymes said j praye gone bere ring take king edward ad telle sent hym full rycher yefte wol hy yeue vpon xij daye shal come euer dwelle blisse withoute ende syr sayd pylgrimes man ben ye place yowr dwellyng fair frendes sayd iohan euangelist dwellyng wyth almyghty god kyng edward frede j loue speciali encheson hath euer liued cle nesse clene mayd praye yow message done haue said wha seint iohan euangelist th hem charged sodenly voyded owte hyr sight pthe pylgrimes tho thanked almighty god went forth hyr way wha gon two thre myles begonne wex wery ad sate downe rest fyll slepe wha slept well one hem awoke lyfte vp hede loked aboute said vnto hys felawe aryse vp lete v go waye sayd one felawe othir wher certes said semeth cotre laid v reste slepe jherusalem thre mile nommen vp hir hondes blissed hem went forth hyr waye ad went hyr way thei sawe shepeherdes goyg hyr shep spaken none othir langage englissh leue frendes said one pylgrimes contre ad lord therof one shepeherdes aswered contre ket englond ad whych good kyng edward lord pylgrimes thaked god almyghti seint iohan euangelist went forth hyr waye ad came canterbury fro then london founden kyng edward tolde hym fro begynnyng vnto ende moche seint ioha hem charged alle thi ge spedde way toke ryng ye kyng edward vnderferdeng ad thanked god almighty seint iohan euangelist tho made hym redy day day wente owte lyfe whe god wold hym sende phow seint edward deyed xij daye capitulo cxxx befell thus cristesmasse eue holy man edward goddes seruyce matynes hygh feste punctel becam ful seke morwe endured moche payne masse let hym lad hys chambre ther reste hym halle amonges baron ad knightes might come hem co fort solace wonet done worthy fest wher hir myrth comfort amo ge hem hall turned care sorwe encheson dred lese hir good lord kyg vpo seint johannes day ewagelist tho came next ye king vnderfege ryghtes holy chirch falleth euery cristen man abode mercy god tho let two pilgrimes come yaf hem rich yeftes betoke hem vnto god also abbot westmynster let hy come toke hy ryge honour god seyt marie seint ioha euagelist abbot toke put among reliques westmynstre punctel euer shal lay king sike till xij eue tho deyed ye good king edward westmynstre ad ther lyeth who loue god hath shewed many fair myracles thys yere incarnacio lord ihesu crist mlxv yere translated put shryne thrugh ye noble martyr seint thomas caterbury harolde godewynes sone made king ad scaped fro duke bretaigne capi cxxxi whan seint edward gone oute world gone god ad worthe entered aperteigned suche lord baros lad wold haue edward heling sone edward oute lawe edmodes ire side sone king asmoche kyndest kynges blode reaulme haroldes sone thurgh erle godewine strength fader godewyne thurgh othir grete lordes reaulme kyn vnto hy sybbe seised englond hande anone let croune forsaid harold king enterement seyt edward king harold godewynes sone seconde yere seynt edward dede wolde haue gone flaundres dryuen thurgh tepest see co tre pountyfe taken brought duke wiyllyam normadye harold wende tho duke william wolde haue ben auenged vpon hym encheson erle godewyne whyche harold fadre let quelle alured seint edwardes brother prycipaly encheson ye forsaid alured quene emmes sone rychardys moder duk normandye ayell ye duk william notheles whan ye duk william harold pryson vnder power moch harold noble knight wyse worthy body fadre accorded ye good king edward therfore wolde misdone hym maner thinges bitwene spoke ordeyned harolde bi good wille swore vpo boke vpon holy saytes sholde spouse wedde duke wylliams doughter deth seint edward shold besyly done dever kepe ad saue reaulme englod profyte avauntage duck wylliam wha harold thus made oth vnto duk william let go yafe hym many riche yeftes ad tho wet thenes came eglod anone dyd thys maner wha seynt edward dede falsely forswore let croune hy kig englod falsely brak couenant made wt duke william wherfore duke wonder wroth ad swore wolde vpo ben aueged euer might come therof anon duk william let asseble grete hoost came englod auege hy vpon harold conquere ye lad might yere harold crouned harolde harestrege kyng denmarke arryued scotlad thought haue ben king englod came tho englod quelled robbed destroyed might tyll cam yorke ther quelled many armes thousand c prestes wha tidyge came king assembled strog power went fight wyt harold demarke wyt owne hod hy quelled danoys disco fyted ad tho left lyue moch sorwe fledde thes hir shippes thus kyg harold englod quelled kyng harold demarke phow willia bastard duke normadye came englod quelled kyg harold capitulo cxxxij wha bataill done harold became proud wold thing wt peple thyng goten held toward self wherfore moost partie peple wroth fro hy departed yt wt hy left mo soudyours vpon day sate mete messagier came hy ad sayd william bastard duke normadye arryued englond grete hoost taken al lad aboute hastynge also myned castell wha kig herd tydinge went thidder wyt lyttell peple wt hast might littel peple wt left whan cam thidder ordeyned yeue bataille duke william duk axed iij thinges wold haue doughter wyfe made swore othe ad behight wold holde land hy truage wold determine thig thurgh bataill harold proude stoute ad trustyd wonder moche vpon hys strength faught duke hys peple harold men discomfyted bataill ad self ther slayne ad thys bataille ended tonbrigge seconde yere hys regne vpon seint calixtes day lyeth waltha kyng william bastard gouerned well wysely werre bitwene ad king frauce ca cxxxiij wha william bastard duke normandye co quered land vpon cristmasse day tho next swynge let croune hi king westmy ster worthy king yaf englisshmen largeli lode knightes afterward went ouer see cam normadie ther dwelled whyle secode yere regne came ayen englond brought wyt maude wyfe ad let croune hir quene englond withsonday tho anone ye kig scotlad called mancoly began strife werre wyt duke william king willia ordeyned hy toward scotland men bothe bi land see destroye kyng mancoly accorded kyg scotland became man helde lad kyg william receyued homage came ayen englod whan king william king xvij yere maude quene deyed king william begoten many fair child seyne robert curthuse willyam le rous rychard also whiche deyde hery beauclerk ad maude also whiche ye erles wyfe boleynes othir foure doughteres wyfes deth began ther grete debate bytwen hy kyng frauce philippe last thei accorded tho dwelled kyng englod lad normadye man werred also vpon man longe tyme king fraunce said vpon day skorne kyng wylliam king wylliam longe tyme lyued chilhed longe time rested hy thys worde came kyng englond ther lay normadye rouen ad word euyll payd ryght wroth toward kinge fraunce swore god whan aryse gysin wold lyghte thowsand candeles kyg fraunce anone let assemble grete hoost normandye also englysshmen ad begynnyng heruest came frauce brend townes ther came thurgh cotre robbed ad dyd euell might thurghoute fraunce laste brede cyte do commaunded peple bere strawe moche might brenne hy self helpe therto might wyt good wylle grete hete fyre whiche grete ad ye sunne yt tho wonder hoot stuffed hy selfe became felle grete sekenesse whan sawe stronge seke ordeyned assygned norma dye vnto robert curthous hys sone englond william rous bequath henry beauclerk tresour tho thus done vnderfenge sacramets holy chyrche ad deyde xxij yere hys regne ad lyeth caan normandye pof kyng wylliam rous wyllia bastardes sone destroyed townes house religyon make newe forest capitulo cxxxiiij willia bastard regned sone wil iam row william woder contraryous man god holy chyrche ad let amende make towne cardeys paynyms destroyed thys king willia destroyed ye holy chirche poscessions part might fynde ther grete debate bytwene hy erchebysshop canterbury ancelme encheson vndername hym hys wykkednesse destroied holy chyrch encheson ther king wylliam bare grete wrath ad cause exylled hym owte lande erchebisshop tho wet courte rome dwelled ope kyng made newe forest cast destroyed xxvi tounes ad lxxx house religyo make forest lenger bredder became wonder glad proude wode ad forest wilde bestys yt thery mervaill wyt men kalled hy keper wodes pasture ad leger lyued wikked became god holy chirche men king let make grete hall westmynster vpon day witsonday helde therin first feste ad loked aboute said halle littel haluendel last became cotrarious thing plesed god displesed hym alle thyng god loued hated dedely ad befell dremed met vpo night lyttel er yt deyed let blode bled grete quantyte blode streme blode lept hygh toward heuen c vethemen clernesse day tourned derkenesse firmament also whan awoke grete drede ne wist done tolde hys dreme meyny counseill ad said grete drede supposed hym myschaunce come seconde nyght monke dremed houshold kyng went chyrch moche peple proude despised peple wyth ad toke ymage crucifixe shamefully bote wyt teth crucifixe mekely suffrid dyd kyng wode man rent armes crucifixe ad cast vnder hys fete defowled threwe brode grete flamme fyre came crucifix mouth dreme many man grete mervaille pthe good man dremed thys dreme told knyght tho moost pryue king alle men forsayde knyght kalled hamundes sone ad tolde dreme kyng sayd shold betoken thyng tha good neuertheles kyg herd laughed ad sette lyttel therof thought wold gone hute pleye forest ad men hym counseilled shold nat day ne maner thing come ye wode bode home mete anon eten myght hym lette nolde gone ye wode haue disporte befell one hys knightes whyche kalled walter tyrell wolde haue shot hert ad arwe glanced vpo braunce trough misauenture smote king hert fell downe dede ye grounde withoute worde spekyg ended lyfe ad grete wonder day deyde let ferme ye erchebisshop rich canterburj xij abbeyes also ad euer dyd grete destructyon ye holy brother pryson tho seysed king henry normandye hande ad helde hys lyfes tyme yere came bisshop auncelme court rome englod ayen kyng accorded yere next comyng ther began grete debate bytwene kyng philip frauce kyng hery englod wher fore kyng hery wet norma dye werre ryght stronge bytwene two tho deyed kyg frauce ad lowys hys sone made kyng anone faders deth ad tho wet kyng hery ayen englod punctel maried maude hys doughter hery emperour almaigne debate bitwene kyng lowys fraunce kyg henry englod kyg henryes two sone lost hygh see capitulo cxxxvj whenne kyng henry ben kyg xvij yere grete echeson erle spoused hys sustre dame maude whiche encheson kyg lowys kyng frauce dyd moche sorwe normadye wherfor kyng englond wonder wrothe grete haste wet ouer see wyt grete power came normadye defende land werre bytwene hem lasted two yere tyll last two foughten gedre ye kig lowys disco fyted vneth scaped way wt moche peyne ad moste part hys men taken kig dyd wyth hem hem lyked ad somme hem ye goodes erchebisshop made oth wold neuer anj word therof ne chau ge bisshoppes spoken ordeined tho went erchebisshop ayene rome withoute doyng kyg iohan tho wrother euer let make co mune crie thurghoute englod holy chyrch rente ad went ouer see thei shold come ayen englod certay day elles thei shold lese hyr rente euermore comaunded eueri shirrefe thurgh oute englad thei shold enquyre bisshop abbot pryour plat holy chyrch fro day afterward receyued maundemet come fro pope shold take body bryge thei shold take kinges hode hir landes holy chyrch whiche yeuen man bi erchebisshop stephen bi priour caunterbury tyme electyon erchebysshop punctel commauded wodes ye erchebisshoppes shold cast downe vnto ye grounde solde king iohan destroyed ordre cisteaux capi cxlix tyme irysshme begone werre vpon kyng iohan king joha ordeyned hy te irlad hugh taxe thurgh oute englod say xxxvm mark sent thurgh englod monkes ordre cisteaux shold helpe vi marck syluer answered ad said durst nothing wythoute hyr abbot cisteaux wherfore kyng johan came irland dyd hem moch sorwe care thei nyst abyde toke moch rausone euerj house hem somme mounted ix mccc mark clene lost destroyed voided hir house ad hir landes thurgh oute englond abbot wauerley drad moch menace forsoke alle abbey went thes preuely ordeyned hy ouer see hous cisteaux wha tyding came pope king moch malice tho king ward ful wroth sent two legatz vnto king owne caled pandolfe othir durat thei shold warne kig pope name shold cese persecucio dyd vnto holy chyrch amende wroge trespasse done erchebisshop canterbury ad pryour vnto monkes canterbury clergye englod shold restore goodes ayen take hem ayens hir elles thei shold kurse kyg bi name thyng conferme pope toke lres billis patentz pthese two legatz camen englod wente kyng northampto ther helde parlamet ad full curtously hym salued saiden syr ben come fro pope rome pee holy chyrch punctel ye land amend amoneste yow first ye popis halfe ye make ful restitucio goodes ye haue rauisshed holy chyrche land ye vnderfenge stephen erchebisshop caterbury dignite pryour canterbury monkes ye yelde ayen vnto erchebisshop hys landes rente withoute holdyg yet ouer ye restitucio make holy chirch shall holde hir pai ed tho aswered king touchyng pryour moke caterbury ye haue sayd wil gladly thyg ye wyll ordeine touchyg erchebisshop shall telle yow myn hert hit lithe erchebisshop leve bisshoprich pope tha hi wol pray vpon auenture sholde lyke othir bisshoprye yeue englod vpo co dicyon wol hym receyue vnderfoge notheles englod erchebysshop yf abyde shal neuer haue good saufconduyt shall taken tho said pandolfe vnto king holy chirche neuer wonet discharge erchebisshop withoute cause resonable euer wonet chastise pryces yt god holy chirch inobediant quod ye king manace ye nay sayde pandolf ye opely haue tolde standeth herte yow telle pope wille thus stand yt hath holy interdited accursed wroges ye haue done holy chirch ad ye clergye ad asmoch ye dwelle beth wille abyde malyce ad wille come none amadement ye shall vnderstonde fro time afterward sentence vpon yow yeue holdeth stede strength vpo thay yow haue comuned time whethir thei ben erles baron knightes othir euer ben hem assoille saufly vnto thys day fro time afterward codicion euer hem accurse wyt yow comen sentece vpon openly specialy assoill quytly erles baron knightes othir maner men hir seruices homage feautes thei shold vnto yow tidinge coferme yeue pleyne power bisshop wynchestre bisshop northewhiche power yeue scotland bisshoppes rouchestre salisbury ad wailis yeue ye power bisshoppes seint dauid landalf seint asse ouer sende thurgh crystendome bisshoppes beyonde see thei shal done accurse alle thay helpeth yow couceill yeueth yow maner nede ye haue partie world assoille hem aso ye auctoryte pope comau de also yow werre hy enemye holy chirch tho aswerde kig mowe ye done tho answered pandolfe seyne yow verbo dei ye ne none heire ye haue neuer daye may crowned tho said king bi almighty god j wist thyg er ye came mi lad ye brought suche tiding shold haue made yow ryde holy yere tho aswerde pandolfe full well wende first comyg ye wold haue ben obedyent god holy chirch haue fulfilled pope commaudement haue shewed pronouced ye pope wille charged therwyth ye haue said ye wist ye cause comyng ye wolde haue made v ryde holy yere punctel ad well ye might haue sayd ye wold haue take holy yere respyte bi pope leue suffre deth ye cowde ordeyne shul nat spare telle yow holy pope message wille charged padolfe delyuered clerk falsed couterfeted kyges money kyg selfe capi cl anone tho commau ded kyg sherews bailifs northapton ye kinges psence thei shold bringe forth ye priso ners might ben vnto deth padolf encheson king wende wold haue gayne sayd hir dedes cause deth thynge spoken afore wha prisoner come kyg kyng comauded hanged ben drawe ad drawe hir eyen oute hir hede amoge clerk falsed kinges money king comau ded shold haged whe padolfe herde comaudemet king stert hy vp smertly anon axed boke cadell ad wold haue cursed alle set vpo clerk ony hode padolfe hi self went seche crosse kyg folowed delyuered clerk hode shold wyt hy euer wold th clerk delyuered went thes padolf felawe durant wet fro ye kyg iohan came ayen pope rome told hy kyg joha wolde nat amede euer abide accursed notheles ye pope grauted ye yere thurgh oute eglod might sing mass couenable chirches make goddes body yeue sike passe shold oute world also men myght christe child ouer wha pope wist sawe kyng wolde nat vnder ye rule gouernauce holy chyrche maner thing pope set king frau ce remissyo synnes sholde take wyth hym alle power might wente englond destroye kyng iohan whan tyding came kyg ioha tho sore annoyed sore drad lest sho de lese reaulme self deth tho sent ye pope messagiers said wold ben iustifyed come maundemet thiges wolde mak satisfactyon maner men pope ordenauce tho set pope ayen englond pa dolf othir messagiers camen canterbury ther king abode xiij day may kyg made oth stand ye pope ordenance padolf legat maner thiges accused shold make full restitucion alle men holy chyrch religyon goodes take hem ayens hir ad alle ye grete lordes englod swore vpo boke ad holydome yf king wolde nat holde oth sayde wolde make holde stregth tho put kyg court rome pope tho yaf vp reaulme englond irlad also hys heires euermore shold come king iohan heires sholde take two reaulmes pope hand shold holde tho two royaumes ye pope ferme payng euery yere vnto ye court rome thousad mark siluer tho toke kyg crowne hede ad set knee thes wordes sayd heryg grete lordes englond resegne vp crowne reaulme englod pope hond innocet iij put holy mercy ordenauce tho vnderfe ge pandolfe croune kyng iohan ad kept v dayes seysin takyg two reaulmes englond irland confermed maner thynges bi chartre foloweth letter obligatorie kig iohan made vn court rome wherfor petres pe bene gadred thurgh oute alle englad ca cli cryste peple thurgh oute worlde dwellyng iohan grate god kyng englond gretyg vniuersite knowyng asmoche haue greued ad offended god owr moder chyrch rome asmoche haue nede merci lord ihesu christ may nothyng worthy offre competant satisfactyon make god holy chirch owne body reaulmes englod irland grace god desyre mek v loue hi meked hy deth crosse thurgh counseil noble erles baron offren freely graunte god apostle seynt petre seint paule modre chirch rome ad owr holy fadre pope jnnocent thridde pope cometh hym reaulme patronage chyrches englond irland hir appertenauces remissyon synnes helpe helthe kyn sowles ad cristen sowles tyme afterward woll receyue holde modre chyrche rome fee ferme doyng feaulte holy fadre pope innocent thridde pope comen hi maner aboue said presence ye wyse pandolfe pope subdekene maken liege homage pope presence hym shull maner thy ge aboue said therto den v alle comen v heires euermore withoute gayne seyeng pope ad eke ward chyrches vacaunt toke thy ge euer last wyll ferme ordeyne specialle rete forsaid reaulme sauyg seit petres pen thing ye moder chyrche rome payeng yere thousand mark syluer ij termes ye yere maner customes shold done forsaid reaulmes seyne mychalmasse estren seyn vij c marc englod ccc mark irland sauyng v heyres iustices ad othir frau chi othir realtes apperteygneth crowne thyges ben said wylle ferme stable withouten ende oblygacyo successours ad heires maner boud owre heyres thurgh presumpcyo falle point ayest thy ge aboue said warned wull nat amende shal lese forsayd reaulme euermore thys chartre oblygacyo owr warrant euermore ferme stable withoute gayn sayeng shull fro daye afterward trewe god moder chyrche rome pope innocet thridde alle thay cometh hym ad reaulmes englod ad irland shull maynten trewly maner point ayes maner bi owr power thurgh goddes helpe clerkes outelawed owt englod came ayen kyg ioha assoilled capitulo clij whane thys chartre made ensealed kyg vnderfege ayen croune pandolfes hande ad sent anon vnto erchebisshop stephen hys othir clerkys lewd men exilled oute land sholde come ayen englod ad haue ayen hir landes hir rente wold make restitucyon goodes taken hem ayens hir king selfe tho padolfe erles baron went tho vnto wycestre ayes erchebisshop stephe wha come kyng went ayes hym fell downe hys fete sayd fair sire ye wellcome crye yow mercy encheson haue trespassed ayens erchebisshop toke hy vp tho armes kyssed hy courtously oftetymes lad dore seynt swytynes chyrch hode assoilled hym sentece hym reconceilled god ad holy chyrche ad seyt margaretes day erchebilshop anon wet sing masse punctel king offred masse mark gold wha masse done went vnderfonge alle hir lades withoute maner gayne sayeng daye made myrthe ioye ynowe yet eterdytyng relesed encheson ye pope set eterdityg shold ben vndoune tyll kyng made iohan wist nat whydder turne gone fell wolde haue gon nycholl went thidderward cam abbey swyneshede abode twoo dayes sat ye mete axed mok howse moche lofe worth sete hym vpon table moke said lofe many tymes tyll venime came oute euery side ye cuppe tho toke ye cuppe fylled wyth good alle brought kyng knelyng sayd syr quod vassaille nevyr dayes youre lyfe ne dronke ye cuppe begy ne monke quod aftyr hys martyrdome aftyr ordeyned grete lordes englond yt alyens sholde gon owt reaulme englond come theryn kyng ry toke tho castelles hys honde whyche king johan hys fadre yeven taken vnto alyens kepe helde wyth hym prowde faukes brend rychely let araye hys castell bedfort whiche kynges yefte johan helde castell ayens kyng henryes wylle wyth myght strength wherfore ye kyng henry came thydder bachylere shent dede disheryted whan king hery victorie euesham ad sir symond erle slayn thurgh helpe might gilbert clare erle gloucestre kepyng warde forsaid simonde thurgh ordenauce king henry wet coutesse gloucestre punctel made holy londe suche vyage world spake hys knyghthode euery man drad hy hygh ad lowe thurghoute crystendom storie hym tellyth aftyrward ye shull opely time kyg ry deide till sir edward crowned kyg grete lordes englod fadreles child wythowte socour thaym might maynten gouerne defende ayens hyr dedely ennemyes pof kyng edward kyng henryes sone capitulo clxj aftyr kyng moch treson thought euyrmore helde hy stylle wyt ad aspye kyges ad euemore made good semblant semed trewe man myght ceyue falsenesse lewelyne thurgh engyne dauid brother werryd ayene vpon kyng edward dauyd pry ce brother herd tydynge ordeyned flyght lewely pryce saw hys brother slowen sore abasshed power hys werre mayntene ad iewelyn began flee ad wende well haue eskaped morwe sir rogyer mortiemer ad prynce morey cesed made hem accorded whylle good kyg edward quene elianore wyfe gascoyne good erle cornewaill made wardeyn englond tyll edward came ayene tho enquered traitours cogeted falsenesse ayens ad ech hem vndyrfege dome aftyr thei deserued mene tyme while ye good kyng edward beyonde see hem make amedes ayens trespaced fals thefe traitour kalled rys ap meriedoke bega make werre ayens nay wherfore grete debate arose bytwene hem hyr frendes moch wolde nat co sente coronacyon ye mene tyme ye forsayd dauid deyde befell dauyd thre doughtyrs whiche worthely maryed fyrst doughtyr maried mercy grace god wet fals traitour sir andrewe herkela way fals traitour tyraunt fals forsworne thurgh noble erle lancastre vnderfeng armes cheualerie thurgh hym made knight tho might see archyers drawe hem one syde othir ad knyghtes also fowghten gedre wonder sore also among othir sir humfrey de boughon erle herford worthy knyght thurgh cristendome stode faught hys enemy vpo brygge thief rybaude skulked vnder brigge fersely spere smote noble knight fowndement bowelles came oute allas sorwe slayne flour solace comfort also curtesye sir rogier clyford noble knyght stode euyr ad fought well nobely hym defended worthy baro last sore wownded hede ad sir willyam sullayad syr rogier bernefeled slayne bataille whan sir andrewe herkela sawe sir thomas men la castre lassed slaked anone companye camen gentyll knyght sir thomas lancastre seyd yeld trai tour yeld gentyll erle aswered tho sayd nay lordes traitours none wyll nevyr v yelde whyles yt owr lyfes lasten leuer haue slayne trouthe tha yelde v yow sir andrew ayene grad vpo sir thomas co panye yollyng wode wolfe said yelde yow traitours taken yeld yow hygh voys saide bethe ware syres none yow hardy vpon lyfe vpon lymme misdone thomas body lancastre ad wyth worde good erle thomas went chapell sayd knelyng vpo knee turned hys visage towardes crosse sayd almyghty god yelde holy put thy mercy wyt vyleyns rybaudes ept aboute hym euery syde tyraunts wode turmentours dispoilled hym hys armure clothed hym robbe ray squyers lyuere forth lad hym vnto yorke water tho myght men seen moche sorwe care ge tyll knightes fledden euery syde rybaudes vyleyns egrely hem discryed grad highe yelde yow traytours yelde yow yolden robbed bou den thevys allas shame despyte gentill ordre knyghthode bataylle lande tho wytoute lawe holy chyrch tho reuerence tha bene bordelhows punctel bataille fadre ayens sone vncle ayens hys nephew somoche vnkendenesse neuer seyn englod tyme amonge folk one nacyo kynrede pyte othyr hungrie wolfe hath shepe wonder grete lordes englod nat nacyon medled othir nacions seyne somme bretos saxon somme danoys pehites somme frenshmen somme norman somme spaynardes somme romayns somme henaudes somme flemmynges othir dyuerse nacyos whiche nacyons accorded kynde blode englond grete lordes ben wedded englyssh peple shold pee haue ben reste amoges hem withoute envye bataill sir rogier cliford tak sir iohan mo bray sir william tuchet sir william fit william many othir worthy knightes taken bataille sir hughe dandell next daye taken put pryson shold haue bene deth yf spoused kynges nece erle gyllebertes suster gloucestre anon sir bartholomewe badelesmere taken stowe park maner bisshoppes lyncolne nephew many baron ad baneretz wherfore made moch sorwe thomas lacastre beheded poufrete v sholde put vpon poyntes treson befell ye barre kynges iustyces bare hede thief fair halle withyn owne castel made thery many fest riche eke poure ad iustyces syr hugh spe cer fadre aymer valaunce erle thomas lord ye kyng put vpo ye haue lade ride wyt baner displaied ayest pee traitour worde gentyll erle thoas wyt hygh vois said nay lordes soth bi seyt thomas neuer traitour iustice said ayen thomas lord kig put vpo ye haue robbed folk mordred peple thefe thomas king also put vpo yow discomfited peple wt folk owne reaume wherfore ye went fled ye wode outelawe also ye taken outelawe thomas traitour ye shul hoged reso ye kig foryeve iewes loue quene isabel thoas reson wolde also ye shold hoged kyg hath foryeve yow yt cause lygnage thomas asmoche ye take fleyng owtelawe kyng wyll youre hede shalbe smytten ye haue well deserued anone doth hy owte presence anone bryg hym hys jugemet whan getyl knyght thomas herd wordes wyth hyghe voys cryed sore wepyng said allas seynt thomas fayr fadre allas shall deed thus grau te nowe blyssefull god aswere avaylled hym thyng kursed gascoynes put hy hydder thydder hym cryed hygh voys god dredfull wel knowe thyn open traitrye euyll deth shalt thow deye thou hast wel deservyd tho sette vpo hys hede scorne olde chappelet rent torne nat worth halpeny sette vpon leue white palfrey full vnsemelich ad eke bare olde bryddell horryble noyse drouen wente scotland wyt houndred thousad men armes witsontyde yere owr lord ihesu crist mccc ad xxij scottes went ad hyd hem mountaynes wodes caried englysshmen fro day day kyng might maner thyng hem fy de enquered aspied last trewth founde sought ad atteynt taken fals traitour noble erle thomas lancastre tolde er vnto deth takyng burbrygge hy saide yere shold take holde traitour holy man said wherfore kyng sent pryuely syr anthoyn lucy knight cotrey cardoille sholde take sir andrewe herckela ad put hy vnto deth brynge thyg vnto ende kyng sent comission andrewe taken cardoill led vnto barre ye maner erle worthely arayed swerd gurt aboute hy ad hosed spored tho spake sir anthoyne maner sir andrewe quod kyg put vpon asmoch thow hast bene orped thy dedes ded vnto mochel honour made erle cardoill ad thow traitour vnto thy lord kyg laddest hys peple cotre shold haue holpe hy bataill beyghelad thow laddest away cotre copelad thurgh erledome lancastre wherfore lord kyng scomfyted scottes thurgh thy lord aftyrward trewly serue tho commauded knave anone haue hys spore helys aftyr let breke ye swerde ouer hede whiche kyng yafe kepe defede lande therwith made hi erle cardoil aftyr let hym vnclothe furred tabart hode furred cote gurdel sir anthoyne said vnto andrewe quod art thou knight knaue thy treson ye kyng wille thou shalt ho ged drawe thy boweles taken owte thy body brent thy body quartred thyn hede smyten sent vnto londo ther shall stonde vpo londo brugge thy fowre quarter shull set fowre townes englond mowe chastysed antoyne said done maner thynge last day octobre yere grace mccc xxij yere sonne tho turned blode peple saw dured fro morne til xi clokke day pof ye miracle yt god wrought seynt thomas loue lacastre wherfore king let close chyrche dores pryowre pounfret yt man sholde vertu holy martyr also god hath yeuen therto creples hyr goyng croked hir ho de hir foot blynde also hir sighte ad many sike folke hyr hele dyuerse maladyes loue thys good martir also ryche man coundom gascoyne suche maladie right syde roted fyll way hym myght se lyuer also hert stanke vnneth men myght come nye hym wherfore fre de wodre sory last almyghty god wolde praied seynt thomas herewich southfolk xxiiij day septebre yere grace mcccxxvi quene ad sir edward hir sone set lres ye maire comminalte londo requyryng thei shold ben helpig quarel cause thei begone seye destroye traitours ye reame none aswere sent agayne wherfor quene sir edward hir sone senten othir patet letter vnder hyr seales tenour lettre folowed maner izabell grace god quene englod lady irlad coutesse pountyf edward eldest sone kyg englod duke gwihenne erle chestre ad poutyf monstroille maire minalte cyte london sendeth gretyg moche haue ye tyme set yow lettres become thys lad wt good aray good maner honour profyte holy chirch right dere lord kyng ad reame might power kepe maynten alle good folke forsayd reame holde vpon prayen yow ye wolde ben helpyg v moche ye may quarel commune profyte reaume haue none aswere ye forsaid lettres ne knowe yowr wille partye wherfore sent yow agayne pray charge yow ye bere yow ayens v haue cause greue ye ben v helpyng mayes ye may ye may well openly knowen alle ben comen wyth v thys reame thenken done tha alle thyg lyked good shal commune proffyte alle reame onely destroye hugh spencer enemye also enemye alle reame englond ye well opely knoweth wherfor praye yow charge yow ye sayth ye owe owre lord kyng v yf said hugh specer enemye come withinne power ye hastely ben take saufly kept vnto ye tyme tyll haue ordeyned hym owr wille ye leue maner wyse ye desire honour profite v alle alle reame vnderstondyng well yf ye owr prayer ad maundement shall holden vnto yow also ye shull gete yowr self wurshypp profyte yf ye sende v hastely answere yowr wille pyeue baldok vj day octobre lettre erly dawenyg day seynt denys taken vpon newe crosse shepe many copy lre takked vpon wyndowes ad dores vpon othir place ye cite men passyng way might see rede tyme kyng edward lodo towre hys mete messagier came hasle sayd quene isabell come londe herewych brought hyr companye sir iohan henaud hym armes wythoute nombre wyt word syr hughe specer fadre spake sayd thus kyng wurshypfull lord kyng englond mowe ye make good chere certey ly ben owres kyg sawe thys word confortable notheles sorefull pensyf herte kyng yet fulfylleth hys mete ther came halle othir messagier ad sayd quene isabell arryued herewych besyde yepswych southfolk syr hugh spencer fadre spake sayd messauger maner telle ye haue seyne fayr frede come stre ghte certys sire soth saye ne hyr companye vij hodred men armes punctel wyth worde sir hughe spencer fadre cryed hygh vois sayd allas allas bene betraied certys lyttel power neuer come londe folk thys londe hyr consent therfor mete toke hyr counceill ad went toward walys arere ye walsshmen ayens quene isabell edward hyr sone fyght purpose euericho maistir waltier stapilton bysshop excestre kynges tresorer beheded london capitulo ccviij tyme kyg edward sore adrad lest men londo wold yelde hem vnto quene isabell ad hir sone edward wherfore sent maistir waltier stapylton hys tresorer wardeyne keper cyte london wyth mayre came gylldehall london axed keyes yates cyte thurgh vertu strength hys commyssyon ad wolde haue kepyng cyte co munes answeryd sayd wolde kepe cyte honour kyng edward ad isabell quene duke kynges sone withoute bisshop tho sore anoyed swore othe shold abye anone kyg edward comen owte walys commune anon cite token bisshopp lad hym amydes chepe smoten hys hede set heed right hond beheded two squyers helde wyth bisshopp one kalled wyllia walle bisshoppes nevew othir called iohan padygton also toke burgys london kalled ioha marchall sir hugh spencer spye fadre smyten hys hede also tyme bisshop lo fayr towr makyg hys closse vpon ryuer tamyse withoute temple bare hym faylled stone make therof ende wherfore commauded men gon ye chirche freres carmes token stone make therwith towre moche sand morter ad olde robous left ad despyte bisshopp done vnto holy chyrch two squyers buryed sand though thei ben hou de ther leyen xi wekes tyll quene isabel sent hir lettres commune ad prayed hem thei wold suffre grau te bisshop myght take owte place bene buryed excestre hys owne chyrche hys two squyers buryed seynt clemens chyrch wytoute temple bare wonder though ye bisshop deyed euell deth coueytous man wyth hy mercy euell couceilled ye king sone arnold spaigne taken asse tent haue lad vm pounde siluer v barelles ferryetes vnto douseperes frauce helpe hast quene isabell hyr deth edward hyr sone also thys arnold put deth withoute cyte londo kyng edward sir hugh spencer erle arundell taken capitulo ccix kyng edward sent maistir walter stapilton tresorer lodo punctel kepe cyte ayes quene isabel wyfe ayes edward hyr sone anone hy selfe toke hym sir hugh spencer sone sir iohan erle arundell maistir robert baldock hys chaunceler fals pyled prest token hyr way toward bristowe ther kyg abode littel terme made sir hugh spe cer fadre conestable keper castell kyng othir spencer went shipp sailled toward walys toke leue stiward ne none ye kynges houshold went ouer walys arere walssh men ayens dame isabell quene duke hyr sone ad erle kente sir iohan henaude went purswed hem hyr power ecresed euery day last kyng take vpo hylle walys sir hugh spencer sone othir syde hylle fals piled clerk maister robert baldock fast besides hem brought ayen englod almyghty god wold kyng hym self sauf kepyng castell kenilworth hy kept sir heri sir thomas brother lacastre sir hugh specer fadre came put hy quenes grace sir edward hyr sone duke gwihenne sir hugh spe cer ye sone tyme yt take wolde ete maner mete thir dryke wist haue non mercy sauf onely dede quene hir counceyll tho ordeyned shold haue bene deth londo feble hys moch fastyng dede almost therfore ordeyned shold haue iugement herfort place toure hood take heed also robert baldoke piled clerk fals kinges chau celere set vpo hir hedes chappelets sharpe netlys ij squyers blewe eres ij grete bugle horne vpon two prysonners myght ther blowyng owte wt horne mo tha myle one simod redyg ye ky ge marhall hem bare hyr armes vpo spere reuersed token sholde vndon euermore vpon morwe sir hugh specer sone dapned deth drawe honged beheded bowelles taken owte hys body brent quartred ad iiij quartiers set iiij townes englond hede sent lodo brigge symond encheso despysed quene isabell drawe honged stage made amydes forsaid sir hughes galewes day lyttell fro then sir iohan arudel beheded sir hugh specers couceillers anon sir hugh specer fadre drawe hoged beheded bristowe hoged ayen ye armes wt ij stroge repes ye iiij day hewe peces ad howndes ete hy ye encheson yt kyg yeue hy erledome wynchestre hys hede lad thidder put vpon spere ther fals baldoke sent london ther deyde pryson amonges thefes men dyd reuerece wold done vnto houde deyden traitours englod blyssed almyghty god wonder thurgh theyr cou ceill good erle thomas la castre vnto deth alle helden thomas la castre thurgh traytours vndon hyr heyres sherited kyng edward put downe dignyte benomme capitulo ccx anon quene jsabel edward hir sone alle grete lordes englod one assent sente kyng edward castell kenillworth ther yt kepyng vndyr warde sir iohan hachy bysshop ely sir iohan percy baro encheson shold ordeyne hys parlemet certey place englond redresse amend state reame kyng edward hem answeryd sayd lordes quod ye se full well loo take seall yeue yow myne power ordeyne parlement wher ye wyll toke hyr leue hym camen ayen baron englond whan kynges patet thyg shewed lordes tho ordeyned parlement shold bene westmynster vtas seynt hilarie grete lordes englond et ordeyne hem ther ayens time parlemet shold ben day yt lement ordeyned kyg wold nat come therfor maner thyg h sette hy self assygned notheles baros sent hym tyme ad othir swore goddes sowle wold come foot wherfore ordeyned grete lordes englond shold lenger ben kyng ben deposed sayd wold croune kyg edward elder duke guy hene sent tydyng vnto ye kyg ward vndyr sir ioha erle garene sir ioha hachym bysshop ely sir iohan percy baron sir william trussell knight erle sir thomas lancastre yelde vp hyr homage vnto hym alle englond pand sir willyam trussell sayd wordes syr edward encheso ye haue traied yowr peple englond ad haue vndon many grete lordes ye reame englod withoute cause nowe ye withstond thaked god also encheso ye wold come lement ye ordeyned westmynster owne letter patet teined trete wyt yowr liege men king sholde therfor thurgh mune assent lordes englond telle vnto yow wordes ye shull vnderstonde sir yt baron englod one asset wyll ye kyng englod vtterli haue put owte realte euermore bisshop ely said tho ye kyg sir edward yelde vp feaute homage erchebisshoppes bisshoppes eglod clergye tho said syr iohan garenne sir edward yelde vp vnto feaute homage erles englond sir hery percy yafe vp also ther hys homage hy baron englod tho said sir willia trussell yelde vp vnto sir myn homage also ye knyghtes englod holden seriaurrye othir maner thyng yow fro day afterward ye shul claymed kyng nothir king holde fro time afterward ye shull holde singuler peple wete thennes vnto londo ther lordes englond hem abode ad sir edward abode pryson good kepyng day co uersion seynt paule xx yere regne pprophecye merlyn declared kyng edward sone kyng edward cap ccxi king edward prophecied merly said ther shold come goot oute care shold haue horne siluer berde withe snowe doppe shold come owt nosethirles shold betoken moche harme hunger deth peple grete losse lad begynnyg regne shold haunted moche lecherye said soth allas ye tyme kyng edward kyg edwardes sone borne canaruan walys soth horne siluer ad berde snowe whan made prince walys moche yafe hy riote felonye soth said merlyn prophecye shold come oute nose doppe time grete huger amoge ye poure peple stroge deth amonge ryche deyde strauge land mochel sorwe werre scotlad afterward loste scotland ad gascoigne whilles hym selfe kyng ther moche lecherye hauted also merly told said goot shold seche ye flour lyfe deth said sothe spoused isabel kyges doughter fraunce time merly said shold made brugges folke vpo dyches ye see wel seen bannokkesborne scotlad wha discofyted ther scottes merly told also stone sholde fall fro castelles many townes shold made pley sayd soth wha kyg edward discomfited scotlad came tho southward ye scottes besieged castelles dyd hem moch harme brent townes vnto hard erth aft er ward merly sayd egle shold come cornewaille shold haue fetheres gold pryde shold haue piere shold despyse lordes blood deye thurgh bere gauersise prophecye ful well knowe ad fonde sothe bi egle vnderstode sir pier ganastone tho erle cornewaille wonder prowde man despised baronage englod aft er ward beheded gauersichet ye erle lacastre erle warrewyk merlyn tolde hys tyme yet shold seme yt bere shold brene bataill shold vpo arme see felde araied lyke shelde sholde deye many whyte hedes said sothe brennyng bere betokened grete drede thurgh cuttyg swerd bataill ordeyned felde shelde vpon arme ye see betokened bata lle mytone ther came scottes maner shelde maner wynge slew vpon swalle men relygyo prestes ad seculers wherfor ye scottes kalled bataille despyte englysshme white bataille merly said ye forsayd bere shold done goot moche harme sholde vpon southwest also vpo blode said also goot sholde lese moch dele lande tyll ye tyme shame sholde hy ouercome tha sholde clothe wyt lyos skyne sholde wyne ayen loste moche thurgh peple shold come oute northwest shold make hy bene adrad avenge hys enemyes thurgh couceil ij owles fyrst sholde peril vndone ij owles sholde wende ouer ye see strau ge lad ther shold dwelle tyll certey tyme sholde come englond ayene ij owles sholde moch harme vnto many one thei sholde cownceylle gote meve werre ayens forsayd bere goot owles sholde come vnto arme see burton vp trent shold wede ouer drede bere sholde flee swan companye vnto bury toward ye north thurgh vnkynde owtputter swan tha sholde slaine sorwe bere sholde slayn full nygh owne nest sholde stode vpon poufrete vpon sone shall shede bemes many folke shall seche mochel vertue said full sothe punctel good erle thoas lacastre borne ye northwest cosyn kyng sone vncle lawe made ye king lese moche lad purchased wylfully till last king therof toke shame self fylled cruelte gate ayene loste ad moche therto thurgh folke let asseble oute ye northwest made ben adrad aueged hy hys baros thurgh couceill sir hughe specer fadre ad sir hugh sone beforne outelawed eglod hir wykkednesse aft er ward came ayene englod sir hugh spencer fadre oute frau ce moch counceilled kyng shold werre vpon thoas lacastre kyng specers erle arudell ad hyr power met thomas la castre burton vp trente hym discofited sir humfrey erle hereford copanie fledde forsayd thoas hufrey hir panie burbrugge sir andrewe herkela kalled vnkyde outeputter also sir symod warde erle yorke came ad met wt thomas lacastre wyt huge companye hem ther discomfited scomfiture erle hereford slayne vpon brugge cowardely spere foundemet good erle thomas take lad vnto pounfrete tho beheded besyde owne castell afterward many men hy sought myracles god dyd hy tyme merlyn sayd sorwe harme shold deye peple hys land wherfor many landes shold vpo hem boldre said sothe encheson baron done deth seynt thomas quarell lancastre peple many londes became bolder meue werre vpon kyng hyr blode turned many ad diuerse nacyons afterward merlyn tolde ad said forsayd owles sholde done moche harme vnto flour lyfe ad dethe shold brynge hyr vnto moche disease shold goo wede oueruer see frauce make pee flourdelyse sholde abyde tyll tyme hyr seed shold come ad seche hyr tho shold abyde tyll tyme shold clothen grace ad two owles shold seke put hem vnto spitouse deth yt prophecye well knowen full sothe sir hugh spencer fadre sir hugh sone dyd moch sorwe persecucyon vnto quene isabell thurgh hyr procurement hir lord kig ordeyned amonges hem put vnto hir wage sey xx shillyng day wherfore ye kyng frauce hir brother wonder sore anoyed sente englond re vnto kyg edward sholde come hys parlement paris frauce kig edward sore adrad come wende haue bene arested till made amendes trespace sir hugh spencer fadre ad sone done harme done quen isabell suster wherfore thurgh hir ordenauce consent spencer quene isabell went ouer see fraunce make accord bitwen kyng edward kyng frauce hyr brother dwelled fraunce till edward hyr eldest sone came hir seche dwelled ther bothe till aliaunce made bitwen hem gentill erle henaude yf wyt helpe might destroie ouercome venyn ad falsenesse ye spencer sir edward shold spouse dame phelip wurshipfull lady ad erles doughtyr henaude wherfore quen jsabell sir edward hir sone sir edmond wodestoke kynges brother englond sir iohan henaude sir rogier mortymer wygmore sir thomas rocelyn sir ioha cromwell sir willia trussel many othir ye aliaunce getil erle thomas lacastre illed owt englod quarell ad disherited hir lades ordeined grete power ad arriued herwych southfolk sone aftyr pursweden specers till take put vnto spytouse deth sayd hir panye ad also grete falsenesse kyg edward peple merly said also gote shold put grete disese grete anguissh grete sorwe shold lede lyfe said soth tyme kyng edward take put warde tyll ye specers put vnto deth also encheson yt nold nat come vnto owne parlement londo ordeyned assigned selfe ad baronage ad also wolde gouerne ad rule peple ne hys reaulme kyng sholde done somme baros englod came yelde vp hir homage vnto hem othir reaume daye conuersion seynt paule ad yere regn xx put ryalte euermore euer lyued hys lyfe afterward moch sorwe anguissh kynd edward thridde conquest capitulo ccxij kig edward carnarvan regned sir edward wydesore hys sone crowned kig annoynted westmynster thurgh consent ad grete lordes reaume ye sonday cadelmasse eue yere grace mcccxxvi age tyme xv yere encheso hys fadre ward ye castell kenilworth eke put downe hys royalte reame englod withoute kyng fro feste seynt katheryne ye yere aboue sayd vnto feste candelmasse tho maner plees ye ky ge benche asten tho comauded sherewes englond thurgh wryte warne party defandauntz thurgh somnyng ayene also ferthermore prysoners kyges gaylles yt attached thurgh sherewes shold lete gone quyte kyg edward aftyr hys coronacyon ye prayer besechig liege reaulme graunted hem chartre stedfast pee alle wolde axe sir ioha henaude companie token hir leue king lordes reaume turned home hir owne contre ayene ad eche hem full riche yeftes euerych man value estate tho englod pee reste grete loue bitwen kyng lordes comuneli englysshmen said amoges hem deuell dede tresour kyg fadre tresour specers fadre son tresour erle arundell maistir robert baldoke ye kinges chauceler deted quene isabellys ordenauce sir rogier mortymer wygmore kyng thyng therof hir wille hir delyuerace nought hyr londes afterward ye shall kyng edward went sta hope mete scottes capitulo ccxiij yet tyme king edward castell kelworth vnder keping sir henry yt erle thoas brothir lacastre yt thomas erle leycestre kyng graunted erledom la castre king fadre seised hond put oute thomas lacastre brother erle lacastre leicestre eke styward englod brother hys tyme sir edward kig edwardes fadre made sorwe wytout ende cause might speke wyfe ne hys sone wherfore moche meschyef though yt lad ruled fals counceill yit kyng edwardes sone kalled edward wt log shankes come worthiest blode world thoos wonet yeve grete yeftes large moost pryue wyt kig owne sone enemyes bi nyght ad daye procured make debate contek bytwen hy sone isabell wife frere preschours hy good frendes euermore cast ordeyned night bi day howe myght brynge hym owte pryson amoge hir copanye yt freres pryuely brought frere called dunbenet ordeyned ad gadred grete companye folk helpe nede frere take put castel ponnfrete deide pryson sir hery erle lancastre kynges fadre kepyng thurgh comaudemet kyng deliured edward ye ky ge fadre endenture vnto syr thomas berewyk sir johan mautrevers lad castell kemlworth vnto castel berewyke kept ther saufly e tren next aftyr hys coronacio kyng ordeyned huge hoste fyght ayens scottes sir johan erles brother henaude fro beyonde see came helpe kyng edward ad brought wyt seven houdred men armes arryued dover comauded go forth tyll thei came yorke ther kyg abode hem scottes came thyder kyg make pee accord accordement bitwen hem last littel tyme tyme englysshme clothed cote hodes peynted lettres flour full semely longe berdes therfor scottes made bylle fastened vpon chyrch dores seyt petre toward stangate ad thus said scripture despite englysshmen loge berde hertles peyted hood wytlees gay cote graceles make englond thriftlees trinite day next began contake cite york bitwen englisshmen ye henaudiers debate quelled erledome nycholl mordred lxxx aftir buried vndyr stone seyt clemets chyrch hawe fossegate encheson henaudes came helpe ye kyng hir pee cried paine lyfe lymme halfe fonde enquest cyte englysshmen begone debate englysshmen stoped ye scottes park stanhope turned ayen scotland capi ccxiiij tyme scottes assembled hyr power camen englond quelled robbed might take also brenten destroied north contre thurgh oute tyll came parke stanhope wiredale scottes helden hem buschemet whe kyng herde thurgh certeyne aspies scottes anone right wyt hoste besieged hem withyn forsaid parke scottes wiste nevyr wherto gon vnto hir harmes abyde parke xv dayes vitaylles hem failled euery syde gretly epired body sith yt brute came fyrst brytaign vnto tyme neuer seyne fayre host englysshmen alien ad men foot ordeyned hem fyght wt scottes thurgh engyn sir henry erle lancastre sir iohan henaude yt wolde haue gone ouer water withe haue fought scottes sir rogier mortimer consented nat therto preuely taken mede ye scottes hem helpe thei might wente ayene vnto hyr owne contre mortymer couceilled moch thoas brotherton erle marchall yt kyng edwardes vncle forsaid thomas shold assemble tyme vnto scottes assented wist doyg bitwen scottes forsaid mortymer encheso yt marchall englod hy parteyned euer vauntwarde sent hastely erle lancastre sir ioha henaude yt shold fight vpo ye scottes preiudice harmyg hy fee thei thei shold sto de hir owne peryll forsaid hys bataille rere doos ye erle lacastre haue fought hym folk meved fyght scottes ad maner deceyued wist nothyng thys treson thus kyg pri cipaly deceyued ad night mortymer wach kepe hoste night destourbled ye wach thyg must mene whyle ye scottes stele bi nyght toward hir owne contre faste might kyng falsely betraied wede traytours lande ben brought ede sayd nowe ye lordes traitoursly kyng deceyued mervously ad boldely ye scottes dyd werre iames douglas cc hondred men armes ryden thurghowte hoste kyng edward nyght scottes skaped fro hir place toward hir contre aboue sayd tyll c men kiges pawillo quelled many men hyr beddes cryed tyme naward naward othir tyme doglas donglas wherfor king pauillo moch othir folke wonder sore affraied blysshed almighty god kyng taken ad grete peryll tho reaume englond ad night mone shone full clere bryght kynges men scottes escaped harmeles ad morwe kyg wyst scottes ascaped hyr contre wonder sory full hertely wept ad yet wyst hy done treson fals treson full well knowe good whyle storie telleth kyng edward came ayen tho york sorwefull hoste departed euery man went hys owne contre ful hevy chere mornyng semblant henaudes toke hyr leue went vnto hyr owne contre kyg hyr trauaille hugely hem rewarded encheson vyage kyng dispedyd moche hys tresour wasted tyme seyne two mones firmament one clere othir derke myght tho see thurghoute world ad grete debate tyme ayens pope iohan xxij aftyr seynt petre ad emperour almaigne tho made hi emperour ayens pope wyll tho helde see auymo wherfor eperour made hys crye rome ordeyned othir pope hyght nycholas frere menour ayes ye right holy chyrch wherfor kursed power othir pope sone leid encheson mervailles seyne men said world nygh ende pof deth king edward carnarvan cap ccxv nowe turne ayene sir edward carnarvan king sometyme englond ad put dignite allas tribulacion sorw hy befell thurgh fals couceill leued trusted vpo moch afterward destroied thurgh hyr falsenesse god wolde edward carnarvan ye castell berkley vnder keping sir morys berkeley ad sir iohan mautrevers made coplayt sorwe disese punctel oftetymes axed wardeyns trespaced ayes dame isabell wife ad sir edward sone made newe kynge thei wolde nought visite tho asweryd one wardeyns worthy lord displese nat shall telle yow encheson done hem vnderstode lady wif came thyng nye yow ye wolde hir strangle quelle also ye wolde lord sone tho answeryd simple chere allas allas pryson owne wille nowe god almyghty wote thought nevyr nowe wolde dede wolde god tha sorwe passed phit longe king thurgh couseyll mortimer graunted warde ad kepyng sir edward hys fadre sir thomas iorney forsayd sir iohan mautrevers thurgh kynges lettre ad put owte holy forsaid sir moryce warde kyng ad toke lad kyng vnto castell corfe whiche castell forsayd kyng edward hated deth kept hym saufly tyll came vnto seit mathewes day septembre yere grace thowsand thre hondred xxvij forsaid sir rogier mortymer sent maner deth wyse edward carnarva shold done dethe anone forsaid thomas iohan seyne lettre ad commau dement made kyg edward carnarvan good chere good solas thei might soper thyng kyng wyste traitrie whan ye tyme goo bedde king wente vnto hys bedde laye slept fast kyg lay slept traitours fals forsworne ayens hir homage hir feaute pryuely kynges chambre hir companye wyt leyden hughe table vpon wombe wyth men pressede helden fast downe iiij corner table vpon body wherwith good awoke wonder sore adrad dede slayne turned hys body vp sodowne tho token fals traitours wode tyrauts horn put foudement depe might token spite coper brenyng put thurgh horne hys body oftetymes rolled therwith hys boweles quelled hyr lord thyg perceyued aftyr entered gloucestre kyng edward spowsed phelip erlis doughtyr henawde york cap ccxvij aftyr cristmasse tho next swyng sir iohan henaude brought wyth phelipp brother doughtyr erle henawde nece englod kyng kyng edward kyng heryes sone edeture called rageman whiche conteyned homage feautes fyrst ye kyg scotland prelats erles ad baron reaulme scotland hir seales set ther othir chartres remembrauces kyng mortymer ad nat loge aftyr ye quene isabell ne toke hir owne hade ye lordship poufrete almost lades value apperteyned croune eglod yt kig dispede v ad escheker quen jsabell mortymer grete meyn hir ccxx nowe shull ye sir rogier mortymer wingmore desired coueyted hygh astate kyng grauted hym called erle march thurgh oute hys lordshyp becam prowde hauteyne wolde lese forsake name auncestres euer mortimer hi mordred edmond wodestoke erle kent kynges brother edward ca uan beheded wychestre capitulo ccxxi vpon tyme befell sir edmod wodestoke erle kent spake vnto pope iohan xxij avyuion said almighty god oftetymes thomas loue lacastre many grete miracle many men woman thurgh dyuerse malady vndone vnto world thurgh praier thei brought vnto hir helthe ad sir edmod praied pope hertely wolde graute hi grace forsaid thomas myght translatyd ope said nay shold traslated vnto time bettyr certefyed clergye englond sent hir obedience thyng god loue thomas lacastre aftir suggestyon forsayd erle kent vnto hy made edmod sawe might spede hys purpose touchyng translacyon praied couceill touchyng sir edward carnarva brother said longe gone king englond thyng myght best done touching delyurance syth commune fame thurgh englond lyfe hole sauf pope herde hym telle sir edward lyve commauded erle vpon benyson shold helpe power might deliured owte pryson ad saue hys body maner might breng thys thyng ende assoilled hy companye pena culpa tho helpe hys deliurance tho toke edmod wodestoke leue pope came ayen englond whan sir edmond comen somme freres preschours came ad said sir edward hys brother yet liue castel corf vndyr kepyng sir thomas gurnay tho sped hy forsayd edmond fast might till yt came vnto ye castell corfe spake faire wyt iohan dauerill conestable castell yafe hy rich yeftes haue acquytauce hy knowe hys couceill thus befell forsaid sir edmond prayed spicially telle hy preuely hys lord hys brother sir edward yf lyued dede lyue prayed hym one haue sight sir ioha dauerill hygh herted man full corage answeryd shortely vnto sir edmond said sir edward hys brother hele vnder kepyng durst shewe vnto man syth yt defended hy ye kinges halfe edward edwardes sone dere brother yf yow plese praye hertely yt ye good confort shall ordeyne yow sone ye shull come oute pryso delyured yt disese yt ye ben great lorship shall vndrestande haue cosentyg almost grete tho quene wist syr edmond come vnto wychestre anon praied fast wete vnto kyng edward hyr sone syr edmond good erle arestyd anone ad led vnto barre robert henaude coroner kynges houshold associated vnto hy sir rogier mortimer tho speke forsaid robert ad said syr edmond erle kente ye shal vnderstonde v wyte principaly vnto owr liege lord sir edward kyng englond almighty god saue ad kepe ye hys dedely ennemye traitour also comune enemye vnto reaume ye haue bene aboute many day make preuy delyuerace sir edward som tyme kyg englod brother whiche put downe rialte comune assent lordes englond pesing owr lord kyges astate also reaulme tho asweryd good man said soth sir vnderstonderstondeth well neuer traytour kyng ne ye reame god ad world ferthermore kynges leue shal preue defende man owght tho sayd mortimer sir edmond fer forth knowe yt may nat well gaynesaid ad psence ben shalbe well prouyd hath fals mortimer sam lettre sir edmond take syr iohan daueryll castell corff toke vnto kyng edward brother sir edmod wist ne supposed thing sir iohan daueryll ben fals delyure hys lre suche wyse mortimer thought maner thing lettre ad said sir edmond shewed letter sealyd axed knewe lettre seal sir edmond loked theron avysed longe printe seal might see lettre withy forth thery wist wel seall thought yt letter bore grete charge thought thing lettre ad said openly heryg hem ye forsoth seall nat forsake loo quod mortimer sire ye heren hath said knowelecheth lettre seal ye shul coteyned theryn mortimere opened lettre folde fore gedre red opyli word word heryng whan letter red sayd
