thurgh fals suggestion made hys othe vnto forsayd king edward ouer astate ad oth pope hi assoilled thurgh hys bylles hy sent anone king edward wist therof ordeined anon baron came vnto berewyke coquered towne whyche coquest ther slayn xxv vijc ye bailloll kig scotlad came yelde hy vnto kyg edward kyg afterward deliuered oute towre london grete lordes scotland take berewyke yaf hem saufco duit go scotland scottes sith thurgh hir falsenesse werred vpon kyng edward sir iohan bailloll king scotlad saw thys went put hym ouer see vnto dupier lyued ther vpon owne lode wel might tyll scottes wolde amende hem hir mysdedes trespace lad hym sir edward sone wherfore ye scottes despyte hym called hym ioha turnelabard cause wolde offende ne trespace ayens kyg edward englond forsoke reame scotland sette therof littel pry sir iohan loge tyme dwelled fraunce tyll deyed sir edward sone vnderfeng hys heritage homage vnto kyng frau ce landes dunpied fell afterward edward joha baillols sone squyer englond yt bore yorke shyre kalled iohan barnaby edward baillol loued moch ny ful pryue iohan barnaby debate frenshman ye toune dunpier quelled hy went way might castell haue socour helpe lorde anone came officiers town take iohan barnaby felo sir edward lord halpe hym rescued ad night made wende owte castel punctel ad went hys way ad came englond wythoute harme kyng frauce saw sir edward rescued felo became woder wroth ayens sir edward anon let hy arestyd toke hande londe tho dwelled sir edward pryson vnto tyme yt sir hery beaumout came frauce whych henry tyme erle angos scotland thurgh wyfe put oute forsaid erledom whe ye accord made bytwen englond scotlad thurgh ye quen jsabell sir rogier mortymer hir companye mariage made bitwen dauid robert brus sone dame iohan ye tour kyng edwardes sustyr englod well vnderstode thys ende shold nevyr come right thurgh helpe sir edward bailloll whyche right heyr reaume scotland king reaume frauce called lowys loued moch sir hery wyt full pryue thought make deliuraee sir edward baillols body might maner wise tho praied kyg wolde graunte hem grace sir edward baillols body vnto ye next parlement might liue wyt owne rete men tyme must stande iuged bi hys perys ye parlemet kyg grauted praier made forsaid edward delyured owte pryson maner aboue said anon oute pryson sir hery toke hym forth wyth hy lad hy englond made hy dwelle prevely maner sande vp onse yorkeshire wt ye lady vescy ordeyned hi great retinue peple englysshmen ad also alien conquere ayene heritage yafe moch siluer vnto sowdeours alien helpe hi thei promysed helpe hy might failled hy nede tyme donald erle morrif herd telle sir edward preuely come went made wt hy grete ioye comyg ayene said behight grete lordes skotlande shold hy entedaut sholde hy holde kyg right heyre scotland ad moch wolde done sholde crowned kyng lande dyden hy homage feaute tho came sir henry beaumont kyg edward englond praied wey charite wold graunte grace vnto sir edward bailloll must saufely goo lad fro sand hall vnto scotlad coquere hys right heritage scotland kyng answeryd said vnto yf suffre ye bailloll wente thurgh lad scotland peple wolde say shold assentyng companie nowe sir praye yow ye wold graute hy leue take vnto sowdeours englisshme might saufely lede hy thurgh land vnto scotland sir vpon thys couenaunt befell god forbede discofyted bataille thurgh scottes j also lordes holde wt bailloll ben euermore tint oute owr rente haue englond kyng vpo thys couenaut graunted hyr bone touchyng tho quarell yt claymed haue londes rente reaulme scotland name ye lordes purswede mater saye sir edward ye bailloill chalenged reame scotland sir henry beaumout erle angos sir dauid stroboly erle athelees sir geffroy monbray waltier comyne many othir put owte hir heritage scotland whan pee made bitwen englond scotland said ye shull vnderstode lordes toke wyth hem v hondred men armes two thousad archiers footman tho te shippe rauenespore sailled see till camen londe kynkehorne xij myle seint iohanes toune anone sent oute hir shippes ayene shold nat hurte ne epired nethir man shold gon shipp ayen though thei nede abide perilles flee stonde rather suffre dethe flee maynten hir trewe quarell wha erle fiffe fers man storne herd bailloll comen take lade scotland came haste kyg horne x thousand scottes distrouble shold nat come londe sir edward bailloll companye discofyted disco fiture sir alizaudre feto quelled many othir erle fiffe tho sory ful ylle shamed littell companye discomfyted shamefully put hy copanye lyve flee tho came sir edward bailloll toke contre aboute hym tyll came vnto ye abbey du sermelyne fownde vytailles hym hys folke amonge othir thyges fonde chaubre aboute v honderd grete staues fyne oke longe pykes yren stelle toke delyured ye strengest men panie anone wet fro thes loged hym felde ij myle seint iohanes towne ye burgeys toun herd erle fiffe disco fyted thurgh ye bailloll sore adrad brak brygges made ouer water erne bailloll might gon ouer wherfor logged hy night littell hede tok rest said vnto peple nowe fayre lordes ye knowe full well ben nowe logged bitwen enemy yf mowe v hampre ther bote deth wherfor yf abyde nyght styll thy ke shall turne v moche sorwe harme power scottes may euery day wex ad encresse may bene littell peple ayens hem wherfore pray loue almyghty god make v bolde hardy may myghtely take scottes nyght boldely werre vpon hem ad let v purswe hem night trauailled thurgh v ad see hardynesse othir scottes comen mete hem see hem trauailled wery sorer wull thei drad v fyght ad fersly shull fyght wyt vpon hem purswe thurgh grace god almighty world shall speke ye doughtynesse cheualrye syres vnderstodeth wel copanye come wyth sir erward bailloll graunted well vnto couceil therof glad anone purswed vpo scottes becomen woder wery bailloll copanye sore folowed hem dyd moch sorwe thurgh hir assaulte yt might feble hem helpe ad littell peple tho said ye scottes amonges hem befall littell peple bailloll hath wynge v moch trauaille sorwe certes semeth v wreccheth grace woder g cyous quarell certes shul ben dede er may come hym v yelde sith fadre sette v pry amonge othir thinges ye bailloll passed watyr erne sir rogier swynerton sone fers angrj wente forth sawe peple armes full well arayed forth wente vnto hem wyth hem fowghten quelled many wold abyde toke notheles assaulte baillols men wende bene moost grete hooste skotlande whan came morne gadred gedre rrsted hem whyle whyle englysshmen rested hem noble baron thomas wesy also ye noble gentyll baron stafford pryked hyr horse vp doune hylles kepe estres contre pryked vp downe saw grete hoost good aray ordeyned thre wynges helmes sheldes shynyng comyng vpon hem two sayd lordes sawe came ayene vnto baillols folk wt grete hast sayd nowe loue god almyghty ben good co fort ye shall haue bataill anone ryght tho spake sir fouke sone gareyne worthy baron grete renomme dede armes syres lordynges vnderstondeth well wull saye vnto yow haue seyn many dyuerse wynges well amo ge sarazen jewes amonge scottes yet saw neuer tyme ferthe part wynge fyght therfore yf wyll abyde ennemyes ben ynowe fight ayens yf good hert good wille fight wyt hem certes bene full fewe ayens companye ther loue god take vnto v good herte let v ben bold thenke nether oure wyfes ne child co quere hem bataille ad thurgh helpe lord god enemyes shull ouercome wyt came hoste scottes toward hem full fersly ayes sir edward bailloll iij batailles well araied armure ad woder fersly camen toward baillolls men sir donald erle marchille sawe said robert brus ye sone robert ye brus wordes syr robert quod full sore fortinketh myne hert yt thees folke bailloll hath brought shold deye wyt dynt scottessh swerd syth ben crysten men well ben therfore thyketh grete charite send vnto hem yelde hem vnto mercy grace rausone thurgh grevous raunsone asmoch haue take lad done ylle nowe certes quod sir robert brus haue well perceyued thou art ennemye traitour vnto scotlad syth thow wilt consente saue dedely enemyes haue v moche sorwe shame nowe semeth wel ye ben hyr asset certes robert quod sir donald falsely ye lye j hir companye ne hir cosent hastely ye shul see fyght hem rather companye certes sir robert said j shal maugre thin heed assaille er thow prykede hyr stedes fersly vpon caskemore wynges hem folewed reche tho came ad mete bailloll companye hongyng bought streit passage fast thei hasted hem vnto englysshmen thousendes fell ye grou de one vp yt othir hepe bothe hors ad man bailloll tho men mygthely stode ayens hem fast quelled scottes vnto grounde many sore wounded longe tyll yt stoden vpon hem foyned hem hyr swerdes ad speres thurgh body ad sore trauaylled vpon hem till becamen full wery wist nat done scottes left lyve fledde away saue hi selfe best maner might tho purswed sir edward bailloll men quelled tyll nyght fro then went vnto seint iohannes towne toke helde hem vitailled selfe hir owne wyll fo den ynowe wherwith make mery tho made bailloll hys men wounded gon shipp wende englond hele hyr wowndes tyme ther flemmyng see stronge thefe robber called crabe flemmyg driuen flau dres wykkednesse ad therfore came scotland holde scottes moch harme vnto englysshmen might crabbe met ye see ye baillols men wou ded bataille sent ayen englod hele hyr wou de crabbe yafe vnto hem grete assaute wold haue quelled euerichon englisshmen defended hem wel manly discomfyted crabbe co panye tho begonne flee scotland came toward seint iohannes towne punctel fonde grete companie scottes come ayene geddre discomfyture gaskemore besieged baillol hys men toune seyt johan anone tolde scottes discomfyted englysshmen wou ded gaskemore went toward englod hele wo de said scottes shold haue might ne grace ayens edward bailloll enche scofyted empeired ye cheualrye scotlad honde full men accompte ayens scottes slayne wherfor couceilled remeue siege seynt ioha ne towne kepe hem best maner cowde myght scottes vnderstode crabbe said soth forsoke liege went then night ad halpe hem selfe best maner might thi ge knowen thurgh scotland lordes ad knightes scomfyted gaskemore scotlad thurgh sir edward bailloil ye shul vnderstode ye lordes lady getyls scotlad came woder fast seint joha ne town yelde ye baillol hy dyden homage feaute hir lades yelde pee receyued frely fro thes went abbey scone crownyd kyng ye scotlad came thyder dyd hy feaute homage reaume scotland maner kig edward englod gadred ayen homage feautes scotlad wherof put oute thurgh couceyll assente dame isabell modre ad sir rogier mortimer erle marche tho toke bailloll kyng scotland leue kyng edward englod went thes owne lande scotlad sette littel hem couceylled hi holpen hym hys quarell wherfore went fro lyued hyr londes ad rente scotlad befell longe king scotland ne remeued came toune anaude toke dwellyng thyder came hy companye knightes stronge men worthy yelde vnto kyng bere hem faire dede continauce trust moch hem anon traytours sawe trust moch vpon hem ordeyned amonges hem fyfty companie ad wold haue quelled hir kig thurgh grace almighty god brake thurgh wall hole chabre god wold ascaped trecherie alle men quelled escapyd wt moch drede vnto ye towne cardoill ther helde sore annoyed befell ladyes eue conceptyo tho sent kyg edward bailloll kyng edward englond falsely traitoursly littell tyme put shame sorwe thurgh hys liegmen vpon trusted wonder moch ad prayed loue god yt wold maynten hym helpe hy ayens ennemyes kyng englond tho grete pyte behight helpe socour ad sente worde shold holde hy pee stille ye forsaid cite cardoylle till gadred power tho ordeyned kyng edward englond cou ceill london let gadre dyuerse shire englod redy wete toward towne berewyke vp twede thyder came kyg edward baillol scotland power besieged towne made withowte towne fayre towne pauillons dyked aboute drede scottes made many assaute gonne engynes toune wherwith destroyed many fayre howses chyrches also bete downe vnto erthe grete stone spitousely came oute gonne ad othir engynes notheles scottes kepte well towne two kyges might come therin loge time notheles kyges abyde ther longe till thay town failled vitailles ad also wery wakyng wisten nat ye shul vndyrsto de scottes ye towne berewyke thurgh commune couceill hir assente let crye vpon walles toun might haue pee englysshmen therof prai den king grace mercy praied hy trewes viij day vpon thys couenaunt yf rescued side ye town toward scotlad scottes withi viij dayes thei wold yelde hem vnto kyg ad town also holde thys couenaut profred kyng xij hostage towne berewyke whe hostage delyured vnto king anone town sent vnto ye scottes told hem hyr sorwe ad meschief scottes camen tho preueli ouer ye watyr twede bought abbey ad sir willia dyket tho stiward skotland many othir camen put grete peryll tyme hir lyfe thei came ouer brigge broke ye stone way many hir copanie drenched ye forsaid wyllia went ouer othir copanye came shippes englond town englodes side ye couenaut bitwen towne shold reskued ye halfe scotland anon kyg edward tho comauded yelde town wolde hange ye hostage scottes said ye towne reskued ynowe ther wold holde wha kyng alixaudres fadre keper towne co mauded euery day ij hostage towne shulde hanged tyll done vnto deth yf wolde yelde towne shold teche hem breke hys couenauntes wha ye towne herde thees tydinges became englysh minystrelles blewe tru pe pypes ad hydously ascryed scottes tho euery englyssh bataille two wy ge pry archiers whyche batalll shoten arewes fast sore scottes myght nat helpe hem selfe shoten xv baron lxxx knightes shippes barge take vnto nobre cc xxx yere kyng makyng abydyng vpon siege turney erle henaude wyt englissh archiers made assaute ye town seint amed slowe l knightes many othir ad also destroied town ye xvj yere regn folowyng wynter tyme kyg dwelled still vpon forsaid siege ad sent ofte englod hys tresorier othir purneiours gold money shold sent hym ther nede procuratours messagiers cursedly full flowly serued hy nede hy deceyued who defaute laches king toke trewes bitwen hym kyg frau ce kyng full wo sorwe ad shame hert drowe fro siege came britaigne ther grete stryfe vitaill lost manj peple whe cam dressed hi ouer see englond ward saylled toward englod ye high see ye moste myshappes stormes tepestes thudring lightnyges fyll hy ye see whiche sayd areised thurgh euyll spirites made bi sorcery nygromacy frau ce wherfor kynges hert full sorwe anguyssh weylyng sighing said vnto lady thys wyse blessyd lady seit marie cause euermore goyng frauce alle thyges wether falle ioyefull lykyng wolde haue allewey turnyng englond ward thinges falle vnprofytable ad harmefull neuyrthelater skapyng alle perilles see god wold came bi night tour londo yere kig held crystmasse meners ad sent word scottes hys messagiers redy wold fight wt hem scottes wold abyde yt fledden ouer scottissh see ad hyd well might xvij yere hys regne abowte feste couersion seint paule kyng edward scotland sawe skottes fledde came ayen englod littel befor lent turnement dunstaple turnement came yonge bachelerie cheualrie englond wyt many erles lordes whych turnement kyng edward selfe preset next yere folowyng xviij yere hys regne hys parlement holden westmynster quynzeme pashe king edward ye thridde made edward hys fyrst begoten sone prynce walys xix yere regne anone aftyr ianiuer foresayd kyng edward let make full noble ioustes grete festes place byrthe wyndesore neuer none seen ther fest ryalte ij kinges two quenes ye prynce walys duke cornewaill x erles ix cowntesses baron many burgeys whych mighten lightely nombred dyuerse landes beyonde see many straugiers ye tyme whan ioustes kyng edward made grete souper ordeyned fyrst began rownde table ordeined stefasted day forsaid rownde table holde wyndesore wytson wyke euermore yerly tyme englysshmen moch han ted cleued wodnesse foly stranger tyme comyng henawdres xviij yere passed ordeyned chawnged hem euery yere diuerse shappes disguysyng clothyng loge large wyde clothes destitut desert fro olde honeste ad good vsage othir time short clothes streite wastyd bagged kyt euery side slatered botened sleues tapites surcotes hodes ouer log ouermoch hagyg sothe shall saye lich tormauntours deueles hir clothyg ad shoyng othir aray tha men woman nyfely yet passed men aray coriouslaker streyt clothed let hange tailles sowed bineth wythin hyr clothes hele hidde hir arses ye disguysinges pryde pa adueture aft er ward brought forth caused many mysshappes meschief reame englod xx yere kyng edward wet ouer ito britaign gascoigne who copanie wet erle warrewyke ye erle southfolk erle hutygton ye erle arudell many othir lordes ad mune peple grete multitude grete nauye cc xj shippes anone aftyr mydsomer auege many wronges harmes hy phelipp valoys king frauce ayest trewes grau ted trewes falsely vntrewly cauellacios losed ad disquate phow king edward sailed normadye arriued hogges grete host ca cc xxvij xxi yere regn kyg edward thurgh cou ceill grete lordes reame englod called ad gadred gedre parlement westmyster estre ordeyned hi passe ouer ye see ayen disese destrouble rebelles frauce nauye come gedre made redy wet wt hugh host ye xij day iuyll sailled normadye arryued hogges wha rested hym vj dayes cause trauaillyng see haue oute men wyt hir necessary oute hyr shippes wet toward cadoun brenyng vastyng destroyng tounes yt fonde way xxvi day iuyll brigge cadony maly orpedli strengthyd defeded wt norma stroge bataille longe thurgh grete multitude peple slayn ther take prysoners ye erle ewe brode xx mile vasted maner thig fode whe phelip valoys ceyued though fast wt stronge hoste wolde come nerre breke alle ye brigges beyode ye watyr seyne fro rone vnto paris wyt ye hast yt might soth noble kyg edward whe came paris brigge fonde broken withy ij dayes let make ayen morwe assumptio lady kyg edward passed ouer ye watyr seyn goyg toward crescy destroyed way tounes wt peple dwellyg theryn fest seyt bartolomewe passed ouer ye water somme vnhurt wt host neuer hand maner way ne passage wher ij slayn letted hir passage ouer therfore ye xxvj day august king edward feeld fast cresey hauyg iij batailles englisshme coutred ad met wt philip valoys hauyng wyt hy iiij batailles whych leest passed gretli nobre englyssh peple whe thees ij hostes mette gedre ther fyll vpo hy king beme duke loreyne erles also flau dres dalunson bloys harecourt anmarle nevers many erles baron lordes knightes punctel men armes ye nobre mvc xlij wtoute footman othyr men wel armed yt nothyng rekened vnvnglorious philippe withdrowe residue peple wherfore sayd comune amog owne peple nostre beal soy retreyt seye fayr withdrawith tha king edward englisshme thanked god almighty victorie hir grete labour taken hem thyng nedefull hir sustynauce sauyng hir lyfe drede hyr enemyes rested hem full erly mornyng frensshme wyt hughe hoost came ayen yeue bataille fyght wyt ye englysshmen mette coutrede erles warrewyke northapto northfolk wyt hir copanye slowen two thousand toke many prysoners gentills hem remanaunt host fledde iij myle thes ye thridde day bataill kyng wete caleys ward destroyng countre rode thyderward wha come yt say thridde day septebre began besege toune wyt castel tinued siege fro ye forsaid thridde day septebre vnto thridde day august next yere ye yere siege caleys kyng skotland wyt full grete multitude scottes came englod nevilles crosse aboute seyt lucas day euagelist hopyg trustyng haue fonde londe destytute voyde peple asmoch kyg englod beyode see saufe prestes men holy chyrch wymen childre plowghme ad othir laborer robbede dyde moch sorwe yet fonde ynow withstode ye grace almighti god day bataill assigned bitwene certay lordes men holy chyrch ye coutre othir comune peple fast cite duresme day thurgh grace almighty god scottes ouercomen yet iij fold many englysshme ther slayn cheualrie knighthode ye reame scotlad take wold haue fledde thes dauid kyng scotlad selfe erle mentife sir willia douglas many grete men aftyr englysshme whan thei rested hem fewe dayes ordeyned kepers northcontre came vnto lo broughten wyt hem dauid king scotlad alle othir lordes take prysoners vnto towr londo ye hast might ther left hem sauf kepyng vnto kinges comyng wenten home aye vnto hyr owne co tre afterward kinges rausone scotlad taxed vnto c mark syluer paied x philp ye kyg frauce cast purposed trechouresly fraude put away siege came ye xxvij day iuyll yere wt grete host stroge power neyg ed vnto siege caleys whiche phelipp last day iuyll sent kyg edward word wold yeve hy pleme bataill iij day next euesog tyme yf durst come fro ye siege abyde whe kig edward herd withoute long tarieng er long avysemet accepted gladly day howre bataill philip assigned ad whe kyg frauce herd next night aftir sette te te fyre remeved wet away then cowardly yt towne castell besieged seyg thei non othir helpe ne socour kyg frauce ne men also hir vitailles withi ne hem spended vasted ad defaute vitailles refresshing eten hors houdes cattes mys kepe hyr throuth loge might wha saw fonde amoge last thing amoge hem ete ne lyue punctel ne socour ne rescuynge fresshme othir side wist well yt must nedes deye defaulte elles yelde toune anone wenten token downe baners ad armes frauce euery syde honged owte wenten walles towne diuerse place naked borne saue onely shyrtes breches helden hir swerdes naked poynt donward hyr hondes putte roppes balters aboute hir nekkes yelde vp keyes towne castell kyng edward englod wyt grete fere drede hert kyng edward saw mercyable king lord receyued alle thay grace fewe gretest personers state gouernauce towne sent englod ther abyde hir rau sone kynges grace suffred cominalte toune go whidder wolde pee withoute harme let hem bere wyt hem hyr thy ge might bere carie away kepyng towne ye castell selfe tha thurgh mediacion cardinal set fro pope trews take ther bitwene frauce englod ix monthes tha next folewyg aboute mychelmasse king edward came ayen englond glorious victorie xxiiij yere regne eest party world ther arose began pestylence ad deth sarazen paynyms grete deth neuer herde afore ad wasted away peple vnethes tenth persone left lyue yere southcoutrees also west coutres ther fyll moch rayne ad grete watres crystmasse vnto midsomer ther vnethes day ne night punctel rayned somwhat thurgh whych watres pestilence enfected abundaut coutrees namely aboute court rome place bi see costes vnethes ther left lyuyg folke bery hem dede honestly maden grete dyches pittes wonder brode depe theryn buried hem maden renge dede bodyes casten littel erthe hele hem aboue caste othir ge dede bodyes ad ge erthe aboue hem thus buried none othyr wyse ye fewer grete men estate buried honestely might xxiiij yere kig edwardes regne hy wyte vnderstode treso begone caleys ordeyned seell ye towne grete somme flory vnto kig phelipp frauce thurgh ye falsenesse ordinauce knyght yt kalled sir geffrey cha ney woder pryue wt kig philip frauce whe kyg edward herde toke wt hy noble gentils lordes many worthy orped men armes psent wyt hy solepnite hyghe fest well wysely hast might ad also preuely might wet ouer see yere good kyg edward helde cristmasse haueryg morwe neweyeres day kyg castell caleys wt men armes none alien wyst therof fals spi atour traitour geffrey charney sawe might openly haue hys purpose castell preuely ad stelyngly came helde toune grete hoste wyt men comen payed forsaid flory couenaut bitwen hem genevey towne keper castell cosentyng geffrey falsenesse trecherie boude eglyssh ministres seruauntes castell myght helpe selfe ne let hem hyr purpose tha wenyg sure ynow thei spake hir wykkednesse falsenesse opynli hyghe yt men might nowe shull ye howe disceyued came pryue posterne ouer lyttell brygge tree comen yn softely pryuely ye brygge drawen vp kept non hem came yn myght gon oute ne mo come vnto ad anon englysshmen wenten oute pryue hole wydowes ouer walles towne castell wente foughten manly frensshmen withoute ad better hem occupyed hem selfe hyr side king withy toune hauyg hym scarcely xxx armes drewe owte swerd lowde voys cryed hygh seynt edward seynt george whe folke herde camen rennyg vnto hi ad yauen ther hyr enemyes grete assaulte ther mo two houdred men armes many othir slayne many fledden away grace god almighty ye victorie fyll englysshme tha kyg toke wt hy geffrey fynder trecherie also many othir frenssh prisoner ad withy came aye englond yere yere fore also ye yere next grete pestilauce men fro eest west namely thurgh boche tho yt siked day deyed thridde day deyde pestilece hadden littell respite lyggyng pope clementz goodnesse grace yafe ful remissyo foryevenesse synnes shriven pestilece lasted londo fro michel masse vnto august next folowyg thakeruille bursydand stiward frauce many othir men contre comune assente lord charlys tho regent frau ce hasted hem went kyg englod assekyg besechyg stedfast pese euer lastyg vpon certeyn codicions shewed writen kyng seen plesed hy neuer dele sythen wolde non othir tyme bettyr accorded deliberacion fresshmen besyly ad grete instau ce asked trewes costes ad kyng grauted morwe vtas pa ye king turned hy hoste toward orliaunce destroieng wastyg contre wey wente thyderward ther fyll vpon hem storme tempest none nacyon herd ne sawe neuer none suche thurgh thowsades men ad hir horse iourneyeng thurgh geauce sodenly slayne perisshed whych tempestes full moch yet fered kyng ne moche hys peple ne wenten forth hyr vyage begonne wherfor aboute fest holy rood day may fast incarnacyon forsayd lordes frauce methyng wyth kyng englod pesible accord fynall vpon certeyne condycyos grautes articulerly gadred ad wryten gedre euermore last ful discretly made bothe kynges profytable ad reames one stable hem hir heyres euer then forth thy ge article whan kyng edward seyne hem grauted hem bothe party sholde sworne godes bodi holy euangelys forsayd couenaut sholde stablisshed accorded graciously knewe wiste wel kyng ynow sauyg hym reame yf reame well truwely gouerned longe euyll gouernyd euell offyciers reame myght nether plenteuous chaffare marchaudise ne rychesse thynges profred hem self ye kyg wold certeynly preue stod fonde preued kyng nede wolde gladly euery men aftyr power ad state hy helpe lene thys ther publysshed shewed ye parlement many pleyntes defautes diuerse offyciers reame namely lord latimer kynges chamburleyne bothe kyng eke reame also last ther spoke treted dame alice peres grete wronges euyll gouernaunce done hyr couceill reame dame alyce peres kyg holde longe tyme hys lemmen wherfor lesse wonder though thurgh ye freelte womanys excityg steryg consented hyr lewdnesse ad euell couceill ye dame alice also ye lord latymer othir stered ye kyng euell gouernauce ayes ye kyg wolde nat gouerned yt tyme hys lordes yt ther ye lemet toke made sone duke lancastre gouernour ye reaum stode still gouernour till ye tyme yt deyde yere anon cadelmasse ye lemet ye kig asked ye xvij yere kig richardes regne deide ye good gracious quen anne yt wyfe kyg rychard ye maner sheu shire furre vpo witsoday tha brought lodo westmystre beryed worthely entered beside seint edwardes shryne who sowle god haue mercy ame phow kig richard spoused dame isabel kyges doughter frauce ye toune caleys brought hir englod let hir crouned quen ye abbey seint peter westmystre ca ccxlij ye xx yere kig richardes regne wete hi ouer see vnto caleys wt duke erles lordes baros many othir worthi squiers wt grete araye mune peple reame good araye appertyned worthi kig price nobley sone hy reuerece obseruauce ouzt vnto hir liege lord mighty kyg emour owene abyde ad receyue worthy gracyous lady shold ben hys wyfe yonge creature xix yere age dame isabell kyges doughter frau ce many othir worthy lordes grete name bothe baron knyghtes wyt moch othir peple camen vnto towne grauenyng ij duke frauce one duke burgoigne duke barry yt wold ferther lasse tha thei plegges tha kyng rychard delyured two plegges hem go sauf ad come sauf two worthy vncles duke gloucestre duke yorke two wente ouer ye watyr grauenyg abyde ther plegges vnto ye tyme mariage feste thees ij duke frauce come ayen vnto greuenyg watyr thees two worty duke came ouer water grauenyg caleys wt hys wurshipfull lady dame isabell yt kiges doughter frau ce ad hir came many worthi lord ladi knightes squyers best araye might metten meyne caleys ye whych welcomed hyr hir meyne best honour reuerece might ad brought towne caleys receyued wyt solepnyte ad wurship might done vnto suche lady brought hyr vnto kyng kyng toke hyr welcomed hyr ad hir fayre meyne made solempnyte myght done king couceill asked ye fressh lordes whethyr couenautes forewardes wyt compassyon ordeyned made bothe party shold trewly kepte holde bytwene hem said ye ad sworne toke hir charge vpon boke made hyr othe well trewely hold maner pointes couenauts withowte contrdaictyo delaye maner wyse punctel brought vnto seint nycholas chyrche caleys worthely wedded wt moste solepnyte kyng quen myght erchebisshop bisshoppes mynystres holy chyrch brought home vnto castell set mete serued maner delicasie ryall metys drinkes plenteuoisely maner stragiers othir creature warned yt feste welcome grete halle tentes sette vpon grene withowte castell receyue maner peple euery offyce redy serue thus worthy mariage solempnely done endeth ryalte two duke fraunce wyth hir peple token hyr leue kyng quene wenten ayen grauenyng water frenssh lordes seye two duke hyr mesone comen ouer ye watyr greuenyng metten euery toke leue othyr departed owr lordes camen ayen caleys frenssh lordes wente ouer watyr home fraunce ayene anon aftyr kyng made hym redy quene hys lordes ladyes hir peple hem camen ouer see englond lo mayre shereues wyth alderman worthy commune rydde ayens hem vnto blake heth ket metten wyth ye king quen ad welcomed hem good aray euery man clothyng crafte mynystrelles fore hem ad brought hem vnto seit george barre sowthwerke toke hyr leue punctel kyng quene rydden kenygton peple lo turned home ayen turnyng ayene lodo brygge somoch presse peple bothe hors ad foot dede brygge xj persones men wome chyldre who sowles almyghty god haue pyte mercy amen aftyrward quene browght vnto towre londo nyght morwe brought thurgh cyre lodo ouer forth vnto westmy stre crowned quene englond brought ayene kyges paleys holde open ryalle fest hyr coronacyo maner peple thyder came sonday next aftyr feste seynt clement xx yere kyg rychardes regne pand tha xxv day august next euell excitacion fals couceill grete wrath malyce kyg olde time vnto hys vncle ye good duke gloucestre erle arundell erle warrewyke anon kyng euell excytacyon euyll counceyll malyce late euenyg day aboue sayd made hym redy strength rode essex vnto toune chelmesford came place sodenly good sir thomas wodestoke ge till duke glowcestre lay place thane good duke came welcome kyg anon kyng arested good duke selfe hys owne body lad downe ye watyr anon put shyp anon lad vnto caleys ad browght capyteynes warde kept holde kynges comaudemet englond tyme ye erle marchall capyteyne caleys anone aftyr commaudemet kig fals couceill commaunded capitey put hy dethe ad anon certeyne yomen te good duke kepyng toke hyr counceyl wold put hym vnto deth ad hir appoytemet shold come vpo hy wha hys bedde ad slepe fethyr bedde ad anon bou de hym foot ad honde ad charged hym lye styll ad thus toke two smale towailles made hi two rid knottes cast towailles aboute duke nekke ad tha toke fethir bedde lay vndyr hym cast aboue tha drowen hyr towailles eche weyes lay vpon fether bed vpo hym vnto tyme dede cause shold make noyse ad th stregled worthy duke vnto deth who sowle god hys hygh pyte haue mercy amen whan kyng arested worthy duke hys vncle sent hym caleys came ayen londo hast wyt wonder grete peple sone come sent erle arudell good erle warrewyk anon came arestyd hym self sir ioha cobha sir ioha cheyne knyghtes arested hym selfe ye maner tyll made parlemet anon put hold ye erle arudell went large vnto parlemet tyme foude sufrysant surete abyde lauwe aswere maner poytes kyng hys conceyll wold put vpo hy xxi yere kyg rychardes regne ordeyned parlemet westmynster whyche kalled grete parlement thys parlement made iugge thys iij worthy lordes othir mo list tyme iuggemet kyng let make hast longe large hows tymbre kalled halle couered wyt tyles ouer ad ope aboute bothe side endes maner might see thurghout ad dome holden vpon forsayd lordes ad iuggement yafe thys forsayd parlement come vnto thys parlement kyng sente hys wryttes vnto euery lord baron knyght squyer euery shire throughoute englond euery lord gadre brynge hys retenue hym short tyme best araye might gete mayntenyng strenghtyg king ayens ennemyes ha come paine dethe king hy selue sent cheshire vnto cheuitais contre gadred brought grete hugh multitude peple bothe knightes squyers principally yome chestreshire yome archiers kyg toke hys owne court yafe hem bouge court good wage kepers owne body night day aboue othir sone loued bed trust whiche sone afterward turned ye kyg grete losse shame hynderyg hys vttyr vndoyng destruction ye shall sone aftyr yt tyme came sir hery erle derby grete meyne men armes archiers erle ruttelad came stroge power peple bothe men armes archiers ye erle kent browght grete power men armes archiers erle marchall came sam maner lord spencer ye maner erle northuberland sir hery percy sone sir thomas percy hys brother worthy lordes broughte fayre meyne stronge power eche man best aray duke lacastre te duke yorke camen maner wyth men armes archiers folowyng kyng sir wylliam strope tresorer englond came maner thus thys aray came worthy men thys land vnto king peple came londo one day somoche euery strete lane subarbes full hem logged x xij myle aboute londo euery wey thees peple brought kyng westmynstre wenten home ayen hyr loggynyng bothe hors man moday xvij day septebre lement bega westmynstre kalled grete lemet fryday nex erle aru dell brought parlemest amog lordes seynt mathews day apostell ad euangelist hewes iugget vnto deth halle made ye paleys westmynstre iugement shold gon foot wyth hys hondes bownde behynde hym place iuged ad forth throughout ye cyte lodo vnto ye toure hille ther hede smyten dede place vi ye grete lordes sate hys iuggement ridde wyt vnto place ther vnto deth see execucion done came lodo thus passed forth thurgh cyte vnto hys deth ad ther toke full pacientely who sowle god haue mercy pand came freres austyns toke vp body hede good erle ad bare home vnto hir hous buried hy yorke shire rauenesporte faste wydelyngto ad came ad entred londe ad two lordes wt hir meyne tha moch peple reame herd hys comyng ad knowen wher anon thei drewe vnto welcomed lordes ad coraged alle willya scrope erle wildeshire tresorer englod wt sir iohan bussh sir henry grene iohan bagot skaped hem wet ouer see irland iij knyghtes taken hyr hedes smyte thus deyed hir fals couetyse tha kyng hoged hys hede smyten fals treson shrowesbury ad hede brought london sette londo brygge othir peple ther slayn bothe party kig let burye ther slaine kinges side bataill erle stafford ad sir walter thoas sone wente ouer see ad erle kent many othir lordes knightes wyt men armes archiers grete nobre chastyze rebelles forne moch harm oure englysshme marchauts many townes porte englod ye see costes lorde thomas kynges sone came flaudres fore towne kalled skluse amonges shippes dyuerse nacyos ther rydde wyt hyr shippes amenge hem wente londe sported hem ij dayes camen ayene hyr shippes token brode see metten wyth iij carikkes iene lade dyuerse marchaudyse well manned ad ther foughte gedre longe tyme englysshmen ye victorye broughten carrykkes cabre wy chelsee canted thees goodes ad one carrikkes sodenly brent lordes hyr peple turned hom ayen went ferther yt time tyme serle yoman kyng rychard robbes came englond oute scotland told dyuerse peple kyg rychard lyue scotland moch peple beleued hys wordes wherfor grete parte peple reame grete errour ad gru chyng ayes kyng thurgh informacion lie ad fals lesing serle made moch peple trusted beleued seyng last take north cotre lawe iugged ben drawe thurgh euery cyte good burgh townes englod serued ad last brought london vnto gildhalle iustyce iuged brought ye toure londo tyborne ad honged punctel quartred hys hede smyten sette lo brygge hys quartres sente foure good tounes englod punctel sette vp ad thus endeth fals treson ad disceyt pand vj yere king rye regne ye iiij erle marre scotlad saufconduyt came englod chalege sir grete coquerour ad ye fyrst yere regne grete loue goodnesse sente freres lagely hys fadre e burye kyg richard secod let take body oute erthe ayen dyd bring westmyster ryall chare couered wyth blak anne hys wyfe hys owne desire ferther side seit edwardes shryne ye abbey seint peter westmynster who sowle god haue mercy ame yere certayne lollardes take fals heretikes purposed thurgh fals treson haue slayne kyng haue destroied clergye ye reame yf myght haue hir fals purpose lord god wold suffre hast kyg waryg therof hir fals ordinauce came sodely wyt power seint iohanes wtoute smythfeld anone goodnesse hyr good couceill good wyll shewe touchyg title right yt normadie gascoygne guihene kyg frauce wyt helde wrogfulli vnryghtfully au cestres hy trewe tytle coqueste right herytage ye whych normadie gascoign guyhene good kyg edward wydesore aucestres hy hadde hold hir life time hys lordes yafe hy couceyll send ebassatours vnto kyg frauce couceill shold yeue vnto hy ryght herytage saye normadye gascoygne gwyhene whiche predecessours hadde hold fore elles wold wy ne dynt swerd short tyme wyth helpe almyghty god dolphyne frauce answered embassatours said maner kyng ouer yong tendre age make werre ayens hym lyke good werriour make conquest thervpon somwhat scorne despyte sent tonne full tenys balles sholde haue playe wyth hy lordes became hy better tha maynten werre anon lordes embassatours toke leue came englod ayene ad told kyg couceil ye vngoodly answere dolphyne presente ye sente vnto king whe king herde hir wordes answere dolphyn wonder sore agreued right euell payed toward ye fresshmen toward kyg ad dolphyn thought auenge vpon hem sone god wold send grace myght ad anon let make tenys balles ye dolphy ye hast yt might made grete gone stone dolphyne play wt anon ordenauce went hi forth hareflete besieged towne aboute lond eke bi watyr sent capiteyne towne charged delyuer towne capyteyne sayd none delyured none wold yelde hym bad hy best tha kyng laid ordynauce vnto ye towne saye go ne engynes trypgetes shete cast walles eke vnto toune kast downe bothe toures toune layd vnto grownde ad played tenys harde go ne stone withyn towne shold playe songe wel away ad allas euer tenys balles made cursed werre bega tyme euer borne morwe kyng dyd crye euery gate towne euery man shold redy morwe erly make assaute vnto ye towne willyam bouchier iohan graut xij othir worthy burgeys came kyng ad besought ryall pryncehode power withdrawe hys malyce destructyon vnto hem besought hi viij dayes respyte trewes yf reskue myght come vnto elles yelde vp towne vnto hir goodes tha kyng sente capyteyne kept remenaut still wyt hym lord gaucorte capiteyne ye towne wete forth rone hast vnto dolphyne helpe socour non ne man reskue ye dolphy wold abyde thus capiteyne came ayene vnto kyng ad yolde vp towne delyuered keyes kalled hys vncle erle dorset made hy capiteyne town harflete delyuered keyes bad hym gone put oute frenssh peple bothe men woman child
